Chapter 1190: The Sacred Master Transmitted the Dao

The Sacred Master Transmits the True Way

While Li Ping was conversing with Yin Shangren, the black-haired youth who had intuitively discovered a path to the Primal Chaos Golden Core had his life signs rapidly weaken. Ultimately, he completely lost all signs of life.

But he did not die.

The black-haired youth still sat there quietly, his internal vital energy and spiritual energy circulating spontaneously.

Vast and mysterious.

“Alas, he couldn’t hold on. He has completely assimilated with the grotto-heaven’s consciousness and lost himself,” Yin Shangren sighed deeply, his face filled with regret.

“His original strength was too weak, and his target choice was also inappropriate. If he had chosen a smaller grotto-heaven next to it, he might have been able to survive.”

Li Ping’s gaze also lingered on the black-haired youth, unable to look away for a long time.

“What is his name?”

“Qu Wentian.”

“A good name. However, I still have one matter I don’t understand,” Li Ping’s voice echoed in the vast, empty secret chamber. “Can a Foundation Establishment cultivator truly seize the creation of a grotto-heaven? That vanished grotto-heaven was named ‘Abyssal Chaos.’ Although it didn’t appear large from Great Qi’s perspective, the scale of Abyssal Chaos was equivalent to almost half of Great Qi’s minor world…”

“Perhaps this child has extraordinary talent,” Yin Shangren replied after a long period of silence, unable to come up with a satisfactory explanation.

“You must understand that people are different. Some things that seem impossible to us can be done with ease by others. The path to Primal Chaos Golden Core that Qu Wentian pioneered, although destined to be tread by only a select few, has nonetheless given me inspiration.”

Yin Shangren looked at Li Ping, his expression turning solemn. “You are right. To completely dismantle the dominance of the Heavenly Venerate Transmission method, our new cultivation method must not be a path for the few and the difficult.”

“The cultivation path of the Heavenly Venerate Transmission method spread like wildfire back then, instantly covering the entire Xuanhuang Realm, and despite the suppression of the Ten Sects, it persisted and eventually replaced them. Was that not because it had almost no threshold? Universally accessible cultivation is the true characteristic of our new method.”

“I have been contemplating: Qu Wentian broke through his realm based on ‘Establishing Foundation with Me’ by seizing the creation of the world. Conversely, the world’s creation should be the most crucial element of the ‘Primal Chaos Golden Core.’”

Yin Shangren’s speech quickened, and his expression grew somewhat excited.

“Without external reliance, accessible to all, the creation of the world…”

“Integrating these three necessary conditions allows us to glimpse the true ideal image of the Primal Chaos Golden Core!”

Yin Shangren waved his hand, and illusory images of childlike faces appeared before the two.

“Seizing the creation of the world is not for the sake of the creation itself, but for the evolution of creation. The creation of the world is profoundly mysterious and difficult for ordinary people to comprehend. Only by forcefully possessing it through ‘devouring’ can it become part of oneself and be slowly understood.”

“But if there were a supremely wise master, meticulously instructing, exhaustively teaching their own understanding of the world’s creation…”

“I believe that even a nascent child could comprehend the Dao!” Yin Shangren stated with certainty.

Seeing Li Ping’s skeptical gaze, he said, “The ‘Establishing Foundation with Me’ method, how complex and inconceivable it appears to outsiders? But to the children I taught, who were exposed to it from childhood and believed it to be the only method of cultivation, it was not that difficult to learn. Especially after the first success of ‘Establishing Foundation with Me,’ it was as if a bottleneck was broken, and successful practitioners appeared one after another.”

“Just as ‘Establishing Foundation with Me’ is, so too is the ‘Primal Chaos Golden Core.’”

“Furthermore, the new cultivation method should be tailored to each individual. Emulating the world’s transformation within oneself to achieve Primal Chaos may not necessarily require pursuing the absolute extreme. After all, worlds vary in size, and cultivators’ innate talent and potential also differ. Fully unleashing one’s own potential is already sufficient…”

“The only requirement is to find such a ‘Supremely Wise Master,’ one who not only possesses unparalleled understanding of the world but can also patiently share their insights without reservation…”

As Yin Shangren spoke, he looked towards the “Destined Sacred Emperor” before him.

“Although I am willing to be a teacher to the world, unfortunately…” Li Ping paused slightly.

“My own understanding of the world’s Dao is insufficient, how can I teach others?”

“I think in the entire Xuanhuang Realm, only Heavenly Venerate Transmission is qualified to be this master, perhaps? Ask Transmission to rebel against himself?”

“Fellow Daoist’s path to the ‘Primal Chaos Golden Core’ still requires careful consideration.”

Yin Shangren could not refute, a flicker of unwillingness and confusion appearing in his eyes.

Li Ping, having come with anticipation but leaving with disappointment,

Left Yin Shangren in place and returned alone.

He consoled the Hundred Flowers Daoist, who had rushed over, thinking the Xuanhuang Realm was under attack by the Myriad Immortals Alliance and was searching for the enemy.

He also rewarded her with some “Golden Origin Force” as a commendation.

As a pure crystallization of cultivation, Golden Origin Force was a great tonic for the Hundred Flowers Daoist, a being of pure energy.

The Hundred Flowers Daoist first expressed her gratitude, then solemnly absorbed it.

“Eh? Fellow Daoist, the one you gave me this time…”

Before she could finish speaking after absorbing the Golden Origin Force, the Hundred Flowers Daoist exclaimed in disbelief.

“Why is it so dense?”

“It’s even like…”

“Essence of Origin Force?!”

The Hundred Flowers Daoist looked at Li Ping with utter shock.

Her Glazed Body, visible to the naked eye, became even more radiant and condensed.

The latent injuries accumulated over many years were slowly repaired. Even the faint link to the Fishing Pool, which had persisted even after escaping its capture, seemed to have become negligible under the wash of Golden Origin Force.

Correspondingly, as the Hundred Flowers Daoist looked at the faceless Sacred Emperor before her, his unfathomably deep figure was slowly imprinted in her heart.

Li Ping offered no explanation, leaving behind only a profoundly mysterious silhouette for the Hundred Flowers Daoist.

“He, has he already approached the True Immortal realm?”

“How is that possible?”

The Hundred Flowers Daoist felt immense shock, yet the power surging within her, far exceeding the ordinary, seemed to be the best evidence for her speculation.

…

As a clone, Li Ping’s cultivation level had naturally not surpassed the main body.

He remained at the Nascent Soul stage, and most of his combat power came from the Great Qi minor world’s destiny. His personal strength was pitifully weak.

The reason he could produce Golden Origin Force nearly approximating Essence of Origin Force was precisely by relying on a group of special individuals.

Deep beneath the Sacred Emperor’s Seat, in the darkest depths.

Unseen by any light, yet here, a group of people lived without being affected.

Daily, besides their regular routines, their most important task was to pray to the Sacred Emperor’s statue.

Chapter 1191: Arranging the False Immortal Net

The Dark Weaving False Immortal Net

The sounds of devout prayer reverberated in the underground chamber.

Like ancient hymns, long and mysterious.

This group of people were, naturally, the You Clan.

Under the combined efforts of Li Ping’s disciples, almost the entire You Clan had been captured within the Great Qi minor world.

Li Ping knew that the being behind the Dark Sea did not mind its believers having other faiths.

So, after coercion, temptation, and finally demonstrating the reality of coexistence before the entire You Clan, these You Clan members soon adapted to this life.

Some even developed a faith in the Destined Sacred Emperor that was firmer and more fervent than their faith in the Dark Sea.

After all, the Dark Sea had shown no divine miracles during their time of existential crisis, while the Destined Sacred Emperor truly delivered large quantities of supplies to the people periodically.

In the darkness, listening to the collective chanting of the You Clan, Li Ping felt specks of Golden Origin Force being generated within him.

“Just a hundred You Clan members, and the faith power they condense is more than all the citizens of Great Qi combined.”

“What secrets are hidden within the You Clan…”

Li Ping had already sent some of the bodies of the resisting You Clan members to Yin Shangren for research.

“It just so happens that his research on the new cultivation method has also hit a bottleneck. Perhaps by changing research topics, there might be unexpected sparks of inspiration.”

Of course, Li Ping was not particularly concerned about the true reason behind the You Clan’s unique physique.

Regardless of its origin, as long as it could be used by him.

His form flickered, and Li Ping arrived at another sealed area near this prayer space.

“Xuan Ba, how is the research progressing? Can the transplanted flesh and blood promote the fertility of the You Clan?”

Wang Xuan Ba, who had been intensely focused on something ahead, withdrew his gaze upon hearing his master’s arrival.

He respectfully bowed and reported, “After several experiments, I have found the optimal combination of exotic beast flesh and blood.”

“I have named it the ‘Life Primordial Embryo.’”

“As long as there are sufficient male and female primordial essences, it can cultivate a large number of younglings at an astonishing speed.”

“But…”

“After all, they are not gestated in a mother’s body. These younglings are born extremely frail, and their expected lifespan might not be long,” Wang Xuan Ba said cautiously.

Unlike the honest and robust young man he used to be, Wang Xuan Ba was now gaunt.

Under Li Ping’s meticulous guidance, and after personally devouring the flesh and blood of numerous exotic beasts and mastering their abilities, his understanding of exotic beasts had even surpassed Li Ping’s.

Upon learning of his master’s concern about the You Clan’s low fertility rate, he volunteered to alleviate his master’s burden.

Thus, he unexpectedly created this rather astonishing “Life Primordial Embryo.”

It was composed entirely of pink, writhing exotic beast flesh and blood, with enclosed chambers inside.

Countless tubes connected these chambers to the primordial embryo’s main body.

While providing sustenance for the gestating younglings, it also allowed the Life Primordial Embryo to absorb the characteristics of the large number of younglings it cultivated.

“This is a win-win process. With each new youngling cultivated, it becomes more intelligent and powerful.”

“Although this progressive process is minuscule, it can be accumulated through quantity to achieve metamorphosis within the expected timeframe.”

“If my prediction is correct, the Life Primordial Embryo might eventually no longer require male and female primordial essences to create life, as long as there is sufficient energy.”

When discussing exotic beasts, even in front of his master, Wang Xuan Ba’s tone was full of confidence.

Li Ping’s gaze pierced the darkness, looking towards the giant “lump of flesh” pulsating in the distance, as if breathing.

“I only need them to serve me in sufficient numbers simultaneously. As for their lifespan…”

“They can be recreated after they die.”

The Sacred Emperor’s words were chilling, and Wang Xuan Ba felt nothing unusual upon hearing them.

After all, in his eyes, these headless You Clan members were no different from those exotic beasts, not truly human.

“You must strictly keep all matters here confidential. Even from your senior brothers and junior brothers,” Li Ping added again.

“Disciple understands,”

Wang Xuan Ba said solemnly.

After Li Ping left, he continued his research.

Compared to the complex affairs outside, he preferred these simple and straightforward matters.

However, with only a few years’ time, the trajectory of the once robust youth from below Mount Jieli had changed dramatically.

Yet, among Li Ping’s disciples, Wang Xuan Ba’s transformation was not the most significant.

Wang Xuan Ba’s actions still bore traces of his former self. In stark contrast, his fifth disciple, Ou Shangtian, had undergone a complete transformation.

Having followed his father to Great Qi and been taken in as a personal disciple by Li Ping, he had transformed from his previous taciturn, wary, and unconfident demeanor into the spirited youth he was today.

His actions were decisive, and he looked down upon all things.

Although he was the youngest among the disciples, in terms of true strength, he surpassed them all.

Within the entire Great Qi, besides Li Ping, there was likely no one who could match him.

Even if Li Ping were to step in, without resorting to secret techniques or divine abilities, subduing Ou Shangtian would not be an easy task.

In addition to Ou Shangtian’s two innate mystical artifacts, the Kun Gan Bone Hand and the Book of Ten Thousand Deaths,

Not long ago, Ou Shangtian had also fished up the Seven-Colored Divine Light from the Fishing Pond under Li Ping’s guidance.

With the protection of the Seven-Colored Divine Light, coupled with the incredible escape abilities of the Kun Gan Bone Hand and the Book of Ten Thousand Deaths, Ou Shangtian’s survivability was even greater than that of most Harmonious Dao cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm.

After a few decisive battles, easily suppressing several minor worlds, this young prodigy had become increasingly arrogant.

However, thanks to his father and Li Ping’s suppression, he had not committed any outrageous acts.

Previously, when he worked with Wang Xuan Ba to capture the You Clan, he had become interested in Wang Xuan Ba’s bizarre exotic beast abilities.

So, he requested the cultivation method of the “Creation Furnace Art” from Li Ping and had been diligently cultivating it recently.

Li Ping was not worried about Ou Shangtian losing control.

The moment he showed signs of losing control, Li Ping would decisively intervene.

The Golden Origin Force condensed by the You Clan had been silently infused into the bodies of key figures in Great Qi.

This power, already infinitely close to True Immortal power, was something these so-called geniuses could not detect.

Only the Hundred Flowers Daoist, an ancient being from the ancient immortal cultivation world, could understand its true nature.

“Since they have fallen into my net, they can only serve me devotedly.”

“After all, every bestowal has its price.”

With the pure Golden Origin Force as his trump card, Li Ping could begin to plan the invasion of the Xuanhuang Realm.

Chapter 1192: The Soul Returns Home After a Thousand Years

A Thousand Years of Soul Returning Home

Despite the Saint Dynasty Great Qi's rapid theoretical advancement in strength, it was not yet comparable to the Myriad Immortals Alliance or the Five Elders Association. Thus, the initial phase of the plan still focused on infiltration and erosion.

During the great upheaval of the Xuanhuang Realm over half a year ago, the Immortal Alliance had lost a considerable number of low-level cultivators. Consequently, rumors were secretly circulating that the Immortal Alliance would implement an expansion of recruitment in the upcoming official entrance examination. Li Ping had already selected a batch of promising candidates, preparing to send them into the Myriad Immortals Alliance during this opportunity.

Low-level cultivators, though seemingly insignificant, could slowly corrupt the internal governance of the Immortal Alliance like termites. Furthermore, as their cultivation and merits grew over time, their positions would rise, and the resulting harm and influence would gradually increase. The cost of investment was extremely low, yet the effect was exceptionally good. The more, the better.

"With the existence of the Golden Origin Force network, not only can they smoothly infiltrate the Immortal Alliance, but they can also be firmly controlled from beginning to end. Information and even material exchanges can be completed without real-world meetings. This method of connection is far more concealed and secure than the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elders Association; they would find it extremely difficult to discover."

In addition to corroding the Myriad Immortals Alliance from within, weakening its potential was also a necessary simultaneous action. "The cultivation elites of the Xuanhuang Realm for the next hundred years must all be brought under control. If they cannot be used for my benefit, they should be eliminated as soon as possible. We can even divert the disaster, framing the assassination plan on the Five Elders Association. I will sit on the mountain and watch the tigers fight…"

While weakening the Myriad Immortals Alliance through various means, Li Ping certainly did not slow down the development of the Saint Dynasty Great Qi. Once the You Clan reached a certain scale and sufficient pure Golden Origin Force was collected, Li Ping would use it to renovate the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation, truly turning the Great Qi minor world into an impregnable fortress hidden in the void.

" I can feel that since the arrival of Yin Shangren, Ou Daozi, and other Xuanhuang luminaries to serve me in the Great Qi minor world, the Saint Dynasty's celestial phenomena, which had previously reached a bottleneck, have now encountered the possibility of further breakthroughs. This is the principle of 'one's loss is another's gain.' I have directly usurped the luck that originally belonged to the Myriad Immortals Alliance. However, it is still not enough to be completely satisfied for advancement. Besides the accumulation of time required to usurp luck from the outside, the intrinsic quality of the Great Qi minor world itself is also a limiting factor. Perhaps it is time to consider upgrading the minor world."

Li Ping's thoughts stirred, and he returned to the Sacred Emperor's Seat. Before long, Sun Erlang, surrounded by an aura of killing intent, appeared before him. The once brave youth had grown into a terrifying god of slaughter within the Saint Dynasty Great Qi. He commanded the Saint Dynasty's imperial army, conquering various realms. Over the years, countless beings from other minor worlds had tragically perished under Sun Erlang's blade.

"Greetings, Master!" Sun Erlang knelt on one knee.

"What is the progress on the construction of the Myriad Realms Grand Formation?" Li Ping asked.

"Eleven have been completed, six are under construction," Sun Erlang replied concisely, simultaneously transmitting the specific information via divine sense.

"For the time being, suspend all conquests. We have expanded too quickly and need to digest our gains properly. Any entity within those minor worlds that harbors any thought of resistance shall be killed without exception. I do not wish for any domestic strife when we officially go to war with the Myriad Immortals Alliance."

The implication in Li Ping's words made Sun Erlang's spirit surge. Even though he knew his Master harbored grand ambitions, this was the first time Li Ping had explicitly expressed his plan to conquer the Myriad Immortals Alliance. This made conquering the minor worlds feel like slicing vegetables, and Sun Erlang, who had felt bored without any pressure, instantly became excited.

Li Ping, of course, saw through Sun Erlang's thoughts. "When you see too many sheep, you start to think the world is full of sheep. Not to mention the Myriad Immortals Alliance, even some hidden minor worlds within the Xuanhuang Realm are beyond the current capabilities of our Saint Dynasty Great Qi," Li Ping said calmly, then pointed at Sun Erlang. "Go to this location. It is the secluded residence of the ancient Taiyan Sect. See if you can persuade them to join our alliance."

"Taiyan Sect…" Sun Erlang's eyes flickered. "Go. There are some peculiarities there; you will understand when you arrive yourself. Do not force anything. My only goal is for you to temper some of your arrogance." Unlike the cultivation strategy for Ou Shangtian, when Sun Erlang's dao path began to deviate slightly, Li Ping chose to actively guide him back. Besides having a deeper emotional bond with Sun Erlang, Li Ping also needed a powerful senior disciple to suppress all other disciples. Therefore, he inevitably had to invest more effort in his cultivation.

"I hope this young man gains something from his journey to the Taiyan Sect," Li Ping thought as he sat on the Sacred Emperor's Seat.

Meanwhile, Sun Erlang followed the Sacred Emperor's instructions and arrived at Yi Xingzhi's tomb. After collecting Yi Xing's remains and the scattered white papers, Sun Erlang headed directly to his destination. "I didn't expect there to be such an ancient cultivator's tomb within Great Qi. I wonder what the purpose of these papers my Master specifically asked me to collect is." On the way, Sun Erlang studied them carefully but could not discover any profound secrets. Suppressing his confusion, he soon arrived at his destination. Taihua Prefecture, Tai Xuan Mountain. "Master said the entrance to the Taiyan Sect is hidden within the mountain?" After searching all around, he found no trace of a spatial passage. Sun Erlang couldn't help but feel troubled. If he used brute force, it wouldn't be impossible to carve a path through the mountain. However, he was here as a diplomat to persuade them to join the Saint Dynasty alliance; being so rash as to destroy their sect's grounds… After some thought, Sun Erlang decided against acting impulsively. He chose a favorable spot on Tai Xuan Mountain, dug a hole, and retrieved the remains of Yi Xing. Just as he was about to prepare for burial… A figure suddenly appeared behind Sun Erlang. "He's here after all!" Sun Erlang thought to himself. However, he feigned a look of great alarm, "Who is it?!" The figure ignored Sun Erlang, merely staring blankly at Yi Xing's remains. As if lost in some memory, the figure remained motionless for a long time. Sun Erlang was not a reckless warrior and naturally did not disturb the figure whose strength appeared unfathomable. He merely waited patiently. "If Big Brother had waited a few more years, perhaps everything would be different." After a long while, the figure sighed and waved his sleeve at Yi Xing. Yi Xing's remains instantly vanished. The figure then turned to look at Sun Erlang. "Young man, why have you come?" Sun Erlang looked at the face before him, which appeared to be around his own age. After a moment of hesitation, he honestly stated his purpose.

Chapter 1193: Sudden Change of Fate

Destiny Suddenly Changes

"Great Qi…" The Taiyan Sect cultivator narrowed his eyes, as if countless streams of light rapidly flashed within them. "Great Xuan?"

"Hmm?" Unsure of what he saw, his tone became one of surprise, and he turned to look at Sun Erlang: "In just a few years, such a major deviation has occurred? What is going on?"

Sun Erlang was completely bewildered, not understanding what the other party was talking about.

"Interesting. Come with me." The Taiyan Sect cultivator examined Sun Erlang again before speaking. With that, his figure instantly became transparent. A silver, illusory path materialized beneath his feet, leading directly into the mountain's interior. Sun Erlang transformed into a beam of light and followed closely.

After they entered the mountain, the silver path vanished. Even the pit Sun Erlang had dug on Tai Xuan Mountain was silently restored.

"My name is Yi Shu. The remains you returned are those of my clan brother." As they walked, the Taiyan Sect disciple said to Sun Erlang, "Back then, the dual calamities of 'Laws Cannot Coexist' and 'Immortal-Mortal Miasma' struck simultaneously. My clan brother made a timely retreat, escaping into a mortal minor world. Although he lost his chance at the immortal path thereafter, he achieved the position of a Mortal Emperor. It can be said that fate played its hand."

"After thousands of years without meeting, to reunite under such circumstances. Although we anticipated this when we parted ways, still…"

"Fate is truly ironic!"

"Simulated illusory scenarios are different from tangible realities!" Yi Shu sighed lightly and fell silent.

"Simulation? Reality?" Sun Erlang keenly seized upon the two keywords in Yi Shu's words. "This Taiyan Sect, in ancient times, was renowned throughout the world for its divination techniques. What he calls simulation and deviation, could it be the future they derive?"

They continued to descend, and when a scene appeared before them again, it was high above the clouds. The azure sky was crystal clear, and below it lay fertile farmlands stretching for thousands of miles. Sun Erlang could distinctly sense the aura of a great number of mortals here.

Yi Shu, however, flew towards the sky ahead. Sun Erlang quickly followed, a slight doubt suddenly arising in his heart. Because after entering this small world, Yi Shu seemed to have undergone some subtle changes. However, Sun Erlang couldn't pinpoint the exact nature of the change for the moment.

"I don't sense any danger, and Master would certainly not harm me…" Sun Erlang suppressed the anomaly in his heart and continued to follow.

Before long, a floating city suddenly appeared in Sun Erlang's previously empty field of vision. The city was enveloped by a transparent crystalline barrier. It was precisely because of this barrier that Sun Erlang had not detected this city in the sky earlier.

"As expected, they have some methods. Such a large city can be completely isolated." Sun Erlang mused inwardly.

Yi Shu finally spoke again, "The Tai Xuan Realm was originally borrowed by our Taiyan Sect. To separate immortals and mortals, and to avoid disturbing the mortals of this realm, we constructed this crystalline barrier."

Sun Erlang was somewhat dismissive of Yi Shu's mention of not disturbing mortals. However, he did not openly object, merely nodding slightly.

They passed through the transparent barrier and formally entered the Taiyan Sect. The moment his feet touched the ground, Sun Erlang suddenly sensed as if countless pairs of eyes were simultaneously looking at him. The aura of many Harmonious Dao cultivators was among them.

Sun Erlang was inwardly alarmed: "The strength of this Taiyan Sect has been preserved too perfectly; they still have so many cultivators? How did they deal with the 'Laws Cannot Coexist' calamity?"

Delving deeper into the floating city, Sun Erlang's feeling of peculiarity intensified. "This place is too quiet. It doesn't resemble a normal, vibrant city at all."

"And also…" Sun Erlang paused his steps. He had finally discovered the source of the anomaly in his heart. The Taiyan Sect cultivators here, much like the Treants in the Spiritual Wood Realm, despite having different faces, all emanated the same aura. It was as if they were countless bodies of the same person!

Sun Erlang, though surprised, remained calm and did not indulge in wild speculation. He directly asked, "Elder Yi, your Taiyan Sect…"

Yi Shu seemed to perceive Sun Erlang's confusion and smiled, "You will know everything after you meet Senior Brother Chen. However, young sir, please rest assured, our Taiyan Sect has always been clear about our debts of gratitude and grievances. You returned the remains of a Taiyan Sect disciple, earning our sect's favor. Although the alliance you speak of may not necessarily come to fruition, your personal safety can absolutely be guaranteed."

Sun Erlang remained noncommittal, swallowing the words he was about to speak.

Following Yi Shu to the center of the floating city, inside a blue transparent crystalline building. It was as if countless visions of himself simultaneously entering appeared. When Sun Erlang emerged from the illusion, a handsome man with waist-length black hair stood before him.

"Senior Brother Chen," Yi Shu cupped his hands. "Yi Xing was also carrying out a sect mission in the Great Xuan minor world. Back then, due to his aptitude, he was always unable to enter the inner sect for cultivation and felt perpetually aggrieved…"

"Now that times have changed, inner sect and outer sect are mere jokes. Let Yi Xing return." Senior Brother Chen, who was Chen Tianhai, whom Li Fan had met before, spoke with a calm tone.

"Thank you, Senior Brother." Yi Shu bowed solemnly and then his form dissolved into blue starlight, vanishing.

Chen Tianhai then turned his gaze to Sun Erlang. His words were shocking: "According to the original trajectory, you, Sun Erlang, after repeatedly seeking immortality at Mount Jieli fruitlessly, became fully resigned. You married and had children. Seven years later, dissatisfied with the excessive demands of the newly appointed prefect, you angrily killed someone. Later, you and your companion Wang Xuan occupied a mountain and became bandits, wreaking havoc in the countryside."

"After causing trouble for over a decade, you were ultimately exterminated by the imperial army. You and Wang Xuan fought to the death, refusing to surrender, and were utterly dismembered."

Sun Erlang raised an eyebrow upon hearing the "destiny" described by the other party.

"But now, everything is different."

"Your future…" Chen Tianhai's figure became ethereal and blue. After a moment, he returned to his normal appearance. "Magnificent! Beyond the variables!"

"The Saint Dynasty Great Qi…" Chen Tianhai's eyes flashed with a peculiar light. "In just a few short years, such a great deviation has occurred…" He muttered, as if discovering something incredibly exciting.

"Do you know the origin of your Master?" Chen Tianhai asked.

Sun Erlang merely looked at Chen Tianhai quietly.

"Yes, it is right that you do not know. Even if you knew, you probably could not reveal it, nor would you be able to speak of it," Chen Tianhai said with a strange smile.

Sun Erlang suddenly felt a sense of discomfort.

"Eh, wait, the cultivation technique you practice…" Chen Tianhai, observing Sun Erlang, suddenly changed the subject, his tone filled with surprise. "Is it the 'Sitting Mountain Art' from the Divine Wood Sect?"

Chapter 1194: Tradition of the Immortal Realm's Yan Tian

The Heavenly Derivation Chronicle of the Immortal Realm

"Could it be that your Master was a disciple of the Divine Wood Sect back then?" Chen Tianhai seemed to have thought of something, his tone filled with surprise.

"The 'Sitting Mountain Art'?" Hearing these three words, Sun Erlang's heart stirred slightly. He also felt a sense of familiarity from the depths of his being.

"No, no," but before Sun Erlang could reply, Chen Tianhai shook his head and denied it himself. "The aura is only somewhat similar."

"Besides, it is said that the 'Sitting Mountain Art' was the cultivation technique of that Divine Wood Sect's Divine Wood, which cultivated by exchanging time for cultivation. It is extremely difficult for ordinary cultivators to practice, and their progress is extremely slow. Young sir, you are only in the late Nascent Soul stage at such a young age, which clearly does not match," Chen Tianhai said with a self-deprecating smile, looking at Sun Erlang with even greater curiosity.

"Junior, I indeed do not practice the 'Sitting Mountain Art,' but rather a profound technique personally passed down by my Master. The reason for my rapid cultivation is largely due to this profound technique," Sun Erlang said solemnly.

"Very well, perhaps I was mistaken then." Chen Tianhai did not argue further and moved past the topic.

"Senior, is the Divine Wood Sect one of the Ten Ancient Immortal Sects?" Although he had clarified the origin of his cultivation technique, Sun Erlang was still somewhat curious about the 'Sitting Mountain Art.' He decided to ask directly.

Sun Erlang found that the Taiyan Sect was very different from the strictly disciplined ancient immortal sects he had imagined. There was almost no distinction between superiors and inferiors. They called him "young sir" affectionately, even though he was a very young outsider. Although he didn't know the reason for such an atmosphere, it was undoubtedly a good thing for Sun Erlang, so he decided to go with the flow.

Chen Tianhai answered all his questions with full knowledge. After inviting Sun Erlang to sit down, he said, "The Divine Wood Sect is even older than our Ten Immortal Sects."

"Their contemporaries were the Desolate God Sect, the Reincarnation Sect, and other ancient immortal sects that have long since perished. Before the immortal path was severed, some of them had already disappeared entirely for various reasons. The Divine Wood Sect is said to be named after an otherworldly divine wood within its sect. This divine wood was reportedly a gift from the Immortal Realm, and after taking root in the Xuanhuang Realm, it displayed all sorts of unimaginable divine abilities. But precisely because of this divine wood, it incurred the displeasure of the 'Eternal Ancient Guardian' [亘古恒垣], ultimately leading to their demise. Truly, fortune and misfortune are unpredictable."

"The meaning of these five words, 'Eternal Ancient Guardian,' is 'existing since ancient times and destined to continue eternally, standing above the river of life, like a wall supporting the sky.' It is an primordial ancient tree that has existed alongside the Xuanhuang Realm since its birth, and it even holds the key to longevity."

"As the saying goes, one mountain cannot accommodate two tigers. The growing power of this otherworldly divine wood was bound to threaten it, leading to the destruction of the Divine Wood Sect…" Chen Tianhai casually recounted ancient anecdotes one after another. Since embarking on his cultivation journey, Sun Erlang had only focused on cultivation and killing. This was the first time he had the good fortune to learn these ancient secrets, and he listened with great interest.

"These sects like the Desolate God Sect and the Divine Wood Sect, just by their names, seem different from other sects," Sun Erlang lamented.

Chen Tianhai chuckled wryly: "Naturally. These are sects born since the creation of the Xuanhuang Realm, and they have intricate connections with the Immortal Realm. When the Immortal Realm existed, their status was naturally unshakeable. However, if the Immortal Realm suffered a great catastrophe and the immortal path was severed, they would also no longer prosper."

Sun Erlang nodded repeatedly upon hearing this.

"Does young sir know the origin of our Taiyan Sect?" Chen Tianhai suddenly changed the subject and asked.

"Junior does not know," Sun Erlang replied honestly.

"Our Taiyan Sect is a direct descendant of True Immortals, having received the 'Nine Scrolls of Heavenly Derivation' from Grand Master Tiandu, allowing us to glimpse all possible changes in the future for a thousand years," Chen Tianhai said proudly. "Unlike that second-rate sect, the Heavenly Mystery Sect, which relies on obscure and profound methods of sensing heavenly mechanisms, we rely on our powerful derivation and calculation abilities to truly simulate the future."

Sun Erlang instantly recalled the word "simulation" he had heard from Yi Shu earlier.

"Young sir, please look!" Chen Tianhai waved his hand, and a blue, azure sphere instantly appeared before Sun Erlang. Sun Erlang looked closely, and within this blue sphere, countless overlapping images seemed to be presented simultaneously. The scenes were of himself and Chen Tianhai conversing here. However, Sun Erlang keenly noticed that in each image, his expression and actions were different in each. There were even scenes where he suddenly attacked here and was easily slain by Chen Tianhai.

"These are all the possible futures we have derived after your arrival. However, during our interaction, I have gained a clearer understanding of your temperament and strength. Therefore, some of these futures are no longer meaningful once they have lost their outcome, even before they have been fully derived."

As Chen Tianhai spoke, about four-fifths of the images in the blue sphere suddenly dimmed. The remaining ones depicted scenes identical to what Sun Erlang was currently experiencing.

Sun Erlang watched this scene, as if he understood something, but upon closer thought, he felt utterly bewildered and unable to grasp it.

Chen Tianhai continued: "In the time it takes us to converse, the number of derivations that align with the future trajectory based on the content of our discussion has continued to decrease. Ultimately, after young sir leaves, our derivation of this matter will conclude and merge with reality. A new derivation will then occur."

The blue sphere completely dimmed. After a moment of silence, it erupted with a dazzling blue light. The sphere vanished, transforming into blue mist that floated before Sun Erlang. The blue mist demonstrated countless possible futures for the entire Xuanhuang Realm.

"Deriving the trajectory of the Xuanhuang Realm's future is fundamentally the same as deriving the trivial matter of meeting you. As long as enough information is grasped and the derivation results are corrected in time, we can simulate a future Xuanhuang Realm. This allows us to see further along the river of time than outsiders."

Chen Tianhai waved his hand, and these blue mists, which had demonstrated various future scenes, retracted into his body. Chen Tianhai, who had originally appeared extraordinary, now transformed into a fantastical being composed entirely of blue crystals. This sight stunned Sun Erlang slightly.

"For over a thousand years, our Taiyan Sect has had no major errors in deriving the Xuanhuang Realm's future trajectory."

"But now…" Chen Tianhai stared directly at Sun Erlang. "It's as if in this room where we are conversing, a mysterious person suddenly appears out of nowhere and slays you before fleeing. This is completely outside of common sense, something that would never happen under normal circumstances…"

"We call this 'Beyond the Variables.'"

Chen Tianhai's blue radiance gradually subsided, and he returned to his normal human appearance.

Chapter 1195: Dao Transformation Returns to Stone Mother

Transforming the Dao into the Stone Mother

A sliver of peculiar light flashed in Chen Tianhai's eyes. "Our Taiyan Sect has been in seclusion for thousands of years, with little interaction with the outside world. Your Master actually knows our location."

"He must know something about us. Even so, he still sent you to contact us…"

"This is because he is certain that we will be interested in this 'Beyond the Variables' of his." Sun Erlang was stunned by this revelation: "Is… is that so?"

However, recalling his Master's mysterious background and seemingly omniscient divine abilities, he instantly felt at ease.

"There are indeed transcendent variables in this world, some of which have profoundly impacted and altered the fate of the Xuanhuang Realm. Although our Nine Scrolls of Heavenly Derivation are said to be able to calculate everything in the world, if an 'Outsider' or a True Immortal from the Immortal Realm descends, such events that transcend the world itself are beyond our capabilities," Chen Tianhai said frankly.

"However, our Taiyan Sect does not reject or fear such variables." His tone was low, with unspoken meanings.

"Outsiders?" Sun Erlang pondered thoughtfully. But then, he suppressed this slight fluctuation in his heart. Regardless of his Master's origin, his current identity was the destined Sacred Emperor of Great Qi, responsible for the rise and fall of countless beings. As his Senior Disciple, he would forever stand firmly in front of his Master.

"So, Senior, have you agreed to our alliance request?" After a brief silence, Sun Erlang asked.

"If there is a chance of victory, why would we refuse?" Chen Tianhai smiled slightly, not answering directly.

"Then, Senior, what is your intention?"

"The derivation simulating such a deviation naturally needs to be corrected. Since the Saint Dynasty Great Qi wishes to form an alliance with us, they of course will not refuse an ally's appraisal, right?" Chen Tianhai said lightly.

"This…" The other party's request was somewhat beyond Sun Erlang's expectations. His Master had not given any instructions on how to handle this matter before he left.

"Erlang, you may make your own decisions regarding all matters. This Taiyan Sect is important…"

"It is also not important." Sun Erlang suddenly recalled his Master's final words before he left: "If you are hesitant even when facing a small Taiyan Sect, how can you contend with the Myriad Immortals Alliance for the Xuanhuang Realm in the future?"

A surge of heroism filled his heart, and Sun Erlang blurted out: "The Saint Dynasty Great Qi has a position vacant and warmly welcomes the Taiyan Sect to join us at any time."

Blue light inexplicably flashed in Chen Tianhai's eyes. He did not respond, seemingly lost in thought.

"Since young sir has said so, then our Taiyan Sect will send an envoy to accompany you to Great Qi to investigate." After a long pause, Chen Tianhai finally spoke.

For some reason, Sun Erlang suddenly felt relieved, as if he had just walked back from the brink of life and death.

"Then, Senior, when shall we depart?"

"No rush. A guest who travels a long distance is precious. Young sir has traveled thousands of miles to be here, which is no easy feat. Our Taiyan Sect has not had a visitor for thousands of years."

"Furthermore, you have returned Yi Xing's remains."

Chen Tianhai pondered for a moment and then asked, "May I ask if young sir is interested in our 'simulation'?"

"Naturally, I am curious."

Chen Tianhai nodded. The ground and decorations around them instantly disappeared. The two figures appeared to be in the void, with a vast azure crystal emitting a soul-stirring light before them.

"This is the 'Dao Transformation Stone Mother.'" Chen Tianhai said in a peculiar tone.

"'Dao Transformation Stone Mother?'" Sun Erlang repeated the four words.

Looking at the mysterious crystal not far away, Sun Erlang was horrified to find that he could not discern the details on the crystal's surface. It seemed infinitely divisible, with countless tiny surfaces extending from every mirror-like facet upon closer inspection. Just by peering at it for a moment, Sun Erlang felt dizzy. He immediately averted his gaze.

"The Dao Transformation Stone Mother is the foundation of our Taiyan Sect. Although Grand Master once imparted the Nine Scrolls of Heavenly Derivation, the methods for comprehending the creation of heaven and earth are truly beyond the reach of ordinary people. Even those with peerless talent would exhaust their life force and be on the verge of death if they wished to cultivate the Nine Scrolls of Heavenly Derivation to completion," Chen Tianhai flashed beside the enormous azure crystal.

His figure seemed to merge with the Dao Transformation Stone Mother.

"Even if geniuses cultivate with such difficulty, how much more so for ordinary people? The characteristics of the Nine Scrolls of Heavenly Derivation predetermine that our Taiyan Sect can only have a handful of disciples in each generation. With a dwindling talent pool, the sect cannot grow. Perhaps one day, we will even be unable to preserve the name of the Ten Immortal Sects."

"This was the predicted fate of our Taiyan Sect, according to the derivations."

"If not for the Dao Transformation Stone Mother." Chen Tianhai's tone suddenly changed.

"Even a small fragment of the Stone Mother could instantly grant a mortal the divination and calculation abilities comparable to a Harmonious Dao expert. What a magnificent creation!"

"Young sir, did you bring those white papers that Yi Xing had with him when he died?" Chen Tianhai suddenly asked Sun Erlang, looking at him.

Sun Erlang then suddenly remembered and quickly took out the white papers.

"These white papers are called 'Calamity Reversal Treasure Boxes,' and they were commonly used by Taiyan Sect disciples in the past to practice their divination and calculation abilities."

"There are forty-nine thousand nine hundred and ninety-nine sheets. As long as they are restored to their original sequence, the treasure box can be reformed."

"Would young sir like to try?" Chen Tianhai scattered the white papers into the air, letting them drift randomly. Then, looking at Sun Erlang, he asked with a smile.

"Restore them in sequence?" Sun Erlang had studied the white papers before; they were all identical, with no special markings.

"Is it all luck, with no special secret methods?" Sun Erlang asked tentatively.

Looking at Chen Tianhai's expression, Sun Erlang calculated slightly in his mind and his face immediately turned somewhat pale. He decisively refused.

"That's right. For ordinary people, this is a task that cannot be completed even if they exhaust their lives. But for disciples of the Taiyan Sect who possess the Dao Transformation Stone…"

"In just a moment!" Chen Tianhai lightly pointed a finger, and the papers scattered throughout the sky began to fly wildly. One by one, they arranged themselves in sequence.

Finally, all the papers returned to their positions, and after a dazzling burst of light, the treasure box was opened. Inside was a jade slip and a blue, crystalline stone.

The appearance of the Dao Transformation Stone from the treasure box seemed to resonate with the Dao Transformation Stone Mother. Under the illumination of the Stone Mother's light, the color of the Dao Transformation Stone appeared even deeper.

Chen Tianhai first put away the jade slip, then caressed the blue gemstone. His expression was somewhat wistful, and then he looked at Sun Erlang and said, "Young sir, this Dao Transformation Stone is gifted to you."

Only when the Dao Transformation Stone fell into his hand did Sun Erlang snap back to his senses.

"Ah?"

Chapter 1196: A Dream Lasts a Thousand Years

A Dream Lasts a Thousand Years

Sun Erlang never expected that after Chen Tianhai had built up so much anticipation regarding the power of the Dao Transformation Stone, he would actually give him the Dao Transformation Stone that had been lost for thousands of years from Yi Xing's tomb. "Thank you, Senior!" However, Sun Erlang was not foolish. Fearing that the other party might go back on his word, he immediately accepted the treasure. Holding it gleefully, he examined it for a long time.

Sun Erlang's expression gradually shifted from surprise to embarrassment. "Senior, this Dao Transformation Stone…"

"It seems useless?" Chen Tianhai replied, "To experience the mysteries of the Dao Transformation Stone, you need to combine it with our sect's 'Dao Transformation Divine Unity' secret technique!"

Sun Erlang immediately became vigilant: "Senior, I already have a Master. I cannot join your Taiyan Sect…"

Chen Tianhai chuckled wryly: "Young sir, you worry too much. We have already gifted you the Dao Transformation Stone, why would we still care about this secret technique?"

With a wave of his hand, Sun Erlang, enveloped in illusory blue light, suddenly felt the information of the 'Dao Transformation Divine Unity' appear in his mind. Slowly circulating the secret technique, the blue gemstone in Sun Erlang's hand flowed like streams of light and was absorbed into his body. And in his sea of consciousness, a radiant crystal of the same shape was slowly forming.

Sun Erlang suddenly felt as if the heavens and earth had lit up. In his mind, countless thoughts flashed simultaneously. His thoughts surged like a storm, and memories from his childhood, even those he had almost forgotten, began to reappear. And upon thinking about his earlier confusion, why Senior Chen of the Taiyan Sect had treated him with such favor, Sun Erlang, who had only had vague guesses before, now derived several possibilities in his mind. The overtures to the Saint Dynasty Great Qi and his Master, his own special physique being beneficial to the Taiyan Sect, and the Taiyan Sect's ability to control through the Dao Transformation Stone—this was part of a conspiracy… Various possibilities were listed one after another.

At the same time, based on the external information obtained, the deductions were constantly adjusted. "This is 'Dao Transformation Divine Unity'?" After a long time, Sun Erlang emerged from his shock and couldn't help but exclaim. He couldn't help but look at the Dao Transformation Stone Mother before him. With just such a small fragment, it possessed such powerful divination and calculation abilities. Just how powerful was this Dao Transformation Stone Mother?

"Senior gifted me the Dao Transformation Stone, is it related to the 'simulation' you asked me about just now?" Gazing at the Dao Transformation Stone Mother, Sun Erlang suddenly asked with inspiration.

Chen Tianhai nodded inexplicably: "Besides the future of the Xuanhuang Realm, the Dao Transformation Stone Mother also contains many other fabricated worlds."

"It is both to fully utilize the Stone Mother's abilities and for better correction of the established reality."

"You can think of them as exercises."

Sun Erlang nodded thoughtfully. The moment he completely absorbed the Dao Transformation Stone, he had visions of returning and reporting this matter to his Master, and all the subsequent scenes. Compared to merely having a thought in the past, this time, even the expressions and reactions of the people he would interact with in the future instantly flashed before him.

"This is simulating the future. However, my calculation ability is insufficient, and I can only derive parts closely related to me."

"And the Dao Transformation Stone Mother, besides deriving the Xuanhuang Realm, even has surplus capacity to simulate more."

While Sun Erlang was contemplating, Chen Tianhai continued: "These fabricated worlds are mostly based on the original materials of the Xuanhuang Realm. Therefore, you might encounter many seemingly familiar existences…"

"But rest assured, they are real enough to allow you to truly experience a complete lifetime."

"Young sir, have you heard this saying? To govern a territory, the talents of a single county are sufficient. Although this principle is popular among mortals, it also applies to our cultivation world. The Xuan Heavenly Sect, which once dominated the heavens and earth, only had the close adherence of the twelve cultivators around the Xuan Heavenly King at its core."

"Xuan Heavenly Sect?" Sun Erlang had never heard this name before and was somewhat curious. However, Chen Tianhai had no intention of elaborating further. Instead, he continued his reasoning: "There is no shortage of talents in this world. What is lacking is merely the space and opportunity for them to grow."

"And in the worlds simulated by the Dao Transformation Stone Mother, we have created such a stage. It allows individuals like young sir to grow rapidly."

After all, due to his young age, Sun Erlang felt a sense of pride upon hearing Chen Tianhai's high praise for him. However, he soon frowned and asked, "How long does this simulation last? Will it make Master wait too long?"

"A thousand years in a dream, a thousand years in an instant. Young sir, are you ready?" Chen Tianhai suddenly shouted loudly.

At the same time, the Dao Transformation Stone Mother emitted a blue light ring. Within the ring, countless scenes of different worlds could be vaguely seen. A figure engulfed in blue light also flew out from Sun Erlang's sea of consciousness, heading directly into the Stone Mother's light ring.

When Chen Tianhai clearly saw where Sun Erlang had ended up, a peculiar expression appeared on his face. "Ancient Xuanhuang, a world where the immortal calamity had not yet occurred. Interesting…"

Chen Tianhai's words were not entirely complete. Indeed, to govern a territory, the talents of a single county are sufficient. However, this is merely enough. Although there are many talents in the world, there are always some who are extraordinary. They may be temporarily buried due to certain reasons, but as long as they get an opportunity, their destiny can be overturned overnight. The Dao Transformation Stone Mother has simulated and iterated through countless worlds. Whenever such individuals appear, they can drastically influence and alter the course of the world's destiny.

"Countless futures have countless branches. The existence or disappearance of certain beings does not affect these possible branches; they are all insignificant individuals, ordinary members of the masses."

"But the disappearance of certain individuals can lead to major changes in the future, or even directly cause the loss of a large number of possibilities. Such individuals are called 'Focal Variables.'"

"The Dao Transformation Stone Mother has statistically analyzed and summarized the numerous Focal Variables that have appeared in simulated worlds, developing an effective prediction method. This Sun Erlang fits certain characteristics of a Focal Variable."

Chen Tianhai's thoughts churned, which was also the reason he treated Sun Erlang so kindly. Since their hiding place had been discovered, the Taiyan Sect could not avoid being drawn into the future variables and becoming involved. It was natural to prepare early. He narrowed his eyes, as if trying to see everything happening in the world where Sun Erlang was located.

"As I predicted, three years of dormancy, one swift rise, and once momentum is established, no one can stop it."

"Fortunately, judging by his actions, order and rationality are still present."

"Not an 'Extreme Variable.'"

After reassuring himself, Chen Tianhai thought. "Someone who can teach such a disciple, I suppose that mysterious Sacred Emperor's actions will not be too unpredictable."

An 'Extreme Variable' is a special type of 'Focal Variable.' Once it appears, it can cause a devastating impact on the existing world, completely overturning the simulated worlds of the Dao Transformation Stone Mother in an instant. The Heavenly Venerate Transmission, who caused the downfall of the Ten Immortal Sects and six Longevity Realm experts, belonged to an 'Extreme Variable.'

Chen Tianhai's memories seemed to return to the past. In the grand hall of the Taiyan Sect.

"I have already replied to the Great Dao Sect. Mere Harmonious Dao cultivators are not to be feared," said Xingji Daoist, the previous Sect Master of Taiyan Sect and Chen Tianhai's Master, in a deep voice.

Chen Tianhai's expression was anxious: "How can you make a conclusion so hastily? I feel that this Heavenly Venerate Transmission is somewhat inexplicably strange. Why not observe further?"

Xingji Daoist was somewhat displeased: "The Dao Transformation Stone Mother has already performed over a hundred million derivations; what problems could there be?"

"Could it be that the combined efforts of so many Longevity Realm cultivators still cannot capture him?"

Chen Tianhai was instantly rendered speechless. The power gap between each major cultivation realm was like a chasm. While a Golden Core could kill a Nascent Soul, a Harmonious Dao expert seeking to eliminate a Longevity Realm expert… had been rare since ancient times in the Xuanhuang Realm. Furthermore, the operation to capture the Heavenly Venerate Transmission was personally led by Fang Dingge, the Sect Master of the Great Dao Sect. It was said that a total of six Longevity Realm experts would act together. Sect Master Fang was extremely cautious; even with such a significant disparity between the enemy and ourselves, he did not underestimate the situation. Not only was the operation strictly confidential, but only the Sect Masters of the Ten Immortal Sects and a few direct disciples were aware of it. He had even sent a message to the Taiyan Sect, seeking to use the Dao Transformation Stone Mother to derive any potential variables in this operation. Such caution was difficult for Xingji Daoist to comprehend. However, as the leader of the Great Dao Sect, he could not refuse the other party's request.

Xingji Daoist used the Dao Transformation Stone Mother to derive all possible outcomes in detail. The results of over a hundred million derivations all concluded with the orderly capture of the Heavenly Venerate Transmission. Theoretically speaking, the Ten Immortal Sects had almost no chance of failure in this operation.

However, for some reason, Chen Tianhai still had a lingering sense of intense unease. He had once disguised himself and secretly approached the Heavenly Venerate Transmission for observation. Before the Myriad Immortals Alliance had attracted the attention of the Ten Immortal Sects. The Heavenly Venerate Transmission himself appeared to be a kind and benevolent old man. For the sake of opening up a unique path for those who could not cultivate, he had established a unique path. But witnessing the fanaticism in the eyes of the new method cultivators surrounding the Heavenly Venerate Transmission, Chen Tianhai felt a chill to his bones. What unsettled him even more was that the Heavenly Venerate Transmission seemed to have sensed his secret observation at the time and looked in his direction, just for a moment. A simple, calm glance felt like a nightmare that repeatedly appeared in Chen Tianhai's mind. It was only after a long time that the negative emotions caused by that glance gradually subsided. However, the newly learned plan, known as the plan, had reawakened the nightmare.

As the foremost direct disciple of the Taiyan Sect, Chen Tianhai had already stepped halfway into the Harmonious Dao realm at a young age. He did not believe that ordinary Harmonious Dao cultivators could have such a terrifying impact on him. Out of personal shame, Chen Tianhai did not explicitly explain the anomalies he experienced to his Master. However, he repeatedly emphasized the extraordinary nature of the Heavenly Venerate Transmission in front of his Master, yet ultimately failed to change his Master's attitude.

After leaving his Master's place, Chen Tianhai's unease only intensified. He suddenly felt the urge to activate the Dao Transformation Stone Mother again to perform a derivation. Chen Tianhai was frightened by this thought. The Dao Transformation Stone Mother was the supreme treasure of the Taiyan Sect, the foundation of its existence, related to the present and even the future dao paths of all Taiyan Sect cultivators. Only the Sect Master of the Taiyan Sect had the right to use it. Even as the foremost direct disciple, Chen Tianhai could only observe from afar and was forbidden from approaching it rashly. The thought arose, and could not be calmed. It even made Chen Tianhai somewhat absent-minded.

Fortunately, he finally found an opportunity. The 'Indefinite Prison,' one of the Ten Sects, seemed to be experiencing some trouble and had sent a distress signal to the other Immortal Sects. The Grand Supreme, Heavenly Sword, and Beast Taming Sects were unable to disengage due to the plan to capture the Heavenly Venerate Transmission. Therefore, this matter was assigned to Xingji Daoist. From Xingji Daoist's expression before his departure, it was evident that the changes occurring within the Indefinite Prison were by no means minor. He handed over the sect's affairs to Chen Tianhai and the other elders. This gave Chen Tianhai an opportunity.

After a period of intense internal struggle, Chen Tianhai ultimately could not suppress the urge in his heart. He went to the Dao Transformation Stone Mother unbeknownst to anyone. All past derivation records were preserved. Chen Tianhai retrieved the previous derivation results. As expected, it was the same as his Master had said, and even his Master had held back some information. He had derived it a full ten billion times, and the results were completely consistent. However, for some reason, Chen Tianhai, who had personally witnessed these derivation results, was still unwilling to give up. He activated the Dao Transformation Stone Mother again. The azure light flickered continuously, and infinite possibilities played out.

"Urgh." A groan interrupted Chen Tianhai's thoughts. The connection with the Dao Transformation Stone Mother was severed, and Sun Erlang had returned from the simulation to reality. His eyes were closed, as if he was still adapting. The aura around him was changing dramatically at a visible rate. It was as if he had transformed from a sharp and brilliant young man into a composed master who had experienced a hundred tribulations in an instant.

"Thank you, Senior, for fulfilling my wish!" After a long time, Sun Erlang opened his eyes. His gaze was calm and profound.

"Young sir, what did you experience?" Chen Tianhai asked knowingly.

"During the ancient Ten Immortal Sects era, before the calamity descended. I was merely a mortal. By chance, I witnessed two Golden Core cultivators fighting and perishing together. Mustering my courage, I collected the resources from their bodies."

"After spending three years, I finally managed to open the storage rings left by the two Golden Core cultivators. From then on, I officially began my cultivation path…" Sun Erlang said calmly.

Chen Tianhai knew that although Sun Erlang narrated it briefly, the process of opening just those two storage rings in the simulated world was incredibly perilous. The old friends of the two Golden Core cultivators came one after another, searching for the whereabouts of the inheritance. Having a treasure trove but no way to access it. Putting all his hope on one gamble, he squandered all his family wealth, and finally obtained a crude cultivation method. Stumbling along, he finally reached the Qi Refining stage, enabling him to use the resources in the storage rings.

Sun Erlang recounted his experiences in the simulated world, eventually reaching the peak of the Harmonious Dao stage and being unable to break through, thus ending his journey. Chen Tianhai, despite having seen the other party's experiences long ago, still listened with great interest.

"If not for my impulsive decision back then, perhaps the Xuanhuang Realm would still be the same as it is now." Chen Tianhai thought to himself.

Chapter 1197: Heaven and Earth Overturned by a Single Thought

The World is Overturned by a Single Thought

Chen Tianhai's heart was slightly put at ease. "The person who taught such a disciple, I suppose that mysterious Sacred Emperor's actions will not be too unpredictable."

'Extreme Variables' are a special type of 'Focal Variable.' Once they appear, they can cause a devastating impact on the existing world, completely overturning the simulated worlds of the Dao Transformation Stone Mother in an instant. The Heavenly Venerate Transmission, who caused the downfall of the Ten Immortal Sects and six Longevity Realm experts, was an 'Extreme Variable.'

Chen Tianhai's memories seemed to return to the past. In the grand hall of the Taiyan Sect.

"I have already replied to the Great Dao Sect. A mere Harmonious Dao cultivator is not to be feared," said Xingji Daoist, the previous Sect Master of Taiyan Sect and Chen Tianhai's Master, in a deep voice.

Chen Tianhai's expression was anxious: "How can you make a conclusion so hastily? I feel that this Heavenly Venerate Transmission is somewhat inexplicably strange. Why not observe further?"

Xingji Daoist was somewhat displeased: "The Dao Transformation Stone Mother has already performed over a hundred million derivations; what problems could there be?"

"Could it be that the combined efforts of so many Longevity Realm cultivators still cannot capture him?"

Chen Tianhai was instantly rendered speechless. The power gap between each major cultivation realm was like a chasm. While a Golden Core could kill a Nascent Soul, a Harmonious Dao expert seeking to eliminate a Longevity Realm expert… had been rare since ancient times in the Xuanhuang Realm.

Furthermore, the operation to capture the Heavenly Venerate Transmission was personally led by Fang Dingge, the Sect Master of the Great Dao Sect. It was said that a total of six Longevity Realm experts would act together. Sect Master Fang was extremely cautious; even with such a significant disparity between the enemy and ourselves, he did not underestimate the situation.

Not only was the operation strictly confidential, but only the Sect Masters of the Ten Immortal Sects and a few direct disciples were aware of it. He had even sent a message to the Taiyan Sect, seeking to use the Dao Transformation Stone Mother to derive any potential variables in this operation. Such caution was difficult for Xingji Daoist to comprehend.

However, as the leader of the Great Dao Sect, he could not refuse the other party's request. Xingji Daoist used the Dao Transformation Stone Mother to derive all possible outcomes in detail. The results of over a hundred million derivations all concluded with the orderly capture of the Heavenly Venerate Transmission. Theoretically speaking, the Ten Immortal Sects had almost no chance of failure in this operation.

The Heavenly Venerate Transmission himself appeared to be a kind and benevolent old man. For the sake of opening up a unique path for those who could not cultivate, he had established a unique path. But witnessing the fanaticism in the eyes of the new method cultivators surrounding the Heavenly Venerate Transmission, Chen Tianhai felt a chill to his bones.

What unsettled him even more was that the Heavenly Venerate Transmission seemed to have sensed his secret observation at the time and looked in his direction, just for a moment. A simple, calm glance felt like a nightmare that repeatedly appeared in Chen Tianhai's mind. It was only after a long time that the negative emotions caused by that glance gradually subsided. However, the newly learned plan, known as the plan, had reawakened the nightmare.

As the foremost direct disciple of the Taiyan Sect, Chen Tianhai had already stepped halfway into the Harmonious Dao realm at a young age. He did not believe that ordinary Harmonious Dao cultivators could have such a terrifying impact on him. Out of personal shame, Chen Tianhai did not explicitly explain the anomalies he experienced to his Master. However, he repeatedly emphasized the extraordinary nature of the Heavenly Venerate Transmission in front of his Master, yet ultimately failed to change his Master's attitude.

After leaving his Master's place, Chen Tianhai's unease only intensified. He suddenly felt the urge to activate the Dao Transformation Stone Mother again to perform a derivation.

Chen Tianhai was frightened by this thought. The Dao Transformation Stone Mother was the supreme treasure of the Taiyan Sect, the foundation of its existence, related to the present and even the future dao paths of all Taiyan Sect cultivators. Only the Sect Master of the Taiyan Sect had the right to use it. Even as the foremost direct disciple, Chen Tianhai could only observe from afar and was forbidden from approaching it rashly.

The thought arose, and could not be calmed. It even made Chen Tianhai somewhat absent-minded. Fortunately, he finally found an opportunity.

The 'Indefinite Prison,' one of the Ten Sects, seemed to be experiencing some trouble and had sent a distress signal to the other Immortal Sects. The Grand Supreme, Heavenly Sword, and Beast Taming Sects were unable to disengage due to the plan to capture the Heavenly Venerate Transmission. Therefore, this matter was assigned to Xingji Daoist.

From Xingji Daoist's expression before his departure, it was evident that the changes occurring within the Indefinite Prison were by no means minor. He handed over the sect's affairs to Chen Tianhai and the other elders. This gave Chen Tianhai an opportunity.

After a period of intense internal struggle, Chen Tianhai ultimately could not suppress the urge in his heart. He went to the Dao Transformation Stone Mother unbeknownst to anyone. All past derivation records were preserved. Chen Tianhai retrieved the previous derivation results. As expected, it was the same as his Master had said, and even his Master had held back some information. He had derived it a full ten billion times, and the results were completely consistent.

However, for some reason, Chen Tianhai, who had personally witnessed these derivation results, was still unwilling to give up. He activated the Dao Transformation Stone Mother again. The azure light flickered continuously, and infinite possibilities played out.

"Urgh." A groan interrupted Chen Tianhai's thoughts. The connection with the Dao Transformation Stone Mother was severed, and Sun Erlang had returned from the simulation to reality. His eyes were closed, as if he was still adapting. The aura around him was changing dramatically at a visible rate. It was as if he had transformed from a sharp and brilliant young man into a composed master who had experienced a hundred tribulations in an instant.

"Thank you, Senior, for fulfilling my wish!" After a long time, Sun Erlang opened his eyes. His gaze was calm and profound.

"Young sir, what did you experience?" Chen Tianhai asked knowingly.

"During the ancient Ten Immortal Sects era, before the calamity descended. I was merely a mortal. By chance, I witnessed two Golden Core cultivators fighting and perishing together. Mustering my courage, I collected the resources from their bodies."

"After spending three years, I finally managed to open the storage rings left by the two Golden Core cultivators. From then on, I officially began my cultivation path…" Sun Erlang said calmly.

Chen Tianhai knew that although Sun Erlang narrated it briefly, the process of opening just those two storage rings in the simulated world was incredibly perilous. The old friends of the two Golden Core cultivators came one after another, searching for the whereabouts of the inheritance. Having a treasure trove but no way to access it. Putting all his hope on one gamble, he squandered all his family wealth, and finally obtained a crude cultivation method. Stumbling along, he finally reached the Qi Refining stage, enabling him to use the resources in the storage rings.

Sun Erlang recounted his experiences in the simulated world, eventually reaching the peak of the Harmonious Dao stage and being unable to break through, thus ending his journey.

Chen Tianhai, despite having seen the other party's experiences long ago, still listened with great interest.

"If not for my impulsive decision back then, perhaps the Xuanhuang Realm would still be the same as it is now." Chen Tianhai thought to himself.

Chapter 1198: Sinner of the Xuanhuang Realm

Criminal of the Xuanhuang Realm

In a sense, Chen Tianhai bore a significant responsibility for the Xuanhuang Realm's current state. It was precisely because he rashly activated the Dao Transformation Stone Mother and performed over ten billion derivations that the Heavenly Venerate Transmission caught a glimpse of the only possibility of victory. He, Chen Tianhai, was an unforgivable sinner for the demise of the Ten Immortal Sects and the six Longevity Realm experts!

The numerous derivations by the Dao Transformation Stone Mother could not be concealed. When his Master, Xingji Daoist, returned and discovered the horrific consequences, likely caused by Chen Tianhai's internal betrayal, he was enraged and intended to kill Chen Tianhai to atone to the world. However, after careful consideration, Xingji Daoist ultimately did not act.

Firstly, their master-disciple bond was deep, like father and son, and Xingji Daoist was ultimately soft-hearted. Secondly, if this news were truly leaked, the Taiyan Sect would become a target of public outrage and might even be eliminated from the Xuanhuang Realm. After all, traitors are always more detestable than enemies. But the tragic deaths of his former friends and his extreme self-condemnation made it impossible for Xingji Daoist to pretend that nothing had happened.

Thus, he could only strip Chen Tianhai of his status as the foremost direct disciple, imprison him in the Taiyan Sect's prison, and suppress him forever. Externally, it was declared that Chen Tianhai had defected.

Chen Tianhai did not know how long he spent in the dark and gloomy prison. By the time he was released, the calamity had already descended, and the Taiyan Sect was facing a crisis of survival. The world was in chaos, and the once-renowned Ten Immortal Sects were preoccupied with their own survival.

The Taiyan Sect disciples, by continuously using the Dao Transformation Stone for complex derivations to suppress the killing intent caused by the inability to cultivate multiple laws simultaneously, had not fallen into extreme chaos like other Immortal Sects. However, they had reached their limit. Not only the Dao Transformation Stones within each cultivator's body, but even the Dao Transformation Stone Mother itself, due to the sudden appearance of an 'Extreme Variable,' had overthrown all past derivations and began recalculating at an accelerated rate. To seek a sliver of hope for the Taiyan Sect, their computational power was almost completely depleted.

Before Xingji Daoist died of exhaustion, he released Chen Tianhai. And he pointed out a path for him.

"Discard your physical body, and your information will be immortal."

"Fortune and disaster are interdependent. Though you made a grave mistake back then, you also predicted the Heavenly Venerate Transmission's true nature because of it."

"Now, the Heavenly Venerate Transmission has been lured away by our final gambit and has temporarily left the Xuanhuang Realm, also buying us a moment of respite to preserve our strength."

"Otherwise, all our Immortal Sect legacies would perish!"

Without even having time to finish his last words, Xingji Daoist had already perished. And before the calamity of cultivating multiple laws simultaneously completely engulfed the Taiyan Sect, Chen Tianhai also completed the integration of the entire Taiyan Sect into the Dao Transformation Stone Mother. Fortunately, before his Master's death, he had already eradicated all opposing forces within the sect for him. Otherwise, Chen Tianhai would not have lasted until that moment.

When every person in the sect could experience and utilize the Dao Transformation Stone Mother's nearly infinite computational power, Chen Tianhai knew his Master's decision was correct. And after integrating the fragmented Dao Transformation Stones back into his body, mingled with the intentions of thousands of Taiyan Sect cultivators, the Dao Transformation Stone Mother itself underwent some miraculous transformation. It developed its own consciousness. A collective consciousness belonging to the Taiyan Sect.

During the Taiyan Sect's millennia of seclusion in the Tai Xuan Realm, Chen Tianhai reviewed the past and re-examined his actions back then. At that time, he was constantly uneasy and had suspected he had fallen into a hidden trap set by the Heavenly Venerate Transmission. However, neither the sect's restrictions, magic treasures, nor even his Master, or other Longevity Realm experts from the Grand Supreme and Heavenly Sword Sects, could find anything amiss with him. Chen Tianhai could only assume it was purely his own inner demons acting up.

"The Heavenly Venerate Transmission's methods are truly insidious and difficult to guard against."

"It's a pity that my Master passed away before he could reveal his true background. As for the other knowledgeable individuals from the Immortal Sects, they have long since disappeared. However, after so many years, I have also derived a general idea…"

Chen Tianhai's thoughts churned as he listened to Sun Erlang recount his simulated experiences.

"By the way, Senior, the cultivation techniques I learned in the simulated world…" Sun Erlang hesitated to speak.

"Naturally, they are also real," Chen Tianhai said lightly. "However, it's best if you don't learn to use them in reality. Otherwise, you might attract the pursuit of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's guardian hall," Chen Tianhai added.

"Myriad Immortals Alliance Guardian Hall…" Sun Erlang whispered, but there was no fear in his eyes.

"Alright, since young sir has gained much, you may return now. Don't keep your Master waiting too long." Chen Tianhai issued a polite dismissal. "Yi Shu will accompany you to the Great Qi minor world."

Before the words were even fully spoken, Sun Erlang felt his vision blur. When he came to his senses, he was already outside the blue transparent building. Yi Shu stood smiling by his side, as if he had been waiting for a long time.

"Hmm?" Sun Erlang immediately sensed that Yi Shu was different from before. He was even different from all the other cultivators within the Taiyan Sect. No longer possessing a cold, completely uniform shared aura, but a living, breathing entity with its own vitality.

"Thanks to young sir, I temporarily have a physical body again and can go out and have some fun." Yi Shu smiled and explained the current situation of the Taiyan Sect to Sun Erlang.

"Information is immortal…" After experiencing hundreds of years of simulation, Sun Erlang had clearly become much more composed. But he was still shocked by the Taiyan Sect's heaven-defying ideas.

"It doesn't matter much whether there's a physical body or not. Even physical reality is a burden. But occasionally varying things is not bad." Yi Shu followed Sun Erlang out of the Tai Xuan Realm, heading directly for the entrance to the Congyun Sea and the Great Qi minor world. Clearly, the Taiyan Sect was not unfamiliar with the location of the Great Qi minor world.

However, upon passing through the Immortal Severing Grand Formation and seeing only a vast, desolate void without any sign of a small world, Yi Shu finally showed a hint of astonishment.

Sun Erlang was first stunned, then as if recalling memories from a hundred years ago, he said somewhat awkwardly: "Senior, please wait a moment. Our Saint Dynasty Great Qi is currently drifting in the void, its location uncertain. I don't know where it is right now…"

"Let me ask." A moment later, a golden light flashed from the darkness, instantly arriving before the two of them.

"Greetings, Senior Bai Hua!" Sun Erlang recognized the arrival and respectfully bowed.

Bai Hua Daoist glanced at Yi Shu without saying much. "Follow me." Glazed golden light enveloped the two, and the surrounding void seemed to twist, emitting strange light. When the golden light dissipated, they had already returned to the Saint Dynasty Great Qi.

Chapter 1199: Xuanhuang's Tribulation Passer

The Xuanhuang Deliverer of Calamity

"Senior Bai Hua's cultivation seems to have improved significantly again?" Sun Erlang, with his hundred years of simulated experience, was now far from what he used to be. Naturally, he could see the changes that had occurred to Bai Hua Daoist during his absence. He couldn't help but feel a sense of awe. Meanwhile, Yi Shu was curiously observing the five interconnected rings in the sky, resonating with each other, and the six bright stars surrounding the rings.
