"Senior Bai Hua has moved two more Grotto-Heavens. It must have been exhausting. These new Grotto-Heavens seem to be even larger in scale than the previous ones, no wonder I feel that Great Qi's speed in traversing the void has noticeably increased," Sun Erlang thought to himself. "The Saint Dynasty Great Qi truly lives up to its name."

Yi Shu sensed the various powers constantly enveloping the small world around him and sincerely remarked. "I believe that in at most fifty years, such a drastic transformation in a mere mortal world will occur. I am truly curious about your Master, young sir."

Bai Hua Daoist glanced at Yi Shu again inexplicably. However, she did not speak, merely let out a cold snort. She brought the two before the Sacred Emperor's Seat and then left directly.

Looking at the towering, mountain-like figure seated above, Sun Erlang's heart trembled. He had initially thought that after experiencing so many realistic simulations in the virtual world and seeing the peak Longevity Realm experts of the former Ten Immortal Sects, he would be able to act more freely when facing his Master. But at this moment, Sun Erlang knew he was wrong. When facing a Longevity Realm expert, Sun Erlang felt the pressure from the difference in realms, the oppression of the strong towards the weak. But when facing his Master, the Faceless Sacred Emperor of Great Qi, Sun Erlang's body, mind, and even soul trembled uncontrollably. The reason was the unfathomable mystery of the Faceless Sacred Emperor, and… a natural condescension as if a higher-level being viewed a lower-level life form.

"Master, I have returned." Sun Erlang knelt on one knee, just as he had in the past.

Yi Shu, on the other hand, cupped his hands slightly. "It's good that you've returned. It seems this trip has yielded significant gains." The voice of the Faceless Sacred Emperor Li Ping echoed in the empty, grand Sacred Emperor's Seat.

Sun Erlang recounted his experiences in detail. After listening to Sun Erlang's report, Li Ping finally spoke to Yi Shu: "Since the Taiyan Sect is so courteous, we cannot be impolite. During this time, you will guide him around the Saint Dynasty." "Without any restrictions, you can take him wherever he wishes to see."

Sun Erlang was slightly stunned, then quickly said, "Disciple understands." "Go now." He did not intend to communicate with Yi Shu at all.

Yi Shu, although a manifestation of the collective consciousness of the Taiyan Sect, also had his own individual personality and temper. He tilted his head slightly, looking up at the Faceless Sacred Emperor seated above, and cupped his hands again. Even after he left the Sacred Emperor's Seat, the Sacred Emperor had not uttered another word.

"Words are not as convincing as experience. Senior, after you have made this journey, you will naturally have your answers." To prevent the other party from feeling awkward, Sun Erlang quickly explained.

"Good, then let me see what is so special about this place." Yi Shu responded with a smile, but his smile seemed different from before.

When he saw that almost everyone in the Saint Dynasty Great Qi was cultivating the same technique, Yi Shu's eyes flashed with surprise.

When he saw the Immortal Spiritual Towers casually placed everywhere in the Saint Dynasty, constantly releasing spiritual energy outwards, Yi Shu's smile slowly disappeared.

When he observed the 'Myriad Spirits Grand Formation' connecting the Saint Dynasty Great Qi to other minor worlds, Yi Shu's expression became one of disbelief and doubt. "Young sir, do you know…" Yi Shu's words stopped at his lips and then he swallowed them.

Sun Erlang thought the other party was shocked by the sights of the Saint Dynasty. Seeing that he had not spoken, he did not press further.

Subsequently, Sun Erlang took Yi Shu on a tour of some of the Saint Dynasty's important locations, such as Wang Xuanba's exotic beast breeding base and the site where the Sky-Patrolling Arrows were forged. Along the way, Yi Shu became increasingly silent. His brow furrowed with confusion and doubt from time to time. Seeing the other party's expression, Sun Erlang, who had been shocked at the Taiyan Sect, felt a sense of satisfaction and secret pride. "Elder Yi, is there anything else you wish to see?"

Yi Shu remained silent for a moment. He gazed into the distance, as if taking in this magical small world entirely. "If it weren't for your intention to counterattack the Xuanhuang Realm, I would almost believe this was a hidden secret realm of the Myriad Immortals Alliance," Yi Shu suddenly remarked after a long pause. "You indeed have the qualifications to contend with the Myriad Immortals Alliance, considering the number of cultivators and the top experts you possess." "However, based on what I have seen so far, it is not enough to form an alliance with our Taiyan Sect," Yi Shu concluded. "Young sir, the waters of the Myriad Immortals Alliance are far deeper than you imagine," Yi Shu said meaningfully.

Sun Erlang did not react with dissatisfaction to Yi Shu's response, merely nodding thoughtfully.

After some thought, Sun Erlang finally led Yi Shu to the space beneath the Sacred Emperor's Seat where Yin Shangren was located. He did not meet Yin Shangren in person. However, just by observing the more than a hundred children who were cultivating here, all having reached the Foundation Establishment stage at such a young age, Yi Shu's composure finally broke. "This…"

With his insight, he instantly recognized the peculiarities of these Foundation Establishment children. "How is this possible?"

At this moment, in the Tai Xuan Realm, the entire Taiyan Sect, and everyone within it, turned their gaze towards the Great Qi minor world. Even the Dao Transformation Stone Mother, which was constantly emitting azure light, seemed to briefly pause.

"Not long ago, a young man took a step further on the basis of 'Establishing Foundation with Me,' achieving the Primal Chaos Golden Core," Sun Erlang said softly. "'Establishing Foundation with Me?!'"

Upon hearing these words, Yi Shu froze completely. It was not an adjective, but truly a state of mental stagnation. Sun Erlang, possessing the Dao Transformation Stone, could see at a glance that this was the manifestation of the Dao Transformation Stone's computational power operating at its absolute limit.

"Impossible!" After a long time, Yi Shu blurted out.

The children in this place, who were diligently cultivating under Yin Shangren's teachings, all looked towards Yi Shu. Their gazes held displeasure. Because they had been taught by Yin Shangren since childhood to most resist the word "impossible."

Yi Shu realized his 失态 (losing composure) and let out a cough to cover it up. He slowly approached a chubby, exquisitely carved female child and observed her carefully. The more he looked, the more astonished he became. Sun Erlang saw that Yi Shu's hand subconsciously clenched tightly. "Beyond Variables? Beyond Variables?" "No, this is not Beyond Variables, this is…" Yi Shu suddenly looked up, as if making eye contact with the Faceless Sacred Emperor seated on the Sacred Emperor's Seat. "Xuanhuang Deliverer of Calamity?!"

Chapter 1200: No One Can Turn the Tide

No One Can Stem the Tide of Heaven

Many years ago, when Yi Shu and most of the Taiyan Sect cultivators first learned of the Door of Deliverance Sect's theory, they all scoffed at it. Facing impending disaster, instead of actively seeking solutions, they chose to be turtles hiding in their shells, placing their hopes on some illusory 'person destined to end the calamity.' This was completely baseless and unpredictable.

However, as one of the Ten Immortal Sects, inheriting from Grand Master Tiandu, the Door of Deliverance Sect's lineage appeared in antiquity. Its ability to endure for so many years proved that it had its own unique reasons. It was just that outsiders could not comprehend the profundity of the Door of Deliverance Sect.

Today, upon arriving at the Saint Dynasty Great Qi, which seemed to have sprung from nowhere, witnessing technologies comparable to the Myriad Immortals Alliance's top standards, and a new cultivation method that was completely different from current practices and could completely overturn the foundation laid by Heavenly Venerate Transmission in the Xuanhuang Realm, Yi Shu's mind instantly recalled the words of the Door of Deliverance Sect years ago.

At that time, the great calamity had just begun. The core members of the Ten Immortal Sects gathered, discussing possible countermeasures. Each sect expressed their opinions, but the Door of Deliverance Sect remained indifferent. "Everyone, calamities are unavoidable. If they could be avoided through struggle, what would be the point of calling it a calamity?"

The Sect Master of the Door of Deliverance Sect, Lu Chengheng, with eyes observing his nose and nose observing his heart, acted as if it had nothing to do with him. "Is this the reason your Door of Deliverance Sect scattered those 'Eyes of Contemplation' everywhere?" Xiahou Yan, the Lord of the Indefinite Prison, who had the quickest temper, retorted with a displeased expression.

"Xiahou, you don't understand. This is a necessary measure to await the appearance of the 'Xuanhuang Deliverer of Calamity'," Lu Chengheng said calmly. "Hogwash about the Xuanhuang Deliverer of Calamity. Facing calamity, all living beings perish. If everyone is dead, where would this savior appear from?" Xiahou almost swore out loud.

"Aren't you questioning the Grand Master's inheritance?" Lu Chengheng's single sentence silenced Xiahou Yan. "Aren't there still you all?" Lu Chengheng smiled and then said meaningfully, "The Xuanhuang Realm is not so easily destroyed. If there is any cultivation realm in this star sea that can survive until the end, it must be our Xuanhuang."

The leaders of the Ten Sects fell silent, none raising an objection. After a brief silence, perhaps to appease everyone, Lu Chengheng briefly explained, "The theory of deliverance is not baseless. Great calamities and cycles of birth and death are part of the natural order of heaven and earth. Even the great calamity of the Immortal Realm may not be beyond the expectations of True Immortals."

"You are all plunged into panic, yet look at Grand Master. Has He shown the slightest sign of distress? He is not concerned." Xuanji, the leader of the Grand Supreme Sect, who had remained silent, finally spoke, "Grand Master's cultivation is profound. He can traverse the Immortal Ruins with ease. The calamity that caused the destruction of the Xuanhuang Realm is of no concern to Him. We cannot do the same. Brother Lu, I will not prevent you from choosing to remain secluded, but you cannot completely refrain from contributing to facing the calamity."

Seeing the unified gaze of everyone, Lu Chengheng finally nodded and compromised. However, Lu Chengheng's last sentence silenced everyone again. "One day, you will all know that our Door of Deliverance Sect was right."

At this moment, crossing thousands of years of time, Yi Shu, the collective consciousness of the Taiyan Sect, suddenly recalled Lu Chengheng's words from back then. Upon a superficial understanding of the principle of 'Establishing Foundation with Me,' the Dao Transformation Stone Mother fed this variable into the future derivations of the Xuanhuang Realm. The originally clear future became blurred as if struck by a chaotic storm. Even with the Stone Mother's current divine computational power, it became somewhat lost for a time.

The Taiyan Sect had also attempted derivations of new cultivation methods capable of subverting the Heavenly Venerate Transmission system. But… Creating something from nothing is different from deriving the future based on existing data. The Dao Transformation Stone Mother could only judge that such a possibility existed, but the probability was too small. It was even smaller than the probability of the Heavenly Venerate Transmission surviving the encirclement and siege by Longevity Realm experts back then.

Besides the sheer difficulty of creating a new cultivation method, the more important factor was the pervasive influence of the Heavenly Venerate Transmission on the Xuanhuang Realm. Just as cultivators gradually forget the Xuanhuang Realm's calamities and continuously ignore the geographical changes occurring in the Xuanhuang Realm over thousands of years. The derivation of a new cultivation method is not only the ultimate manifestation of one's creativity but also a struggle against the influence of the Heavenly Venerate Transmission. Thus, as deduced by the Dao Transformation Stone Mother, which fully understood the current power of the Heavenly Venerate Transmission, the probability of a new cultivation method being born was infinitesimally close to zero.

However, something that far exceeded the possibilities of derivation inexplicably occurred. In a corner of the Xuanhuang Realm, drifting in the void and still unknown to anyone, a newly formed force… The new cultivation method had not only quietly emerged but had even reached the Golden Core stage! It was as if the sky was falling, causing the derivations of the Dao Transformation Stone Mother to falter momentarily.

This was because, based on all known factors, it was impossible to explain the reason for the emergence of the new cultivation method at this point in time. It could only be explained by the uncommon, external 'Xuanhuang Deliverer of Calamity' who was outside the variables. The Ten Sects had also discussed the Xuanhuang Deliverer of Calamity privately amongst themselves, reaching a near-unanimous conclusion: If such a Deliverer of Calamity truly existed, they would either be from outside the Xuanhuang Realm or the reincarnation of a powerful individual. A native cultivator who grew solely on their own could in no way possibly turn the tide of disaster. Even with extraordinary genius, it was impossible. The Xuanhuang Realm's environment had already ceased to provide the fertile ground capable of nurturing someone who could contend with the Heavenly Venerate Transmission.

"What is the origin of this Faceless Sacred Emperor of Great Qi?" At this moment, Yi Shu, or rather the Taiyan Sect's collective consciousness, had completely abandoned any thought of disdain. Instead, they regarded the Saint Dynasty Great Qi as an equal, or even a higher-ranking power. And they were truly deriving the possibility of forming an alliance with the Saint Dynasty Great Qi.

As one of the former rulers of the Xuanhuang Realm, now compressed by the Myriad Immortals Alliance led by the Heavenly Venerate Transmission to reside only in the Tai Xuan minor world, it was impossible for the Taiyan Sect not to harbor any resentment. Even though they no longer needed land or resources, the fact that what they once possessed was stripped away fueled a lingering resentment within the Taiyan Sect's consciousness, like a recurring nightmare.

"Sects like the Grand Dao and Grand Supreme, although outwardly resisting the Myriad Immortals Alliance, had long since colluded with the Heavenly Venerate Transmission and become his lackeys." "However, like us, they have likely not completely surrendered. What they lack is only an opportunity." And the emergence of the Saint Dynasty Great Qi, especially the appearance of the new cultivation method, gave the Taiyan Sect a glimmer of hope. However, as a sect that had survived since the ancient calamity, they approached any decision concerning their fate with extreme caution.

Chapter 1201: The Future of Dao Dissolution

The Future of Dao Transformation

Yi Shu gradually recovered from his shock but still did not express his stance. However, his actions had already changed. Originally, he had planned to observe for a while and then return. Now, he requested Sun Erlang to allow him to stay for a long period of observation.

Sun Erlang looked troubled: "I cannot make this decision on my own; I need to seek instructions from Master."

Yi Shu nodded: "I believe your Master will agree."

As expected, the Faceless Sacred Emperor agreed to the Taiyan Sect's request to stay, but with a condition.

"Help the cultivators in the Saint Dynasty Great Qi grow rapidly through 'simulation'?" Yi Shu hesitated for a moment.

"Master said that even if the Taiyan Sect did not assist, he had other methods, though they would be more troublesome. The core of the Taiyan Sect is their derivation of the Xuanhuang's future. As long as there is no definitive outcome, Master also agrees to the Taiyan Sect maintaining a certain degree of neutrality. Consider it a form of transaction," Sun Erlang repeated Li Ping's words verbatim.

Yi Shu fell silent for a moment, and after deliberation between the Taiyan Sect and the Dao Transformation Stone Mother, they finally agreed. For the Taiyan Sect, a few more simulations were merely the utilization of idle computational power, but it could open up another path for the future, which was undoubtedly a worthwhile deal. It was like when some cultivators chose to flee before the calamity descended; the Ten Immortal Sects never placed all their hopes on a single option.

From then on, the Saint Dynasty Great Qi gained an observer. Besides the Sacred Emperor's Seat and the place where the You Clan resided, and the Xuanhuang Realm Fishing Pond, Yi Shu could observe freely without any constraints.

Li Ping was not worried about this. With the fortune of the Saint Dynasty bestowed upon him, coupled with the continuous improvement of the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation, Yi Shu's every move was under his control. Even Yi Shu's life and death were within his thoughts.

Meanwhile, in the distant Xuanhuang Realm, someone was already plotting against the Taiyan Sect.

"Although I have no intention of harming others, I must leave a fallback plan."

"The Taiyan Sect has abandoned their physical realities and collectively exists within the Dao Transformation Stone Mother. Information is immortal, which is truly remarkable. Even when Immortal Experts from the Immortal Ruins wield destructive power, they can escape that terrifying calamity. However…"

"As the saying goes, each trade has its specialty!"

In the Yan Fa Jue space, Li Fan appeared to be meditating with his eyes closed. In reality, his thoughts were constantly churning. Information immortality rendered physical means and even ordinary immortal techniques ineffective. However, data pollution might be effective.

As far as Li Fan knew, among the current circulating lineages in the Xuanhuang Realm, such a method did not exist. His idea stemmed from the mysterious 'Primordial Origin Spirit Grand Array.' A composite of nine Immortal-grade Grand Arrays, its power was unimaginable, capable of recreating earth, fire, water, and wind in the void and creating a new world. Fortunately, with the 'End Dissolution Disc,' and through various coincidences, Li Fan had initially mastered three of them: 'Xuanji, Myriad Spirits Returning to Numbers,' 'Arid Fall, Void Chamber Blooming Flowers,' and 'Boundless, Primordial Seen Square.' Among them, the Xuanji, Myriad Spirits Returning to Numbers Grand Array possessed the miraculous ability to digitize everything within the array's coverage and transform it at will.

"Although it is only theoretical, the materials required to set up the array are fundamentally unobtainable. Thankfully, the Taiyan Sect also lacks physical form, making pure information more prone to flaws."

"Primordial Square, Myriad Spirits Returning to Numbers, if the two arrays cooperate…"

In his sea of consciousness, the End Dissolution Disc, aided by the computational power of the Dao Transformation Stone, was rapidly deriving a brand new array formation.

In the past six months, Li Fan's clone had roughly completed the analysis of the Primordial Square Array within the 'Immeasurable Mirror.' After the clone's repairs, the abilities of the damaged Immeasurable Mirror had significantly improved. The corresponding price was that the clone had weakened further. However, Li Fan was not worried. Sun Luyuan had long failed to complete the task assigned by the mirror master 'Fu,' and even his intentional perfunctory actions had been noticed by the other party. The pressure he bore was increasing, and perhaps soon he would be forced to yield and attempt to spy on the Heavenly Profound Mirror again using the Immeasurable Mirror.

Sensing the news from his clone Li Ping, Li Fan was now contemplating other matters. He was pondering the origin of the Dao Transformation Stone Mother. When the Taiyan Sect initially received the inheritance from Grand Master Tiandu, they likely did not possess the Dao Transformation Stone Mother. It was only later that they somehow found such a treasure, which transformed their sect's cultivation method from one suitable only for a select few to one that everyone could practice, thus completely solidifying the Taiyan Sect's standing among the Ten Sects.

"There are many divination treasures in the Xuanhuang Realm, such as the Immeasurable Mirror. Although damaged, it can still predict some future events. However, the wondrous nature of the Immeasurable Mirror and even the Heavenly Profound Mirror is more like the result of refining Immortal-grade power; they are 'tools.'"

"But the Dao Transformation Stone Mother is more like pure 'substance.'"

"Legendary heavenly materials and earthly treasures… Although the Xuanhuang Realm is vast, it doesn't seem like a place that could naturally give birth to such divine artifacts."

Li Fan suddenly recalled a lost record he heard from someone from the Door of Deliverance Sect. An alien star fell upon the Xuanhuang Realm, causing all spiritual energy in the Xuanhuang Realm to fail. "Could it be that this Dao Transformation Stone Mother also originated from beyond the star sea?" Li Fan thus speculated. However, it was only speculation; only by infiltrating the Dao Transformation Stone one day could the true answer be known.

"The Stone Mother derives the future purely through its own powerful computational ability. Even so, it has reached a certain extreme, demonstrating the power of its calculation. If supplemented by external objects to further optimize its derivation methods, who knows what heights it could reach."

For example, the Dao Transformation Stone in Li Fan's sea of consciousness, although promoted to the upper grade after several fusions, still struggled to derive Immortal-grade Grand Arrays when acting alone, let alone such existences as the 'Life and Death Reversal Grand Array.' Similarly, relying solely on the Dissolution Disc itself, being merely a mortal artifact, still made it somewhat challenging to derive Immortal-grade Grand Arrays. However, the combination of the two was vastly different.

"Mutually beneficial, enhancing each other."

Such a harmonious scene made Li Fan fantasize about what it would be like if the Dao Transformation Stone Mother were equipped with something like the End Dissolution Disc, and not just for array formations. It would lead to immeasurable possibilities. The Yan Fa Jue cultivation method, the future prediction of the Immeasurable Mirror… If these were combined with the terrifying computational power of the Dao Transformation Stone Mother, it would undoubtedly lead to a qualitative change. Perhaps by continuously cycling through each life, the Dao Transformation Stone Mother, which had already reached the pinnacle of perfection, could be infinitely superimposed. Pushing it to an unimaginable level.

The End Dissolution Disc's assistance to Li Fan in his cycles of reincarnation was already beyond words. If other factors were added… it couldn't help but make Li Fan's heart race.

"Perhaps the path to breaking through this predicament lies within."

"With treasures before us, it depends on how we plan."

Li Fan's eyes flickered.

(End of this chapter)

Chapter 1202: Chief of the Law Protection Hall

Chief of the Law Enforcement Hall

The Dao Transformation Stone Mother, being a being that had successfully survived the Xuanhuang Realm's tribulation of annihilation, was not to be underestimated by Li Fan.

"There is no need to rush for success. In this lifetime, I will be an absolutely reliable partner to gain the Taiyan Sect's trust and learn more of their hidden secrets."

"I myself will first perfect this data pollution array and, if opportunities arise, try it out on a small scale to see the effects."

The Yan Fa Jue space provided Li Fan with safe time, undisturbed by the outside world. Other than occasionally dealing with the little萝莉's (loli's) tantrums, it was quite leisurely.

The communication between the three guarding elders became less and less frequent, each immersed in their own worlds. However, one day, a special group of people arrived in the Yan Fa Jue space. Without the Law Enforcement Jade Token, they were granted special approval by the Immortal Alliance and, led by the Chief Elder of the Law Enforcement Hall, arrived here.

Hua Yueye, who was usually a bit lazy, seemed a bit nervous and greeted repeatedly, "Greetings, Elder Xu."

Li Fan noticed that not only the other two guardians, but even the usually carefree and fearless Yan Fa Jue little萝莉 (loli) had become much more restrained.

While bowing, Li Fan looked at the white-haired old man before him, who appeared blind, and his mind flashed with information about this Chief of the Law Enforcement Hall.

"Xu Yuanxian has served as the Chief Elder of the Law Enforcement Hall for over three thousand years. Although he appears amiable on the surface, he is actually eccentric and rigid in temperament. He adheres to the Immortal Alliance's system to a dogmatic degree, showing no mercy. He even refuses to break rules when those who transmit techniques come to visit. He is valued by the Legate Jiang, and although others may disapprove of him, they can do nothing about him."

"Since he can serve as the Chief Elder of the Law Enforcement Hall, Xu Yuanxian's own strength is unfathomable, not comparable to ordinary Harmonious Dao cultivators. The Myriad Immortals Alliance's only record of killing a Harmonious Dao cultivator and retrieving leaked techniques was an action taken by this person. It was clean and swift, without even giving observers time to react."

Xu Yuanxian stated the purpose of his visit: "The Immortal Alliance's grand examination has just concluded, and these young ones are the cream of the crop. The Legate Council has specially approved them to use Yan Fa Jue to derive a Harmonious Dao level technique."

"Hmm?"

"How can this be?!"

The three guardians and the Yan Fa Jue little萝莉 (loli) were all somewhat surprised. The little萝莉 (loli) pouted, about to complain. Glancing at Xu Yuanxian's expression, she cautiously swallowed her words.

Li Fan was the fastest to react, nodding, "Please, Chief Elder, present the Council's seal." With a serious expression, he did not slack off just because the other party was his superior.

Xu Yuanxian was also very cooperative, displaying a seal. Sensing the Legate aura surrounding it, Li Fan meticulously verified the information, and only then nodded to indicate it had passed inspection.

Postponing the cultivators waiting for deduction, Li Fan arranged for Yan Fa Jue to handle the tasks of these newly recruited Immortal Alliance cultivators first. A total of sixteen people, with different ages and cultivation levels.

The giant Yan Fa light sphere continuously rotated, and the little萝莉 (loli) grumpily performed the deduction work.

While this group waited in line for technique deduction, Li Fan, out of curiosity, transmitted his voice to Xu Yuanxian: "Esteemed Chief Elder, please forgive my lack of insight, but these cultivators… do not seem to have particularly exceptional aptitude. Why is the Immortal Alliance treating them so favorably?"

The transmission did not avoid the other two guardians, who also looked curious. However, the only response was silence. Xu Yuanxian said nothing, as if he hadn't heard Li Fan's transmission at all. The two guardians wisely averted their gaze.

Li Fan did not ask further, and the ceremony in the hall fell into an awkward silence. Only when all sixteen people had collectively completed their technique deductions and were about to leave did Xu Yuanxian finally respond.

"I also want to know the answer to this question."

"But there are too many unknown things in the world; there is no need to understand everything. Just do your own job well."

"Since the Legate Council has made this decision, there must be a reason. We subordinates should simply follow orders."

The three guardians bowed their heads, indicating they had received the lesson. Only after Xu Yuanxian had completely left the Yan Fa Jue space did they dare to converse.

"The Chief Elder is truly as rigid as his reputation."

"Fellow Daoist Sun, you reacted so quickly. The Chief Elder likes it when you follow the rules, just like you did just now. If you impress him, in five hundred years, when you leave, he might pick you as the next Chief Elder." Hua Yueye teased.

Li Fan ignored their teasing and, following regulations, first recorded the special use of Yan Fa Jue and reported it. Then, he said faintly, "The Chief Elder of the Law Enforcement Hall has a job that is even more like imprisonment than ours. I have no interest in it."

"I have a lovely wife waiting for me at home."

Half true, half false, it made the two guardians laugh heartily. This incident was merely a small interlude during their supervision of Yan Fa Jue. Soon, the few of them forgot about it.

Of course, except for Li Fan. Because…

Among those sixteen people, there was a mole planted by the Saint Dynasty Great Qi in the Myriad Immortals Alliance. His name was Yang Fei. Li Fan knew him, but he didn't know Li Fan. However, this did not diminish Li Fan's sense of vigilance. The Immortal Alliance never did anything meaningless. These sixteen people, just after joining the Myriad Immortals Alliance, received such preferential treatment. It was hard not to make Li Fan suspect some conspiracy behind it.

"Could it be like the previous 'Chosen of the Immortals,' used as sacrifices to awaken the power of the statues left by the Legate Heavenly Venerate in various places? No, if they were sacrifices, they were destined to die. There would be no need to waste Yan Fa Jue's computational power…"

Li Fan keenly sensed the abnormality behind this. Meanwhile, in the underground secret chamber of the Sun family, his divine sense finally waited for the opportune moment.

Sun Luyuan entered the secret chamber again, his eyes bloodshot. With a struggling expression, he finally took out a small Heavenly Profound Mirror. Then, using his own vital blood, he nourished Sun Luyao within the Boundless Mirror while explaining, "The pressure from above is too great. Forgive me, brother."

"I originally thought I could resist death. But looking at the faces of the Sun family…"

Sun Luyao transformed into a black shadow, revealing his form, and according to Li Fan's divine sense instructions, comforted him, "Brother, I understand. It's okay, leave it to me."

Sun Luyuan trembled slightly, his fists clenched, his fingernails digging deep into his flesh.

At this moment, the information about the 'Saint Dynasty Great Qi' he had found earlier resurfaced in his mind.

"Perhaps, I can try to contact them."

"Being a dog for a lifetime also carries the risk of being beheaded at any moment. Perhaps this Great Qi can bring me some surprises?"

The Boundless Mirror pretended to search for information related to the Heavenly Profound Mirror's avatars within the Heavenly Profound Realm. In reality, it was trying to probe the reason why those sixteen cultivators were treated so favorably.

Chapter 1203: A Secret Meeting in the Sea of Stars

Star Sea Meeting in the Dark

This was clearly a top secret of the Myriad Immortals Alliance. It was hidden very deeply. Even though a part of the [Primordial Origin Square] Grand Array had been repaired, the Boundless Mirror still found it extremely difficult to search. It also had to be careful not to be discovered by the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

In the continuous search, the Boundless Mirror began to operate at an overload. The body of the mirror began to shake violently, and faint cracks appeared on its surface. Sun Luyuan's eyes turned red, and he almost put away the small Heavenly Profound Mirror several times. However, the firm resolve transmitted by Sun Luyao made him stop each time.

"Brother, I can still hold on."

"I've found some clues, I can't give up now!"

"Brother, I can do it!"

Listening to Sun Luyao's almost unbearable pained voice, Sun Luyuan's recent resolve became increasingly firm. Time seemed to pass extraordinarily slowly. Sun Luyuan's heart was torn and he felt like he was sitting on pins and needles. Besides worrying that his brother couldn't hold on and everything would be destroyed, he was also worried about being discovered by the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Finally, the Boundless Mirror actively withdrew the devouring black light. The strange small mirror even lost its ability to float and fell to the ground with a clang. Sun Luyuan quickly took out backup vital blood to replenish it. After a while, the Boundless Mirror trembled and recovered a little.

"How is it…" Sun Luyuan even dared not ask.

"Brother, I have brought back honor to your name."

Fortunately, his brother did not disappoint him. The moment he heard these four words, Sun Luyuan felt relieved. After examining the top-secret information his brother had gathered, his expression changed repeatedly.

"Fu's suspicions were correct. Cang has already been controlled."

"Weidu..."

"It seems that the internal situation of the mirror handlers is more complicated than we imagined."

Sun Luyao's black shadow said weakly, "Brother, our Sun family is too weak. With the slightest carelessness, we will be torn to pieces."

"Don't worry. I'll handle it from now on." Sun Luyuan said in a deep voice.

"Also, Brother. Can you leave the small Heavenly Profound Mirror here this time?" Just as he was about to leave, Sun Luyao suddenly said this.

Sun Luyuan couldn't help but hesitate.

"Don't worry, Brother. I haven't lost control. In fact, after several recent extreme explorations, I don't know why my control over the Boundless Mirror has deepened even further. I want to try a few more times when I have the energy. It will be more skillful in the future..."

Finally, Sun Luyuan was persuaded by his brother's sincere words. Moreover, his condition was indeed much better than when he had lost control after exploring before. Therefore, after repeatedly cautioning him, he still left the small Heavenly Profound Mirror behind.

Not long after Sun Luyuan hurriedly left.

A phantom image floated out from the Boundless Mirror and entered the small Heavenly Profound Mirror. A moment later, beams of light flickered continuously, and a large amount of spirit-nourishing materials were purchased. Li Fan's divine sense greedily devoured them, and his originally weak condition quickly reversed. With his Heavenly Profound Mirror origin, he could completely steal a large amount of resources through the small mirror without anyone noticing.

At this moment, Sun Luyao's figure also floated out. Looking at Li Fan, he was filled with fear. These spirit-nourishing treasures were useless to him. But the casual guidance from this lord could make his fusion with the Boundless Mirror go more smoothly. He knew that this was something he and his brother had spent painstaking efforts on for hundreds of years without success. The terrifying nature of this lord was beyond doubt. In Sun Luyao's eyes, he was far more terrifying than any mirror handler, and his surrender seemed natural.

"Brother, you can understand my actions, right?" Sun Luyao thought silently to himself. The pretense of pain in front of Sun Luyuan was naturally all an act. Although there were some twists and turns, it was a close call. However, he didn't understand the information that lord had painstakingly sought.

"Sixteen cultivators, summoned by the Legate, leaving Xuanhuang and going beyond the heavens."

To Sun Luyao, this seemed unremarkable. But to Li Fan, it had a completely different meaning. While his divine sense was slowly recovering, Li Fan was also contemplating this matter.

"The Legate is actually summoning cultivators to leave the Xuanhuang Realm? What is going on?"

"With his strength, even if these sixteen people were cultivated into Harmonious Dao cultivators in a short period, they would still be like ants."

"It's not like selecting from the existing Harmonious Dao cultivators of the Immortal Alliance."

Li Fan recalled the mole he had arranged, Yang Fei. He didn't seem to have anything special about him. Li Fan wasn't worried that Yang Fei would expose him if he encountered the Legate, because he himself didn't even know he was a spy for the Saint Dynasty Great Qi. Because Yang Fei himself was indeed an Immortal Alliance cultivator, but by chance, before participating in the Immortal Alliance's grand examination, he met a few friends who were good at studying the Immortal Alliance's grand examination and guessed a few questions correctly.

"It is certain that the Legate summoning these sixteen cultivators to go is related to the 'Reverberating Star Power' that is shaking the Xuanhuang Realm."

"It's just that I don't know what the Legate encountered that required these sixteen cultivators?"

"Moreover, the Reverberating Star Power near the Immortal Ruins has already disappeared. I don't know how these people left the Xuanhuang Realm?"

This matter was too secretive, and even the records in the Heavenly Profound Mirror were sparse.

"It's a pity that my Holy Embryo is on the other side of the star sea; otherwise, I could follow them and find out."

Thinking of this, Li Fan's thoughts suddenly paused. He suddenly thought that the Legate's purpose in the pitch-black sea of stars was to collect fragments of various immortal cultivation worlds. And the location of the Holy Embryo was the Sea of Relics, where all the remnants of immortal cultivators were gathered by the mysterious Reverberating Star Power.

"Since the relics are gathered, are the fragments of immortal cultivation worlds also gathered?"

"Besides the Sea of Relics, is there also a Sea of Broken Realms?"

On the other side of the star sea, Li Fan, the Holy Embryo hidden outside the Xuan Xian Zhou, suddenly opened his eyes. His gaze seemed to pierce through the endless ruins and darkness, looking deep into the Sea of Relics.

"Could it be that I am now very close to the Legate?" Li Fan couldn't help but think so.

"If my guess is correct, then if I wait here, I might encounter the sixteen cultivators of the Myriad Immortals Alliance."

"Thinking further, such a powerful being as the Legate, who has roamed the pitch-black sea of stars for thousands of years, must know about the immortal boat civilization hidden here. Perhaps they have already interacted."

"It's just that the immortal boat might not know the Legate's true identity."

Although based on the current information, the immortal boat civilization seemed extremely weak. However, having survived for thousands of years in the pitch-black sea of stars, and even having some knowledge of the power of True Immortal Runes… The peak power of the immortal boat was definitely not to be underestimated.

"Zhao Xian's strength is too low, and he knows too little about the past of the immortal boat."

"It seems that some accelerated growth is needed."

Chapter 1204: Heavenly Cripple and Earthly Defect Sea

The Broken Sea of Heaven and Earth

Drifting in the sea of stars for tens of thousands of years, even without a civilization collapse, the cultivation technique theories of the Xuan Xian Zhou had not progressed at all.

All the worlds they saw were destroyed, with only various destructive remnants of True Immortal Runes echoing in the sea of stars.

Relying on what was available, the Xuan Xian Zhou then placed all their hopes on the research of this great power.

As for other aspects… Compared to the Xuanhuang Realm, which had suffered so many calamities, it was inferior by more than a notch.

At the very least, in the extreme environment where multiple laws could not be cultivated together, the miraculous techniques born in the Xuanhuang Realm were all breathtaking existences in the eyes of the Xuan Xian Zhou cultivators.

With the foundation of the Myriad Immortals Alliance's cultivation technique library, Li Fan's divine sense quickly found the most suitable cultivation method for Zhao Xian.

Of course, from Zhao Xian's own perspective, this was part of the vast number of techniques deduced by the Academy of Laws through Yan Fa Jue in the future.

"Spirit God Harmonization Technique. A divine technique suitable for cultivators to practice even in an environment of extreme resource scarcity. It can achieve perfect coordination of divine sense and spiritual power. Whichever side is stronger can be converted to the weaker side."

"Within the academy, the spiritual power provided is extremely limited. It's at its limit for me to advance to Golden Core. To go further is impossible. However, I can use secret methods that increase divine sense to drive the increase of spiritual power…"

"In the academy's exchange list, the value of the items needed to cast secret techniques is far less than spirit stones."

Zhao Xian, who was troubled by hitting a bottleneck, suddenly had an inspiration and recalled more from that future dream.

In his excitement, he immediately spent all his accumulated contributions over the years to exchange for the materials needed to refine his divine sense.

Black God Gel, Red Ancient Sap, Spirit Nourishing Amber… These common spiritual sense-calming sundries in the immortal boat, under Zhao Xian's fiery refining, melted into a clear liquid.

Then, like a whale swallowing water, it continuously entered his sea of consciousness.

The scorching heatwave almost instantly incinerated Zhao Xian's divine sense.

After a brief blankness of consciousness, Zhao Xian found that he had actually adapted to this heat.

At the same time, the strength of his divine sense began to increase visibly.

"Truly a supreme and wondrous method!" Zhao Xian marveled in his heart.

However, Zhao Xian did not know that the reason his fragile late-stage Qi Refining divine sense was preserved during such intense refining was all thanks to Li Fan's divine sense.

In fact, most of the effects of the liquids refined from those treasures were also absorbed and refined by Li Fan's divine sense.

After all, Zhao Xian was only at the late stage of Qi Refining. Even a slight diversion was enough to steadily improve his divine sense.

When Zhao Xian woke up from his cultivation, he felt that the strength of his divine sense had almost quadrupled compared to before.

It had reached the level of the middle stage of Foundation Establishment.

Compared to this "vast" divine sense power, his spiritual power cultivation seemed a bit weak.

It felt like a giant fiddling with a toy body.

Zhao Xian suppressed his inner ecstasy and quickly circulated the [Spirit God Harmonization Technique].

An invisible grinding disc suddenly appeared in his sea of consciousness, crushing the power of his divine sense and turning it into pure power to nourish Zhao Xian's body.

Without absorbing any spiritual energy, Zhao Xian's cultivation advanced crazily at a terrifying speed.

Finally, after three days, Zhao Xian's divine sense and spiritual power were balanced at the early stage of Foundation Establishment.

"I've successfully established my foundation?" Zhao Xian looked at his hands in disbelief.

"The breakthrough was too easy, I didn't feel any inner demons or bottlenecks as my master and seniors in the academy described."

"After establishing my foundation, my authority in the academy has also increased significantly. I can exchange for more resources, and my cultivation will probably be faster than before…"

After all, he was just a young boy, and Zhao Xian couldn't help but feel excited imagining the future.

Finally, the scene of the immortal boat's demise in that future dream brought him back to reality.

"The road ahead is long, and I still have a long way to go. I cannot be arrogant."

Zhao Xian was contemplating how to make greater use of his "foreknowledge" to achieve rapid advancement in status.

Meanwhile, Li Fan's divine sense was reminiscing about the scene of Zhao Xian's breakthrough.

Zhao Xian had not truly encountered any obstacles to his breakthrough; it was Li Fan who had blocked them.

"That fluctuation that appeared out of nowhere, directly targeting the heart."

"It's not True Immortal Runes. It's the Heavenly Dao of the sea of stars…"

At this moment, Li Fan, the Holy Embryo outside the Xuan Xian Zhou, suddenly had a feeling.

His body directly came into contact with this space full of deathly silence.

During the process of crossing the pitch-black sea of stars, the Holy Embryo Li Fan had already understood that this pitch-black sea of stars actually shared the same basic principles with the Xuanhuang Realm.

Its upper limit was even slightly higher than the Xuanhuang Realm's.

The sword path that had reached its limit in the Xuanhuang Realm had unknowingly broken through its original bottleneck and reached a new height during his travels through the sea of stars.

And the bottleneck that manifested as [Heavenly Calamity] in the Xuanhuang Realm had another form of existence in this pitch-black sea of stars.

"Persuading people to return to the Dao, leading to despair. A breakthrough at the peak of Qi Refining actually possesses such power. If I hadn't experienced too much and my will was incomparably resilient…"

"I might have had to use the Immortal Heart Curse to resolve it."

The Holy Embryo Li Fan inwardly trembled.

In the illusions shrouded by that invisible fluctuation, the Holy Embryo Li Fan seemed to see himself successfully breaking through, then enduring countless hardships, only to ultimately die from various calamities.

No matter how hard he tried, he could not escape the end of failure.

"It's better to return to the Dao, return to the Dao..."

The obsession echoed like a demonic sound, dissuading him from cultivating.

"This Heavenly Dao of the pitch-black sea of stars is quite interesting. It somewhat resembles the ancient inner demons recorded in the Xuanhuang Realm's classics."

"From a single point, one can see the whole. Although this sea of stars has been ravaged by True Immortal Runes, its basic underlying operations are still intact."

The Holy Embryo Li Fan pondered continuously, his vision suddenly broadened, as if he saw a world even wider than the Xuanhuang Realm, a world outside the Xuanhuang.

Even though this world was broken and incomplete, it brought Li Fan new ideas for comprehending the principles of the world.

He once again savored the contents of the Heavenly Physician's [Heaven Mending Record].

"If the situation in the Xuanhuang Realm is a stitched-together monster suffering from incurable diseases and being reanimated by someone else, then this pitch-black sea of stars is a world that has long since died, and most of its body has been crushed by immense force, with only a few fragmented limbs remaining…"

"The Xuanhuang Realm can still be saved, but this pitch-black sea of stars is completely beyond hope."

"Of course, this is from the perspective of the Heavenly Physician's [Heaven Mending Record] at the time."

Chapter 1205: Breaking Through the Star Sea by Force

Breaking Through the Star Sea Dao with Force

"The only thing that can be done is to dissect and analyze these world fragments, and perhaps deduce and restore the appearance of this pitch-black sea of stars when it was alive."

"However, after all, it is an existence several levels higher than the ordinary immortal cultivation worlds of Xuanhuang. Even its corpse can bring immense benefits."

The aura on the Holy Embryo Li Fan's body suddenly changed. It was like magma erupting violently. His aura, already at the peak of the Nascent Soul stage, instantly expanded several times.

Unfortunately, the Holy Embryo was still unable to escape the restriction between the avatar and the main body. It was as if an invisible chain was brutally suppressing the surging aura.

The Holy Embryo Li Fan grunted, actually spitting out a mouthful of blood. Countless black cracks appeared in the small world evolved by the black sword within his body, as if it would be destroyed at any moment.

But the Holy Embryo Li Fan's eyes were filled with excitement. "Heaven and Earth are broken, the Dao principles are weakened."

"As expected, in this pitch-black sea of stars, the avatar can potentially surpass the main body in realm!"

The Holy Embryo Li Fan savored the impact of the soaring power. It was like a brute force savagely breaking through the shackles of heaven and earth.

"I am still lacking the fundamental driving force for breaking through. The incomplete Dao has led to backlash."

"If I had accumulated more, I could have broken through that shackle in one go."

Li Fan suddenly thought of the scene when his avatar forcefully broke through the [Heavenly Calamity] bottleneck while practicing the Heaven-Swallowing and Earth-Devouring Great Technique.

"This is called [Breaking Dao with Force]. In a normal great world, without being a True Immortal, one does not possess such powerful strength. But the pitch-black sea of stars is broken and incomplete, greatly lowering the requirements."

"After my avatar forcefully broke through the bottleneck of Heavenly Calamity before, it was counterattacked by the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao with that giant palm. In this pitch-black sea of stars, even this kind of backlash might not descend."

The Holy Embryo Li Fan, like Zhao Xian just now, felt a sense of sudden enlightenment and joy.

"From one to ten thousand. Since this inherent Dao principle can be broken, can others also be achieved?"

"A whale falls, and all things come to life. The death of the sea of stars may be an unparalleled opportunity for the surviving cultivators."

"The Legate's performance of strength far exceeding ordinary cultivators, apart from the new method cultivators of the entire Xuanhuang Realm being his foundation, is likely related to this."

"Having stayed in the sea of stars for ten thousand years, he is probably infinitely close to becoming a legend among Immortals."

…

The insights of the Holy Embryo in the pitch-black sea of stars had a great impact on Li Fan's main body as well. The discovery that the broken and incomplete great world of the sea of stars was beneficial to cultivators caused his aura to become slightly unstable.

This attracted the attention of Hua Yueye and Zhang Xu, two Harmonious Dao elders.

"Fellow Daoist Sun?"

"It's nothing, just thinking about my beloved wife at home, my mind wandered." Li Fan said with some shame.

The two guardians looked at him strangely and nodded in understanding.

Stabilizing his mind, Li Fan's main body forcibly suppressed the urge to rush out of the Xuanhuang Realm immediately.

"Opportunities and crises always coexist."

"Although the current pitch-black sea of stars is a sacred land for cultivation, it is undoubtedly fraught with danger."

"If it weren't for the Holy Embryo being a Foundation Establishment of Heaven's Wonder, it would have likely perished halfway. Facing the strange phenomena in the sea of stars, even my Five Elements Great Cave Heaven's evolved world couldn't last long."

The intangible void in the dark space, and the deadly black plague… Neither of them could be dealt with by the current Li Fan.

"It's the same to gain insights by borrowing the Holy Embryo's perception." Li Fan comforted himself.

"The sixteen Harmonious Dao cultivators of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, if they leave the Xuanhuang Realm, should also be able to gradually discover this secret."

"It's just that I don't know if they can still come back alive?" Li Fan was pessimistic about the fate of these sixteen people.

In the eyes of the Legate, the cultivators of the Xuanhuang Realm were definitely mere tools. This summoning should not escape that fate.

"However, I can find a way to learn the method of leaving the Xuanhuang Realm without Reverberating Star Power."

"The appearance of Reverberating Star Power in this lifetime was purely accidental. There is no guarantee that it can be replicated in the future. Since I already know the importance of the pitch-black sea of stars, how can I miss it?"

"Even if it's a top-secret at this moment and cannot be investigated, after a few decades, or when the Saint Dynasty Great Qi threatens the Myriad Immortals Alliance and they go to war, such secrets will be ignored and not difficult to inquire about."

…

Despite saying so, Li Fan kept a close eye on these sixteen people. Through the small Heavenly Profound Mirror, the divine sense left in the Sun family could stably maintain its form.

The recovery of the divine sense's strength, along with Sun Luyao in the Boundless Mirror, grew stronger and stronger, and their fusion with the Boundless Mirror became more and more evident.

One day, while peeking into the Heavenly Profound Mirror, Sun Luyao suddenly mustered the courage to say to Li Fan, "Senior, I seem to have sensed the location of another fragment of the Boundless Mirror again."

"Perhaps after absorbing it, the Boundless Mirror's abilities will be further enhanced." The Sun brothers had almost searched the entire territory of the Myriad Immortals Alliance and found that fragment, which indeed brought about a qualitative change in the Boundless Mirror. If it could recover more, it might truly bring surprises to Li Fan.

However, Li Fan's divine sense pretended not to hear. He patiently finished peeking into the Heavenly Profound Mirror, and still found no information about the sixteen people summoned by the Legate.

Then, he coldly looked at Sun Luyao, "What location?"

Sun Luyao cautiously transmitted the sensed information.

"Oh?" Li Fan's divine sense was somewhat surprised after seeing the location Sun Luyao pointed out. It was in the Hundred Stone Grotto-Heaven, located on the border of Shilin Prefecture. The ruins of the Heavenly Mystery Sect and the entrance to the Spiritual Wood Realm were all in these underground caves.

"I understand." Li Fan's divine sense replied faintly, without showing any intention to search for it.

Sun Luyao dared not ask further.

Seven days later, Sun Luyuan returned to the secret chamber. With Li Fan's permission, Sun Luyao eagerly repeated the matter. Unlike Li Fan's indifference, Sun Luyuan was overjoyed. "If we can find another fragment, perhaps you won't have to suffer so much!"

Sun Luyao nodded in agreement.

"By the way, Brother, what was Old Man Fu's reaction after he knew about the Heavenly Profound Mirror's avatar?" Sun Luyao asked again.

Sun Luyuan frowned upon hearing this: "The Heavenly Profound Mirror giving birth to a human avatar is a major event that needs to be handled cautiously. He has no reaction for the time being, which I can understand. However, it's strange that I haven't been able to contact him since our last meeting."

"Can't contact him?"

"Not only Fu, but I can't even enter the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters temporarily. It seems that something extremely important is happening."

Chapter 1206: Ancient Immeasurable Obscured

The Ancient Primordial Dust

"It's truly strange that even an urgent matter like the Heavenly Profound Mirror potentially escaping as a human avatar is being shelved..."

"If I couldn't contact the outside world unilaterally, I would almost think the Immortal Alliance had fallen." Sun Luyuan frowned and said.

Sun Luyao looked surprised at this point: "Is that so? I didn't detect anything related to that in the Heavenly Profound Mirror."

The two brothers looked at each other. Sun Luyao said uncertainly: "I don't know if my peeking failed, or if the Myriad Immortals Alliance is even hiding this matter from the Heavenly Profound Mirror?"

"The Immortal Alliance headquarters is a separate space within the Heavenly Profound Mirror. If they want to shield the Heavenly Profound Mirror's perception, it would likely require the combined efforts of the Council of Legates and the Mirror Master..." Sun Luyuan's expression became serious, as if he remembered something.

"The Immortal Alliance headquarters is inside the Heavenly Profound Mirror?" Sun Luyao was surprised, as he wasn't aware of this.

Sun Luyuan came back to his senses and nodded, but didn't explain further.

"It's a good thing Old Man Fu can't get away. It's a perfect opportunity for us to go and find that fragment of the Boundless Mirror you sensed."

"Okay, Brother." Sun Luyao naturally had no objections to this.

"I originally wanted to take you to the [Vital Blood Pool] for nourishment during this rare interval. We can only do it when we return." Sun Luyuan shook his head slightly.

The Vital Blood Pool was a secret place of the Sun family, containing the vital blood donated by the direct descendants of the family. Refined with secret methods, its effects were even better than that of Sun Luyuan, a close relative, donating vital blood. However, collecting vital blood from family disciples could not be done too frequently, otherwise, it would definitely arouse suspicion. Therefore, it took a considerable amount of time to accumulate enough nourishment.

Sun Luyao had tasted it a few times before and indeed felt some effect.

But…

"Compared to the methods of our ancestors, it's far inferior."

The vital blood nourishment of the family ultimately strengthened the power of Sun Luyao's remnant soul. The stronger one's own power, the easier it was to erode the Boundless Mirror. As for Li Fan, he directly showed him the method of controlling the Boundless Mirror. Not only did he no longer need brute force to erode it, but even the damaged and disordered Boundless Mirror showed signs of slow recovery, making him no longer feel the previous pain when facing it.

Although he thought this in his heart, he still had to maintain appearances. So he pretended to look somewhat regretful.

Sun Luyuan saw this and comforted him, "Let's see if this trip outside is successful. If we return quickly, there will still be plenty of time."

After saying this, Sun Luyuan returned and made some preparations. When he reappeared in the secret chamber, he had already taken the form of a younger generation of the Sun family, Sun Luyuan's usual disguise.

"Let's go."

Putting the Boundless Mirror into his 怀 (huái, embrace/bosom), Sun Luyuan quietly left the Sun family and headed for Shilin Prefecture.

Perhaps due to its damage and instability, the Boundless Mirror could not use teleportation formations and could only rely on physical flight. Fortunately, this distance was not too far for a Harmonious Dao cultivator, and they soon arrived at the entrance of the Hundred Stone Grotto-Heaven.

According to Sun Luyao's perception, they continuously delved into the underground caves. When they encountered a dead end, they forcefully broke through, getting closer and closer to their destination.

"This damned place." But the deeper they went, the harder the cave walls became, and Sun Luyuan even began to struggle.

"Brother, we're almost there." Sun Luyao sensed the familiar aura ahead and couldn't help but feel excited.

Perhaps it was because he had been underground for too long and his perception was affected. Only when he truly arrived here did he realize that this fragment might be larger than he had imagined.

"Huh?! Someone's behind us?" Just as they were separated by a wall from the Boundless Mirror fragment, Sun Luyuan's expression changed, and he stopped.

"I was actually tracked." Sun Luyuan reacted quickly and changed his direction of travel, continuing to delve deeper into the cave. He accelerated suddenly, his figure instantly disappearing into the maze-like passages.

Two cultivators in blue robes appeared, their expressions grim.

"Damn it, he discovered us."

"It seems this Sun Luyuan's cultivation has improved again."

"It's fine, we've sealed the entrance. He can't escape."

……

However, these two didn't know that much deeper in the cave, Sun Luyuan had already seen their actions through the Boundless Mirror.

"Tian Quan, the Chen family." Sun Luyuan coldly snorted. He had long known about the various petty tricks of the Chen family of the Medicine Hall, who had been coveting the Boundless Mirror. But the other party still had some foundation. Before they took concrete action, there was no reason to attack.

"They actually came to our doorstep, giving me an opportunity." A plan instantly formed in Sun Luyuan's mind. He revealed his aura, luring the two Chen family members deeper underground. Then, he quietly hid and quickly returned to the location of the Boundless Mirror fragment.

Boom!

He opened a sealed cave, and Sun Luyuan quickly located the fragment. This seemed to be the ruins of an ancient sect, and the Boundless Mirror fragment was actually integrated into another mirror-like magic treasure. It was a pity that this sect had long since perished, and this mirror-like magic treasure was covered in dust, buried underground for thousands of years.

Knowing that this place was not suitable for lingering, Sun Luyuan didn't bother to examine it closely and put it away. Then, he no longer concealed himself, even burning his vital blood. His strength exploded in an instant. In the blink of an eye, he had rushed to the exit of the Hundred Stone Grotto-Heaven. The two cultivators guarding the exit were caught off guard and couldn't resist. They actually let Sun Luyuan charge out.

"Chen family! If I don't get revenge, I'm not a man!" Although he wasn't injured, Sun Luyuan suddenly spat out a mouthful of blood, and his aura quickly weakened. His voice, like thunder, echoed in the sky above Shilin Prefecture for a long time.

Then, Sun Luyuan transformed into a beam of light and flew towards the center of the Immortal Alliance. He left behind two somewhat bewildered Chen family cultivators. When the two Harmonious Dao cultivators, who had been lured away, finally arrived, they realized what had happened.

"It's bad." The four of them looked at each other, their faces gloomy. Since the matter had been exposed, there was no way to pursue him openly.

"The operation failed, and the Sun family will likely completely break ties with us. Let's go back quickly to discuss how to deal with it."

"Hmph, so be it. We don't want this immortal artifact anymore. We'll make this matter public. I don't believe that their small Sun family can protect this immortal artifact!"

The four members of the Chen family disappeared one after another.

In Shilin Prefecture, the furious roar of Sun Luyuan just now gradually sparked discussions among the people. Meanwhile, Sun Luyuan had already returned home. He went directly to the underground secret chamber and took out the Boundless Mirror.

Today is only one chapter. Returning from a business trip is too tiring.

(End of this chapter)

Chapter 1207: Immortal Disaster Wind Tribulation Appears

Disaster of Immortal Tribulation Appears

On the way, Sun Luyuan could clearly feel the restless stirring of the Boundless Mirror in his arms, as well as his brother Sun Luyao's familiar roar of losing control. He suppressed it forcefully until they returned safely before releasing it.

"Brother, quickly give it to me! I can't stand it anymore!" The mirror surface shook violently, and Sun Luyao's smoke-like black shadow seemed to be blown by a hurricane, constantly distorting and flickering.

"Calm down!" Sun Luyuan lowered his voice and skillfully took out a drop of his vital blood, alleviating his brother's frenzy.

Then, he took out the mirror taken from the ruins of the Hundred Stone Grotto-Heaven. The same origin aura indicated that the main body of the mirror was indeed a fragment of the Boundless Mirror, but it had been reforged into a separate magic treasure.

Sun Luyuan carefully broke the restrictions on the mirror before throwing it to his brother.

With the limitations removed, the dark, greedy shadow floated above the mirror. Dark beams of light spewed from Sun Luyao's mouth, corroding this ancient treasure.

As this mirror slowly disappeared into the black light, the Boundless Mirror, where Sun Luyao's possession resided, began to change at a visible speed. The marks of time slowly disappeared, and the ancient feeling vanished, replaced by a sense of vicissitude after experiencing hardships.

The surface of the Boundless Mirror frequently emanated a soul-stirring luster, causing even Sun Luyuan to inwardly tremble. "Is this the power of an immortal artifact…" he mused, eagerly anticipating his brother's performance after waking from his 吞噬 (tūnshì, devouring/swallowing).

Meanwhile, Li Fan, the divine sense hidden within the Boundless Mirror, could more directly witness the transformation of the Boundless Mirror. Or rather, its restoration.

The [Boundless, Primordial Square Visible] Grand Array, which had many deficiencies, was slowly being replenished. As if it had a core, an indescribable miraculous power flowed out from the formation like a gentle stream, nourishing the old body of the Boundless Mirror. This was also the reason why, in the eyes of outsiders, the immortal artifact was renewed in the blink of an eye.

Along with it, Li Fan's divine sense also benefited, transforming from a mere divine sense into a soul. Li Fan even had a feeling that if he continued to absorb the energy from the Boundless Mirror, his divine sense could eventually become stronger than his main body's soul.

After all, Li Fan had reached his current realm step by step, with an extremely solid foundation. Not to mention the theoretical accumulation from multiple reincarnations, even the Five Elements Great Cave Heaven and the Xuanhuang Birth and Death Transformation were the essences of the Xuanhuang Realm. The peak Harmonious Dao realm built on this foundation could be matched by the energy within this broken mirror!

Even if it was only in terms of soul, it greatly shocked Li Fan. He echoed Sun Luyuan's exclamation: "Is this the power of an immortal artifact?"

The energy emerging from the Boundless Mirror seemed like order, like life.

However, just as Li Fan thought it would completely repair the Boundless Mirror, the Boundless Mirror uncontrollably fell to the ground.

The mirror surface projected a mass of light and shadow, shrouding the underground secret chamber. The images flashed rapidly. The scenes it predicted made both Sun Luyuan and Li Fan's hearts tremble.

The peaceful Xuanhuang continent was engulfed by war. Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators were fighting against another unknown force. Everywhere arrows of light flew, causing earth-shattering explosions wherever they struck.

A golden giant was locked in a fierce battle with a black-haired, naked man. Even the white mist barrier between heaven and earth distorted and broke under the impact of their power.

Even more shocking was that on this battlefield, there was a figure standing above everyone, dressed in black imperial robes, with an unidentifiable face. Opposite him, another figure was equally blurry.

Boom! As if pushed to its limit, the projected image of the Boundless Mirror instantaneously became distorted and converged into one point. Then, a burst of intense white light erupted. After the light disappeared, there was only darkness and silence.

Hiss! The surface of the Boundless Mirror, which had just recovered somewhat, once again appeared with a crack. Sun Luyao let out a scream, and his shadowy black form was forcibly sucked back into the mirror.

"Brother!" Sun Luyuan instantly snapped back from his shock, his expression changing, and he rushed to pick up the Boundless Mirror. However, the moment his hand touched it, it felt as if it had been scalded by a fierce flame, and he quickly retracted it.

Sun Luyuan looked solemnly at his outstretched right hand. In such a short time, it seemed to have experienced thousands of years. His flesh withered, and wrinkles appeared. Not only his physical body. Sun Luyuan felt that a part of his soul had also genuinely experienced the passage of time and could no longer return to its original state.

Just a careless touch had this effect, let alone Li Fan's divine sense within the Boundless Mirror. Earlier, when he saw the future of the Xuanhuang Realm spontaneously deduced within the Boundless Mirror, Li Fan, despite his shock, wanted to examine it closely. But then, a fatal sense of crisis suddenly arose within him, making him completely disregard these matters.

This destructive power was hidden in the deepest part of the Boundless Mirror. Even Li Fan's divine sense, who had basically mastered it, had not noticed it at all before it erupted. And it came so swiftly and explosively. It was as if it could erode time itself.

The Boundless Mirror, which had just recovered some energy after absorbing the fragment, instantly experienced countless tribulations of wind and frost, and once again became dilapidated. And the core of the Boundless Mirror, the Primordial Square array, was like being blown by a strong wind. Some of its complete structures became damaged again.

Li Fan's divine sense was naturally unable to escape this fate. Already a remnant, it quickly became like a candle in the wind, about to completely dissipate. Fortunately, firstly, he had already refined the Boundless Mirror in large part through the array-refining method, and by residing within the mirror, he had gained a bit more resistance with the mirror's power. Secondly, the moment he realized his divine sense was about to perish, Li Fan instinctively chanted the Xuanhuang Immortal Heart Curse. Although it couldn't recover what was lost, it greatly slowed down the dissipation of his divine sense in this storm.

After persevering for a long time, the terrifying calamity within the Boundless Mirror finally slowly subsided. Li Fan sensed that it hadn't disappeared, but had returned to the depths of the Boundless Mirror, lying dormant once more.

At this time, Sun Luyuan's anxious voice slowly came. "Brother, what happened to you?" However, Sun Luyao, due to severe damage, was too weak to respond.

Seeing this, Sun Luyuan reacted quickly. He immediately took the Boundless Mirror into the Sun family's Vital Blood Pool. Although it was called the Vital Blood Pool, there was no foul smell of blood at all. Instead, it was filled with the fragrance of heavenly materials and earthly treasures. The pool water was not blood-red, but like a dreamlike rainbow, like flowing starlight from the heavens.

Immersed in it, Li Fan, this aging divine sense, finally felt relieved.

"Why was it consumed so quickly?" Sun Luyuan, seeing the speed at which the Vital Blood Pool water changed color, was shocked. However, he gritted his teeth and left, clearly going to gather vital blood again.

Chapter 1208: Hidden Dangers in the Black and Yellow Realm

The Peril Within Xuanhuang

Having survived the ordeal, Li Fan began to recall the terrifying power within the Boundless Mirror from moments ago.

"Is this the reason the Boundless Mirror was damaged?"

"It felt even more potent than those True Immortal Runes I've encountered."

"Though all I've seen so far are imitations of True Immortal Runes, the remnants in the Boundless Mirror are merely residual echoes."

"Could the tribulations of the Immortal Realm be related to this?"

Despite his myriad curiosities, Li Fan had no intention of delving deeper for the moment. Any existence capable of destroying an Immortal Realm was far beyond his current capabilities.

"It only left traces within the Boundless Mirror. Even if induced and released, it would at most cover the area of a single city."

"It might only be useful at critical junctures," Li Fan mused.

"It's no wonder an esteemed Immortal Artifact ended up being possessed by the remnant soul of a Foundation Establishment cultivator. That obliterating storm was too terrifying."

"An Immortal Artifact that originally belonged to the Boundless Sect, located in the Xuanhuang Realm, underwent such a transformation..."

"Doesn't that imply this calamity occurred within the Xuanhuang Realm?"

"If residual waves could damage an Immortal Artifact, it's impossible for it to have occurred without leaving any trace."

Li Fan's thoughts paused. He suddenly recalled two major events that had altered the course of Xuanhuang Realm's history, which might be related. The first was the inexplicable disappearance of Xuanyuan Hong, the King of Xuanhuang. The second was the disappearance of the six Longevity Realm experts who had besieged the then Harmonious Dao cultivator, the Law Transmitter.

"The cultivation of these individuals had reached the pinnacle of their era."

"In the Xuanhuang Realm, ordinary means could not harm them. Unless..." Li Fan's heart stirred.

"A power that surpassed the mundane."

Li Fan then recalled Grand Master Tiandu, the master of the Taiyan Sect, who had arrived in the Xuanhuang Realm after the great calamity. After being injured, he had remained in Daoyuan Province without moving.

"Was his arrival back then truly a coincidence?"

At this moment, Li Fan couldn't help but be filled with deep suspicion. This matter also served as a stark warning to Li Fan. Even though his perspective had expanded beyond the Xuanhuang Realm to the ends of the star sea, there were still existences within the Xuanhuang Realm that he could not fathom and were beyond his reach. He had to proceed with utmost caution in all his endeavors.

As his thoughts churned, Sun Luyuan returned in a hurry. He refined a large mass of vital blood and several other materials, adding them to the Vital Blood Pool. The pool water, which had dimmed somewhat, once again became radiant. Li Fan also paid attention to the condition of the Boundless Mirror. It had regressed almost to its state before absorbing the fragment. However, it was now slightly more complete, and Li Fan believed that after Sun Luyao awoke, his condition would improve to a certain extent. Moreover, Li Fan had also briefly glimpsed the more complete Primordial Square Array. While perfect restoration might be out of reach, minor repairs and mending should be feasible.

Three days later, Sun Luyao, the spirit of the Boundless Mirror, finally awoke from his brief slumber.

"Brother, I need some things." After relaying the materials needed to repair the array, he fell unconscious again. Sun Luyuan looked at the list of materials provided by his brother and hurried to gather them.

During this time, fearing retaliation from Sun Luyuan, the Chen family of the Medicine Hall had been closely monitoring Sun Luyuan's movements. However, Sun Luyuan seemed to have forgotten about this, coming and going as if busy with some urgent matter. This left the Chen family perplexed. Furthermore, their backer, the Law Transmitter Cang, at the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters, had been unreachable. Thus, the Chen family chose to wait and see.

With Sun Luyuan's unsparing efforts in collecting the materials, the required supplies were quickly assembled. What appeared to be Sun Luyao absorbing them was in fact Li Fan's divine sense acting remotely. As the fragmented core of the array was restored, the condition of the Boundless Mirror slowly stabilized.

Upon hearing about his brother's experience, Sun Luyuan's brow furrowed.

"Brother, do you remember the ancient ruins where we first found this mirror?" Sun Luyao was slightly taken aback.

"I initially thought that ruin was merely an ancient relic that had weathered the passage of time. But with you saying so..." Sun Luyuan's expression turned grim. "It seems that place was destroyed by the obliterating storm within the mirror..."

"Perhaps it was precisely because of its previous release that we brothers had an opportunity. Otherwise, with our cultivation at the time, how could we have subdued this mirror." Sun Luyao recalled the past and slowly started to understand.

"That's possible. I also remember that there was almost nothing of value in the ruins. The only item recognized by the Heavenly Profound Mirror received very low contribution points for recycling..."

"Rest assured and recover. I will go back to that ancient ruin in some time to investigate. The entrance there is extremely well-hidden, and since it's only a ruin, not much should have changed over the years. Perhaps there will be some discoveries," Sun Luyuan said in a deep voice.

"Brother, be careful," Sun Luyao cautioned without objection.

"And the Chen family..." Sun Luyuan suddenly snorted coldly. He recalled the scenes inexplicably deduced by the Boundless Mirror earlier.

"The force locked in a fierce battle with the Myriad Immortals Alliance seemed to be the Great Qi Dynasty that you investigated earlier."

"This suggests that the Heavenly Profound Mirror's predictions have some basis."

"Both wondrous artifacts have made such predictions..."

"It seems it's time to try and make contact with them." Sun Luyuan naturally would not approach them directly at first. After all, the Great Qi Dynasty had not yet openly opposed the Myriad Immortals Alliance. He would have his confidant investigate first before making further decisions.

Comparatively, the Boundless Mirror, once believed to be a treasure, had now become a potential disaster waiting to erupt, causing Sun Luyuan greater worry. His brother had become the spirit of the Boundless Mirror and certainly could not abandon it.

After making some preparations, Sun Luyuan planned to return to the ruins from that year. The encounter at the Hundred Stone Grotto-Heaven had made Sun Luyuan aware that the Chen family was still secretly monitoring him. To avoid unnecessary trouble, Sun Luyuan directly contacted an old friend.

Ji Hongdao!

"Old Ji, I need your help with something..." Sun Luyuan contacted him via spiritual talisman. Soon, Ji Hongdao arrived at the Sun family's doorstep.

"Hahaha, Old Sun, I finally get to repay the favor you owed me back then," Ji Hongdao laughed heartily. "I heard you had a conflict with the Medicine Hall's Chen family recently?" he asked, lowering his voice as they entered the house.

"Yes, the treasure that Lu Yao resides in somehow became known to the Chen family," Sun Luyuan replied truthfully. Ji Hongdao understood.

"Don't worry, although they have the support of a Law Transmitter, and you have the Mirror Master backing you."

"Since their actions were exposed this time, they won't dare to act rashly again in a short period."

Sun Luyuan said solemnly, "Villains are at their end; one must be cautious. I will trouble you during this outing."

Chapter 1209: The Immortal Sect Hidden Underground

Underground Immortal Sect

Yi Shu gradually recovered from his shock but still did not express his stance. However, his actions had already changed. Originally, he had planned to observe for a while and then return. Now, he requested Sun Erlang to allow him to stay for a long period of observation.

Sun Erlang looked troubled: "I cannot make this decision on my own; I need to seek instructions from Master."

Yi Shu nodded: "I believe your Master will agree."
