As expected, the Faceless Sacred Emperor agreed to the Taiyan Sect's request to stay, but with a condition.

"Help the cultivators in the Saint Dynasty Great Qi grow rapidly through 'simulation'?" Yi Shu hesitated for a moment.

"Master said that even if the Taiyan Sect did not assist, he had other methods, though they would be more troublesome. The core of the Taiyan Sect is their derivation of the Xuanhuang's future. As long as there is no definitive outcome, Master also agrees to the Taiyan Sect maintaining a certain degree of neutrality. Consider it a form of transaction," Sun Erlang repeated Li Ping's words verbatim.

Yi Shu fell silent for a moment, and after deliberation between the Taiyan Sect and the Dao Transformation Stone Mother, they finally agreed. For the Taiyan Sect, a few more simulations were merely the utilization of idle computational power, but it could open up another path for the future, which was undoubtedly a worthwhile deal. It was like when some cultivators chose to flee before the calamity descended; the Ten Immortal Sects never placed all their hopes on a single option.

From then on, the Saint Dynasty Great Qi gained an observer. Besides the Sacred Emperor's Seat and the place where the You Clan resided, and the Xuanhuang Realm Fishing Pond, Yi Shu could observe freely without any constraints.

Li Ping was not worried about this. With the fortune of the Saint Dynasty bestowed upon him, coupled with the continuous improvement of the Myriad Spirits Grand Formation, Yi Shu's every move was under his control. Even Yi Shu's life and death were within his thoughts.

Meanwhile, in the distant Xuanhuang Realm, someone was already plotting against the Taiyan Sect.

"Although I have no intention of harming others, I must leave a fallback plan."

"The Taiyan Sect has abandoned their physical realities and collectively exists within the Dao Transformation Stone Mother. Information is immortal, which is truly remarkable. Even when Immortal Experts from the Immortal Ruins wield destructive power, they can escape that terrifying calamity. However…"

"As the saying goes, each trade has its specialty!"

In the Yan Fa Jue space, Li Fan appeared to be meditating with his eyes closed. In reality, his thoughts were constantly churning. Information immortality rendered physical means and even ordinary immortal techniques ineffective. However, data pollution might be effective.

As far as Li Fan knew, among the current circulating lineages in the Xuanhuang Realm, such a method did not exist. His idea stemmed from the mysterious 'Primordial Origin Spirit Grand Array.' A composite of nine Immortal-grade Grand Arrays, its power was unimaginable, capable of recreating earth, fire, water, and wind in the void and creating a new world.

Fortunately, with the 'End Dissolution Disc,' and through various coincidences, Li Fan had initially mastered three of them: 'Xuanji, Myriad Spirits Returning to Numbers,' 'Arid Fall, Void Chamber Blooming Flowers,' and 'Boundless, Primordial Seen Square.' Among them, the Xuanji, Myriad Spirits Returning to Numbers Grand Array possessed the miraculous ability to digitize everything within the array's coverage and transform it at will.

"Although it is only theoretical, the materials required to set up the array are fundamentally unobtainable. Thankfully, the Taiyan Sect also lacks physical form, making

Chapter 1210: Bone of the Archmage

The Arch-Mage's Bones

The sect of Primordial Beginning, like the Heavenly Sword and the Great Dao Sect, was once one of the Ten Great Immortal Sects.

However, its presence was considerably weaker.

It had little contact within the Fallen Immortal Realm, and in the present era, relevant records were scarce.

It was as if the sect had suddenly vanished from the world.

Before this, Li Fan had only learned from Senior Stone Slab that the Five Elements Great Cave Heaven, which he used to achieve his Nascent Soul, was a creation of the Primordial Beginning Sect. He had not investigated them further since.

Unexpectedly, today, at a depth of three thousand zhang beneath a chasm, he discovered traces of the Primordial Beginning Sect.

But they were merely traces.

The entire ruin was deserted.

Except for a stone tablet in a collapsed building at the center of the ruins, faintly inscribed with the characters "Primordial Beginning," there was nothing else that indicated the grandeur of an ancient Great Immortal Sect.

"It seems the Primordial Beginning Sect didn't fare well."

After inquiring with Sun Luyao, he learned that this was indeed the ruin where they had discovered the Boundless Mirror previously.

However, at that time, they had only entered a small part of it.

Now, for reasons unknown, the formations separating different areas had vanished, revealing the true appearance of the entire Primordial Beginning Sect.

"Boundless Expansion, One Realm Visible!"

Li Fan's divine sense murmured.

Invisibly, the Boundless Mirror emitted a faint, undetectable light.

Instantly, it enveloped the entire Primordial Beginning Sect ruin.

Consequently, a complete map of the ruin instantly appeared in the Boundless Mirror.

It even showed which areas still had spiritual energy fluctuations, which had hidden secret chambers, and the danger levels of each area...

All this information was readily available.

All of this was accomplished by the Boundless Mirror under the nose of Ji Hongdao.

Yet, this formation master, who was among the top echelon of formation masters in the Myriad Immortals Alliance, was completely unaware.

Li Fan's mind recalled the scene from the 114th reincarnation, when he went to Cloud Sea to study formations in Tianyu Prefecture, and Ji Hongdao personally lectured to thousands of formation prodigies in the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

At that time, he felt that not only Ji Hongdao but even Huangfu Song's formation skill was beyond his reach.

However, after more than ten reincarnations, his formation skill had reached a level that Ji Hongdao could not comprehend.

"I advanced continuously in each lifetime, while they remained stagnant..."

"The gap will only widen in the future."

Li Fan watched Sun Luyuan and his companion carefully explore, shaking his head slightly.

Losing patience, he directly ordered Sun Luyao to guide them to the only valuable location remaining in the Primordial Beginning Sect.

"Brother Sun, be careful. The aura of the formations here is the most complete..." Ji Hongdao warned, leading the way.

Sun Luyao felt somewhat speechless but couldn't expose himself.

The two proceeded with extreme caution, passing through a wall concealed by formations, and entered a secret chamber.

Within the chamber, two statues, one large and one small, were placed.

The larger one was seated on a cushion, holding a whisk.

The smaller one stood behind it, a smile on its face.

These peculiar statues instantly drew their attention.

Without acting rashly, they observed carefully.

"They appear to be mere stone statues, with no hidden mechanisms," Ji Hongdao concluded after a long while.

Sun Luyuan breathed a sigh of relief.

Concurrently, within the Boundless Mirror.

Li Fan glanced at the scene previously scanned and drawn by the Boundless Expansion Formation, then at the secret chamber.

His heart sank. "Can you see those two statues?" Li Fan asked Sun Luyao.

"Statues? What statues?" Sun Luyao was stunned, feeling bewildered.

"Tell your brother not to touch them," Li Fan commanded directly without explanation.

Receiving Sun Luyao's reminder, Sun Luyuan, trusting his brother, stopped Ji Hongdao's attempt to investigate further.

"Brother, what danger does this thing possess?"

However, he scrutinized the statues for a long time without discerning anything unusual.

"I've accidentally glimpsed similar records to these statues in ancient texts before. They seem to be the origin of the Ten Sects' inheritance, the Grand Arch-Mage Tiandu..." Sun Luyao relayed Li Fan's judgment.

"Grand Arch-Mage Tiandu?" Sun Luyuan and Ji Hongdao both took a step back.

They had heard of this legendary figure.

It was rumored that he was at the Half-step True Immortal realm.

Anything related to True Immortals naturally inspired fear.

The higher one's cultivation, the more they understood the gap between cultivators and True Immortals, the more so this was true.

Within the Boundless Mirror, Li Fan's divine sense thoughts raced.

Previously, he had suffered greatly from the Void-Faced True Immortal statue.

It had taken him six reincarnations to eliminate the Void-Faced True Immortal's influence on him.

Although Grand Arch-Mage Tiandu and the Void-Faced True Immortal were not on the same level, he had still left a mark on himself. He had to be cautious.

"The Primordial Beginning Sect's inheritance comes from Grand Arch-Mage Tiandu, and it's reasonable to have his statues within the sect."

"But..."

"Other Immortal Sects do not seem to have statues of Grand Arch-Mage Tiandu."

"Moreover, even if they wanted to worship him, wouldn't it be in a grand, solemn main hall? Why place them in a dark, underground secret chamber?"

Li Fan's intuition told him something was amiss.

"The Primordial Beginning Sect doesn't seem like a sect that respects its masters and reveres its teachings. According to Senior Stone Slab, as early as the great tribulation of the Xuanhuang Realm began to manifest, they had already planned to cultivate the Five Elements Great Cave Heaven and directly devour the Xuanhuang to create a brand new immortal cultivation world, but they were later stopped."

"The one who stopped the Primordial Beginning Sect was undoubtedly Mr. Bai."

"Before the Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth fully opposed cultivators, cultivators still revered the Heavenly Dao. Born from heaven and earth, like the parents of cultivators."

"Yet, the Primordial Beginning Sect ruthlessly extracted the essence of heaven and earth, no different from new law cultivators."

"Grand Arch-Mage Tiandu..."

Li Fan scanned the statue of Grand Arch-Mage Tiandu again with the Boundless Expansion Formation.

There were two statues, one large and one small.

Rumor had it that the seated figure imparted countless cultivation methods and secret arts to the ten sects.

However, an inexplicable intuition told Li Fan that the standing child might be more extraordinary.

Thus, the Boundless Expansion Formation focused its attention on the smiling child statue.

Boundless faint light swept over the area where the statues were located, time and again.

With each sweep, lines slowly appeared in the image revealed by the Boundless Mirror.

However, these lines also slowly disappeared over time.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, accelerating the scan speed of the Boundless Mirror.

The lines slowly accumulated again.

"Brother, help me."

Proving unable to withstand the overload, Sun Luyao sought help from his brother.

Only after receiving Sun Luyuan's vital blood support was the Boundless Mirror finally able to reveal the true appearance of the statues in the secret chamber.

They were two bones.

It was as if all the flesh and blood of some creature had been stripped away, leaving only these two bones.

Chapter 1211: Source of Immortal Disaster

The Source of Immortality Calamity

According to common sense, if it were just ordinary remains, Li Fan should not have sensed any life force from them. However, these two bones… made Li Fan's heart suddenly tighten, as if being stared at by some existence. The stone statues formed by the bones also seemed as if they could come alive at any moment, exuding a strange aura.

Li Fan decisively ended the probe of the Boundless Mirror without hesitation. The scene before him instantly changed. The bones disappeared, and what met his eyes were still those seemingly ordinary stone statues. The sense of crisis in Li Fan's heart slowly faded.

"Senior…" Sun Luyao was startled by the scene just now and was somewhat at a loss.

"Tell your brother to stay away from those two stone statues." Li Fan instructed calmly on the surface, but inwardly, a storm was raging. Were those two bones indeed the Great Law Master's? Based on their external appearance, they were most likely from the Great Law Master. But why would the half-immortal have two bones left in the Primordial Beginning Sect?

"Could it be that he was so severely injured that his bones were stolen by cultivators and he was powerless to retrieve them?" This thought flashed through Li Fan's mind. But he quickly questioned himself. "Is that possible?" The power that enveloped the entire Yuan Dao Prefecture, capable of devouring ten years of time, indicated that the Great Law Master had not yet fallen. The might of a half-immortal, no matter how severely injured, was not something that cultivators below that realm could deal with. Not to mention, he was a former ancient Eternal Life stage cultivator.

"Unless…"

"Boundless Mirror." Li Fan looked at the timid Sun Luyao, this new spirit of the Boundless Mirror. When the Sun brothers first found the broken Boundless Mirror, its immortal artifact spirit had already disappeared, which allowed the two mortals to take advantage. Judging from the destructive storm that erupted from the Boundless Mirror not long ago, it seemed to be related to the confrontation with this disaster, causing the spirit to dissipate and the Boundless Mirror to be damaged.

"The Boundless Mirror is an ancient immortal artifact of Xuanhuang, rewarded by the Immortal Realm to the Boundless Sect. Even if the Immortal Realm was destroyed due to unspeakable tribulations, it should not have affected the Boundless Mirror. But, inexplicably, this destructive storm, which should not have appeared in the mortal world, played out in the Boundless Mirror…"

Li Fan suddenly recalled his Holy Embryo avatar infiltrating the Xuan Xian Zhou on the other side of the star sea, and simultaneously bringing that formless disaster in the pitch-black sea of stars into it, causing several cultivators to die tragically.

"Spread…"

"Beyond Xuanhuang…" In the history of the Xuanhuang Realm, the only known entity that might have had contact with the Immortal Realm and came from outside Xuanhuang was the Great Law Master.

"Looking at it this way, the Boundless Mirror and even the Primordial Beginning Sect might have been affected by the Great Law Master." The past events here were too mysterious, and the clues available were too few. Li Fan could only make such a guess. "However, if the guess is not far off, then perhaps the trouble with the Boundless Mirror can be resolved."

Li Fan's eyes flickered.

Chen Hongdao and Sun Luyuan, after learning of the risks of this place, made the wise choice to temporarily leave the secret chamber. However, they had differing opinions on what to do next.

"The remains of the Great Law Master are extraordinary. We should report this matter to the Immortal Alliance as soon as possible." Chen Hongdao said solemnly.

Sun Luyuan clearly expressed his opposition: "Brother Hong, you are muddle-headed! The Great Law Master is said to be the teacher of the Ten Immortal Sects. If this news reaches the Five Elders Association, they will surely try to seize it at all costs. A great war is inevitable, and countless lives will be lost! Can you guarantee that the Myriad Immortals Alliance's current state will not leak this information?"

Chen Hongdao was speechless.

Sun Luyuan continued, "Considering the attitude of the Legates, who only see the Heavenly Venerate…"

"Even the bones of a quasi-immortal might not be treated with reverence. If they are brought to the Immortal Alliance, the result will be either research or display in the Museum of Divine Treasures for people to visit."

"Moreover, the Great Law Master is a legendary quasi-immortal. Whether he has fallen is uncertain. If we desecrate him today, we might face his revenge in the future." Sun Luyuan finished speaking, his face full of sincerity.

Chen Hongdao said helplessly, "Then what do you suggest?"

"Leave it as it is." Sun Luyuan said firmly.

"Brother Hong, think about it. Even if they are the bones of a quasi-immortal, what benefit do they bring to us? With the new law preceding, even Longevity is almost hopeless, let alone becoming an immortal!"

"If we take them away, we might bring about endless calamities in the future, and there are no tangible benefits. Why bother?"

…

In the end, Chen Hongdao was persuaded. The fundamental reason was that these were only two bones. And they were only the bones of a quasi-immortal who had not successfully ascended. As Sun Luyuan said, for Harmonious Dao cultivators like them, they were of little use. Of course, if they were the true remains of an immortal, the choice would be different.

"Although we won't take them for now, we cannot let others take them. Brother Hong, with your profound formation skills, why not use formations to completely seal this place? Coupled with the original protective formations, we can ensure no mistakes." Sun Luyuan suggested.

This showed his stance. Sun Luyuan knew almost nothing about formations. As long as Chen Hongdao set up a formation here, he himself could not secretly come here to take the bones away alone.

Chen Hongdao did not refuse and immediately began setting up the formation.

After this ruin was sealed again, as the two of them returned, Sun Luyuan sighed in a deep voice, "If one of us can achieve Longevity, then we can bring out these bones to study them. Perhaps we can even advance further."

Chen Hongdao smiled bitterly and shook his head, not taking it to heart at all. If it were when they were young and before they reached Harmonious Dao, they might still have had aspirations and the ideal of achieving Longevity. But now that they were in the Harmonious Dao realm, they had long given up the hope of achieving Longevity. The four steps of Harmonious Dao were all as difficult as ascending to heaven. The more they understood, the more despair they felt.

The two men fell silent for a long time.

After a long while, Sun Luyuan sighed, "I really don't know what kind of earth-shattering talent it takes to achieve reversal against the path."

"In our Myriad Immortals Alliance for so many years, besides the Heavenly Venerate, there is only one person, and he has also disappeared."

"If there were one more, our Immortal Alliance's situation would certainly be vastly different."

"Why does the Five Elders Association have five Longevity Realm experts? Could it be that they are truly more talented than our Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators and have accomplished what we cannot?" This was also a question that countless Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators could not let go of.

Hearing Sun Luyuan's sigh, as if remembering something, Chen Hongdao hesitated to speak.

"Brothers, is there anything we brothers can't say?" Sun Luyuan teased.

Chapter 1212: Leading Disaster to the Immortal Calamity

Disaster of Immortal Tribulation Appears

“Actually…” Ji Hongdao hesitated for a moment, then transmitted his voice: “I only heard about it by chance, and I don’t know if it’s true. Brother Sun, just take it as a bit of fun. However, it’s best not to spread this matter.”

After making his disclaimer, he continued with a hint of solemnity: “Actually, two of the five Heavenly Venerates of the Five Elders Council were originally members of our Myriad Immortals Alliance.”

“But for some reason…” Ji Hongdao shrugged.

Sun Luyuan heard this rumor for the first time and was instantly horrified.

He wanted to ask more, but seeing Ji Hongdao make a gesture, he wisely kept silent.

After all, the matter was too unbelievable.

Lost in thought, the two quietly returned to the Sun family.

“This trip was in vain. Your brother’s problem possessing that mirror hasn’t been solved. What do you plan to do?” Ji Hongdao asked.

“Let’s take it one step at a time,” Sun Luyuan said helplessly.

“However, Brother Ji, you also said that the formation in the ruins is quite old. This indicates that my previous guess was likely wrong. After the calamity erupted in the Boundless Mirror, it might calm down for a long time. At least for now, my brother is safe in the short term.”

Ji Hongdao nodded at this: “I still have official duties to attend to, so I’ll be leaving first. If anything comes up, contact me anytime.”

“Thank you, Brother Ji!” Sun Luyuan said gratefully.

“Oh, what’s there to be polite about?” Ji Hongdao waved his hand.

After a few more pleasantries, he transformed into a stream of light and departed.

Sun Luyuan’s expression gradually calmed down.

In fact, the reason he had prevented Ji Hongdao from reporting the discovery of the Great Law Master’s remains was not only due to his previous explanation but also his own intentions.

“If the news of the Immortal Alliance discovering the Great Law Master’s remains truly leads to a great war between the two sides…”

A dangerous glint flashed in Sun Luyuan’s eyes.

“Perhaps this is an opportunity.”

“In the deductions of the Boundless Mirror, even the Saint Dynasty Great Qi could fight the Myriad Immortals Alliance on equal footing. If they were to encounter a faction that had just emerged from a war and suffered heavy losses…”

Sun Luyuan would never have imagined that he had thought of the same thing as someone else.

After the initial shock subsided, Li Fan had conceived of this strategy.

However, after careful consideration, he abandoned the idea of using the Great Law Master’s remains as a pawn.

Drawing the half-immortal into the game was too risky.

To achieve the same effect, Li Fan had many other alternatives.

For example, the matter of Dong Ji being refined into a puppet.

For example, fabricating the rumor that the Myriad Immortals Alliance was hiding another reincarnation Heavenly Venerate who was about to achieve enlightenment.

As long as Li Fan wished, he could instigate a war in the Xuanhuang Realm at any time.

However…

Recalling the rumor Ji Hongdao had mentioned on the Crossing Dust Boat, Li Fan frowned slightly.

“Two of the five Heavenly Venerates of the Five Elders Council were actually members of the Myriad Immortals Alliance?”

“And they stood opposed to the Immortal Alliance…”

“Could it be because of the Dong Ji incident, a sense of shared misfortune?”

“Or perhaps, it was because they knew that the Law Transmission was dismembering and dividing the Xuanhuang Realm?”

The Myriad Immortals Alliance would naturally try its best to conceal such matters.

Apart from the eyewitnesses from back then, it would be extremely difficult to find any written records.

Even after Li Fan’s many reincarnations, he was completely unaware of this.

Fortunately, knowing about it now made it much easier to inquire about it.

While Li Fan was contemplating, the conversation between Sun Luyuan and Sun Luyao had already concluded.

“Brother, is this method truly effective?”

“Brother, don’t worry, it’s about eighty to ninety percent certain. This even emerged in my mind naturally after I saw the Great Heavenly Dao Master. I suspect the Boundless Mirror has some connection with the Great Law Master.” Sun Luyao said with certainty.

“Alright, brother, I’ll think of a way. But this ‘You Clan’ you mentioned, I’ve never heard of them before. They must be a top secret of the Immortal Alliance. It won’t be easy to get some…” Sun Luyuan frowned deeply.

“Brother, don’t worry. I can still hold on for a while longer.” Sun Luyao smiled and comforted him.

Sun Luyuan sighed slightly and left the secret chamber directly.

Yes, the method Li Fan had given them to resolve the Boundless Mirror’s annihilating wind disaster was inspired by his previous guess.

Redirecting disaster!

To use an immortal artifact, or something close to it, to lure away the calamity hidden within the Boundless Mirror.

Li Fan suspected that the annihilating calamity, which had transferred from the Great Heavenly Dao Master to the Boundless Mirror, was likely very sensitive to beings at the ‘Immortal’ level.

Perhaps it would actively attack upon sensing their aura.

Then, a large portion of its power could be transferred.

Li Fan certainly wouldn’t use a genuine semi-immortal artifact as bait, but he could create some items that possessed an immortal aura.

This would rely on the condensed Origin Force essence provided by the You Clan.

“With the golden Origin Force essence, combined with the barely Immortal-grade Grand Array [Infinite Primordial Seen Square], we should be able to create a semi-immortal artifact.”

“Even if it’s just a facade, it should be enough.”

“It doesn’t matter if it fails; it’s just a test.”

Besides the branch captured by the Saint Dynasty Great Qi, the Myriad Immortals Alliance still held a large number of You Clan members.

As long as they found a way, with the Sun family’s status and connections, they should be able to obtain some.

However, what truly worried Li Fan now was the situation at the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters.

Ever since receiving the Law Transmission’s message about the sixteen Harmonious Dao cultivators leaving the Xuanhuang Realm, the Immortal Alliance headquarters had been in a state of lockdown.

It seemed they were planning something significant.

“With the Myriad Immortals Alliance’s foundation, it should be easy to accelerate the cultivation of sixteen Harmonious Dao cultivators.

“There’s no need to be so secretive and for such a long time.”

“The only thing I can think of that warrants such caution and fear of leakage…”

“Is a method to escape the Immortal Ruins and leave the Xuanhuang Realm!”

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan’s eyes.

The reason why various factions in the Xuanhuang Realm were currently lying low was largely due to the existence of the Immortal Ruins.

There was no escape.

If they knew of a method to safely leave the Xuanhuang Realm, without knowing about the existence of the high wall,

Many people would undoubtedly do so.

Without hesitation.

Just like what had happened in the Xuanhuang Realm thousands of years ago.

Every man for himself when disaster strikes!

“Even the Myriad Immortals Alliance itself would have to weigh whether anyone within the alliance would take the opportunity to escape.”

“After all, they can’t possibly reveal the existence of the high wall to the public. Otherwise, the world would fall into chaos.”

With this in mind, Li Fan once again urged the Boundless Mirror to probe the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

He had initially expected to find nothing, as before.

Unexpectedly, this time, he actually found some clues.

“Void Crystal, purchase quickly. Don’t be overt. Use covert means. Destroy them once obtained.”

“Void Crystal.”

…

Three or four such messages circulated from the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters through the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Chapter 1213: High Pressure of the Immortal Alliance

Immortal Alliance's High-Pressure Stance

“Void Crystal?”

In an instant, Li Fan’s mind conjured up information related to it.

Void Crystal was a silk-like solid crystal.

It could float in the air, move like flowing water, and emanated a colorful, dreamlike glow.

It was often mixed into magic treasures by female cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm, causing the treasures to emit brilliant, dazzling radiance when in their normal state or when activated.

But…

Besides its aesthetic appeal, it seemed to have no other use.

Therefore, although its production was not high, its price remained at a moderate level of eight thousand contribution points per piece.

Such a seemingly flashy and impractical item was now being purchased by people in the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters at the risk of severe punishment if discovered.

Clearly, Void Crystal must be related to the sixteen Harmonious Dao cultivators who were about to leave the Xuanhuang Realm.

In the Sun family’s secret chamber, Li Fan’s Heavenly Profound Mirror origin and the Boundless Mirror’s probing worked in tandem. He quickly detected several obscure related transmissions and transaction records.

These people were very secretive and cautious.

Most of them would agree on the Heavenly Profound Mirror and then conduct face-to-face transactions using standard spirit stones.

Occasionally, when a purchase was made through the Heavenly Profound Mirror, they would still list the information as if they were selling it after obtaining it, ensuring that a certain amount of Void Crystal circulated in the Heavenly Profound Mirror market without significant price fluctuations.

However, as the items were passed from hand to hand, most of the Void Crystals on the market were gradually controlled by the same group of people. The so-called transactions were merely a matter of transferring from one hand to another.

“A good method, much more pleasing to the eye than my crude market manipulation.”

“It seems this isn’t the first time they’ve done something like this.”

Li Fan clicked his tongue in admiration. Using the power of the Heavenly Profound Mirror’s origin, he also joined in.

He possessed the ability to erase information traces in the Heavenly Profound Mirror at any time, so he wasn’t as timid and hesitant as these underhanded rats.

He acted recklessly, purchasing madly.

He completely disregarded the so-called price, acquiring them at a price that no one could refuse.

Like a giant whale, he stirred up a monstrous wave in the Heavenly Profound Mirror’s transaction market.

Soon, the price of Void Crystal skyrocketed, soaring straight up.

This anomaly naturally attracted the attention of more cultivators.

Although they didn’t know the true use of Void Crystal at this time, it didn’t stop them from following suit and acquiring it.

The false Heavenly Profound Mirror identity created by Li Fan’s avatar soon received several unfamiliar transmissions.

“Which family are you from? Acting so recklessly, aren’t you afraid of death?”

“Brother, be more restrained. Don’t make it so no one else can eat.”

“Hmph, I’ll give you a piece of advice: greed is useless. Spit out what you’ve swallowed, and we can all survive together.”

…

To all such harassing messages, Li Fan simply replied with: “Very well, I’ll lure you all out now. Wait for liquidation!”

The cultivators on the other side immediately fell silent.

Upon investigation, quite a few had already died inexplicably during this short period.

“They’re so ruthless even to their own people.”

“But they’re all fools too.”

Li Fan didn’t take these people seriously. While toying with them, his action of acquiring Void Crystal did not stop.

But unfortunately, this time the Myriad Immortals Alliance reacted unusually quickly.

“Senior, quickly collect them!”

шωш¤¤￠○

Sun Luyao sent a warning.

And Li Fan’s tail-cutting action had already begun. One by one, the Void Crystals were taken out of the small Heavenly Profound Mirror, and then the created identity information was directly erased.

Li Fan’s divine sense then unleashed a strand of annihilating black light, directly destroying the small Heavenly Profound Mirror.

At this moment, an announcement from the Myriad Immortals Alliance finally arrived late.

It declared Void Crystal to be a prohibited circulation item.

All Void Crystals currently held by cultivators would be recycled by the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

The Myriad Immortals Alliance urged all parties to cooperate with the relevant work. Any attempt to obstruct this would be punished by banishment.

…

The news caused shockwaves in all directions.

This was arguably the strictest measure announced by the Myriad Immortals Alliance since its inception.

And it was all for a small, previously almost unnoticed item, Void Crystal.

What profound mystery did this item hold that warranted the Myriad Immortals Alliance making such a grand gesture?

Those cultivators who possessed Void Crystal but were unwilling to hand it over simply dismantled and studied it.

But as before, they discovered nothing.

Suspicion and discussion brewed like a storm.

And the Myriad Immortals Alliance, without any intention of explaining, directly implemented an even more forceful blockade.

In the Heavenly Profound Mirror, no more information related to Void Crystal could be found.

As for members within the Immortal Alliance organization, anyone caught discussing Void Crystal privately was directly dismissed from their position.

Discussions among non-organizational cultivators were also monitored by the martial arts halls of various prefectures, leading to warnings.

Such high-pressure tactics made all cultivators understand that this time was different from before; Void Crystal had truly become a forbidden topic.

The cultivators of Xuanhuang cherished their lives.

For a time, the Myriad Immortals Alliance was struck silent.

Voices could be suppressed, but how could the doubts and curiosity in their hearts be permanently suppressed?

The Myriad Immortals Alliance’s control had not yet reached every cultivator.

Therefore, in deep mountain caves far from the immortal cities of various prefectures, and in secret chambers heavily protected by restrictions, discussions about Void Crystal were unavoidable.

However, all the Void Crystals in the Xuanhuang Realm had already been confiscated.

They could only speculate.

Let alone speculating, even if they had the physical item, it would be difficult to figure out the true method of using Void Crystal.

In the Sun family’s secret chamber, even Li Fan, using the Boundless Mirror for detailed analysis, could not find any peculiarity.

“It seems that Void Crystal is only an important component of the related materials. There should be other steps.”

After consuming hundreds of Void Crystals, Li Fan had to reluctantly halt his research for the time being.

“We can only wait for the Immortal Alliance to complete the task of the sixteen Harmonious Dao cultivators leaving the Xuanhuang Realm before finding a way to inquire.”

“But we can prepare for observation in advance.”

Sun family.

Wu Ninglu, who was cultivating with her eyes closed, utilizing the resources bestowed by Sun Luyuan, did not notice a dark shadow slithering out of her storage ring.

The shadow entered her sea of consciousness and soon took control of Wu Ninglu’s body.

This was a soul fragment that Li Fan’s main body had left behind before entering the Law Derivation Jade space of the Myriad Immortals Alliance Guardian Hall.

Compared to the hidden divine sense, the power of this soul fragment was far greater.

After the divine sense unleashed a sword strike, destroying the small Heavenly Profound Mirror and cutting off the clue for investigation, it fell into a weakened state again.

However, this soul fragment, like a cultivator, could replenish its consumption by drawing on the spiritual energy of heaven and earth.

Chapter 1214: Purple Qi Enters the Starry Sky

Purple Qi Enters the Starry Sea

“This soul fragment was originally intended for the most crucial moment.”

“But now, it seems I have no choice but to put it to use.”

Lurking beside Wu Ninglu, Li Fan’s soul fragment had already learned all about her behavior and conduct.

Controlling her body, Li Fan’s soul fragment found an excuse to leave the Sun family without arousing suspicion.

After evading the pursuit of the Medicine Hall’s Chen family, he arrived at a remote, deserted underground location in the wilderness. Using readily available materials, he began constructing stone puppets.

He wanted to deliver these stone puppets to the outskirts of the Xuanhuang Realm before the sixteen Harmonious Dao cultivators departed.

He wanted to observe their method of escape at close range.

With Li Fan’s current attainments in formations, he had no fear of being discovered by the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

“They say one is so busy one cannot attend to anything, yet I have split myself into several parts, and still, it’s not enough.”

Li Fan’s soul fragment felt a hint of helplessness.

Counting carefully, his main body was hidden in the Law Derivation Jade space of the Myriad Immortals Alliance Guardian Hall.

The Holy Embryo traveled to the other side of the star sea, investigating the mysteries of the Reverberating Star Power.

The Boundless Mirror divine sense was too weak, unable to manage everything…

As for the Saint Emperor’s avatar, it had by unfortunate coincidence been taken into the Netherworld by Master Yin.

Therefore, only this hidden soul fragment could personally handle the matter.

The situation in the Sea of Darkness aside.

The day the Myriad Immortals Alliance completed the Law Transmission mission arrived sooner than Li Fan had expected.

Thirty-three days after Void Crystal was classified as a prohibited item.

A brilliant rainbow suddenly appeared in the Xuanhuang Realm’s sky.

It seemed to blend all the colors in the world, distorted and illusory.

Like a reverse-flying meteor, it pierced the sky and swept forth majestically.

The rainbow tore through the Xuanhuang Realm’s sky under the watchful eyes of many.

Its lingering afterglow, however, did not dissipate for a long time, permeating the sky for several days.

For the following half month, the Xuanhuang Realm’s sky was a spectacle of colorful, bizarre, and dreamlike hues.

Curious cultivators attempted to capture these scattered rainbow lights.

These colorful lights actually had a physical form; they could be collected and refined.

Moreover, they possessed the characteristic of making objects emit colorful light.

Coupled with the Void Crystal, which was strictly prohibited from discussion by the Myriad Immortals Alliance’s multiple decrees, cultivators understood.

This was Void Crystal, used to forge the artifact for leaving the realm.

The revelation of the truth did not cause much chaos.

Because for most cultivators, they were unaware of the existence of the Immortal Ruins, let alone the fact that the Xuanhuang Realm was fundamentally unable to escape.

They only knew that communication between the Xuanhuang Realm and the outside world had been severed for a long time, and they speculated that the Myriad Immortals Alliance was attempting to re-establish contact.

But these people were unimportant.

What mattered were those cultivators who, upon understanding, began to have different thoughts.

The Myriad Immortals Alliance began to stir with undercurrents.

Time flowed back to the moment the colorful rainbow departed the Xuanhuang Realm.

Through the eyes of approximately a hundred stone puppets, Li Fan gained a clearer understanding of the entire process of the rainbow leaving the Xuanhuang Realm.

The moment it left the Xuanhuang Realm, its trajectory, as expected, deviated from a straight line and suddenly turned.

It veered towards the direction of the Immortal Ruins.

But not entirely.

It was like a ball of dough being gradually stretched.

Only a portion of the colorful rainbow had its trajectory forcibly altered by the attraction of the Immortal Ruins.

The rest continued to resolutely speed towards the depths of the starry sea.

As the colorful rainbow advanced, more and more of its colors were drawn out, falling towards the Immortal Ruins. Red, orange, yellow, green, blue, indigo…

As these colors disappeared, the rainbow’s hues gradually became more singular.

Ultimately, only a strand of purple qi remained.

It flew alone into the unknown starry sea.

From the perspective of the Xuanhuang Realm below, it looked like a beam of light shot into the starry sea, which had dispersed into various colors.

It was merely a slightly peculiar phenomenon, not even warranting much discussion.

But in Li Fan’s eyes, this scene was almost miraculous.

“It actually resisted the suction of the Immortal Ruins?!”

“No, rather than resisting, it’s more like delaying and neutralizing!”

“Part of the suction it received was released, offsetting the force to a certain extent. Then, as it was peeled away layer by layer and rapidly distanced itself from the Immortal Ruins, the pull it experienced became smaller and smaller.”

“Countless precise calculations were required to achieve this feat!”

“It wasn’t a victory of pure strength, but a triumph of ‘skill’.”

Li Fan’s mind replayed the dynamic curve of the color separation.

It seemed to contain infinite mysteries.

The Dao Transformation Stone Crystal operated at high speed, attempting to deduce and replicate it in his sea of consciousness.

However, after the yellow light separated, it became dizzy and could not persist.

Feeling a sense of regret, he had no choice but to stop.

“Is this the method Law Transmission came up with?”

“Elegant.”

Li Fan could only offer these two words as his evaluation.

“Void Crystal likely only served for the separation of different colors.”

“As for the driving force for escaping the Xuanhuang Realm, it should still be those sixteen Harmonious Dao cultivators.”

“With the Longevity Realm being bound to the Xuanhuang Realm’s laws, unless one reaches Law Transmission’s level, it’s impossible to leave easily. Harmonious Dao is already the highest combat power that can be deployed by Xuanhuang.”

“Although they were artificially boosted by the Myriad Immortals Alliance, I can sense that the sixteen Harmonious Dao cultivators are not weak.”

Li Fan’s thoughts churned.

The scene of the colorful rainbow leaving the Xuanhuang Realm had deeply stimulated him.

When someone easily achieves a goal that you have attempted for a long time without success, one truly realizes the disparity.

“Law Transmission Heavenly Venerate is indeed extraordinary.”

“But it doesn’t matter. As long as I master this method, when I return to reality…”

“I will still be ahead of him.”

…

Saint Dynasty Great Qi.

Sun Erlang looked at Yi Shu somewhat strangely.

Recently, this senior would occasionally stop speaking mid-sentence and freeze.

If he hadn’t personally witnessed the terrifying power of the Dao Transformation Stone Mother and knew that this was the Stone Mother utilizing its computational power, Sun Erlang might have thought he had contracted some form of dementia.

But what was the Stone Mother doing that affected these fragmented bodies of the Taiyan Sect?

Having spent some time with Yi Shu, he understood the collective temperament of the Taiyan Sect.

Without presuming, he directly asked.

After a considerable while, Yi Shu finally regained his senses.

“It’s nothing. I was just thinking of a method to escape even without abandoning the Stone Mother’s main body under certain extreme circumstances.”

“Before achieving complete information immortality, losing the Dao Transformation Stone Mother’s main body would still have a significant impact on us,” Yi Shu explained to Sun Erlang.

“Extreme circumstances?” Having witnessed the Stone Mother’s power and experienced reincarnation in simulation worlds, Sun Erlang found it difficult to imagine what kind of disaster would force the Stone Mother into a desperate escape.

Chapter 1215: Washing the Dark Sea

Washing the Grim Sea

“If that day ever comes, senior, please don’t forget to take me along,” Sun Erlang said with a smile and a jest a moment later.

“No problem,” Yi Shu glanced at Sun Erlang and nodded in agreement.

Sun Erlang was stunned.

“Is your Master not in the Great Qi small world recently? I can’t sense his presence anymore,” Yi Shu bypassed the topic and asked instead.

Sun Erlang frowned upon hearing this: “Yes. I just don’t know where he went? As I recall, this is the first time he has left the Saint Dynasty.”

Yi Shu looked towards the seemingly ever-taller Saint Emperor’s Throne, countless shadows flashing in his eyes.

In the secret chamber below the Saint Emperor’s Throne, where the You Clan was being raised.

Over a thousand You Clan members circled, performing a mysterious ritual with dance and song.

In the center of their formation, a black gateway that seemed to devour all light stood tall.

And through this mysterious dark gate, one could reach the other side of the Xuanhuang Realm, the Dark Sea.

Saint Emperor Li Ping was currently within.

He was accompanied by Master Yin.

In the Dark Sea, sight, sound, and even divine sense lost their communicative properties.

But Li Fan could still feel Master Yin’s whispered words beside his ear.

It was like some mystical power was directly attached to his skin, enabling close-range communication.

Being in the Dark Sea, and cut off from the Saint Dynasty’s fortune, Li Ping’s current strength was pitifully weak. A single Nascent Soul cultivator from the Myriad Immortals Alliance should be able to kill him easily.

But the Saint Emperor of Destiny, standing in this alien domain, felt no fear.

Because within him flowed a power undetectable by ordinary cultivators.

A golden, vast power that transcended the mortal realm.

The You Clan nurturing plan was progressing smoothly.

It even bypassed the physical growth process; as soon as they were born, they were mature individuals with peak physical functions.

Although the drawback was a further reduction in lifespan, only three to five years on average,

As long as the flesh factory produced them continuously, the scale and number of You Clan members loyal to the Saint Emperor’s prayers could be maintained.

After the You Clan population surpassed four digits, the daily generated essence of faith had reached a considerable level.

Under Li Ping’s deliberate manipulation and weaving, a golden net centered around his heart had formed within his body.

Origin Force essence flowed like a river, and the current Saint Emperor Li Ping, even without using his cultivation, could unleash all sorts of inconceivable divine abilities with a mere gesture.

For example, with a single thought, he could trace the source of the Origin Force essence and instantly return to the Saint Dynasty Great Qi, regardless of his location in the Xuanhuang Realm. Even if other forces interfered, it would at most only delay his return; it could not completely prevent it.

Furthermore, when he was attacked, the golden net of Origin Force essence would automatically defend and counterattack.

With the current scale of the golden net within him, Saint Emperor Li Ping was certain that even a Longevity cultivator of the Xuanhuang Realm could not keep him down.

Of course, Law Transmission was an exception.

This was his confidence in personally venturing into the Dark Sea.

Through the power of Master Yin’s world spirit, the two communicated, exchanging words intermittently.

“Don’t you feel the strangeness here?” Master Yin’s voice was intermittent; his main body was nowhere to be found.

“Pitch black, nothing else,” Saint Emperor Li Ping said sternly.

“Alas, you’re different from me. It’s normal that you can’t hear these sounds. The low murmurs of various eras and figures in the history of the Xuanhuang Realm rise and fall in this Dark Sea…”

With Master Yin’s explanation, Li Ping finally understood the strangeness he was referring to.

The Netherworld was the aggregation of the Xuanhuang Realm’s power that had diverged from the Immortal Ruins.

These were originally parts of the Xuanhuang Realm. When they were drawn to the Netherworld for inexplicable reasons, they simultaneously brought along some “information.” It could be a sound, or a few images.

It could even be a complete divine sense.

Over time, suppressed by the power of this place, they all sank into the Dark Sea.

“So, the Dark Sea is actually quite lively.” Li Ping said thoughtfully.

“That can’t be said. The nature of this place dictates that all information sinks. I can only access these fragments of time by absorbing them. Didn’t you ask me the reason for the You Clan’s special physique? I think I know the answer.”

With these words, Li Ping felt the darkness behind him stir violently.

Master Yin suddenly appeared.

In stark contrast to the gloominess here, the small vortex-like state around him, which allowed Li Fan to "see" him clearly.

“If we consider the power of the Immortal Ruins as suction, then the power that maintains the existence of the Netherworld can be seen as repulsion. This repulsive force does not continuously exist like the Immortal Ruins’ suction. Instead, it washes over like ocean tides, appearing and receding rhythmically. The accumulation of this force over time has created such a peculiar existence in the Xuanhuang Realm.”

Master Yin’s tone was filled with awe.

While he had vaguely known about this region before, he had never studied it systematically.

This in-depth investigation deeply impressed him with the mystery of the Dark Sea.

“The suction comes from outside the Xuanhuang Realm, while the repulsion originates from the Xuanhuang Realm itself. But it’s not from the Xuanhuang heaven and earth itself…”

Master Yin fell silent for a moment, appearing to be calculating something.

“If I’m not mistaken, this periodic spontaneous repulsive force should be from the ancient Xuan Tian Sect’s [Great Void Crossing Star Array]!”

At the mention of this Grand Array, Master Yin’s tone became somewhat subtle.

It was as if unpleasant memories flashed through his mind.

But he quickly suppressed this emotion stemming from his inherent nature and continued his analysis.

“So that’s how it is. Void Crossing, Void Crossing. If one cannot counteract the suction of the Immortal Ruins that caused the birth of the Dark Star Sea, how can one float in the boundless starry sea?”

“Compared to that, the golden chains’ method of capturing other worlds is more like salvaging resources and strengthening oneself, merely incidental.”

“Indeed, it is a great Grand Array unparalleled in the history of the Xuanhuang Realm. It’s a pity that the Grand Array is now damaged, and if I’m not mistaken, each activation of the Dark Sea’s repulsive force comes at the cost of the Xuanhuang heaven and earth. Previously, the Xuanhuang Realm could capture other worlds to offset this consumption.”

“But times have changed. Let alone supplying the Dark Repulsive Force, the Xuanhuang Realm can barely protect itself.”

Master Yin surprisingly displayed a rare tone of schadenfreude.

Chapter 1216: The Truth of the Floating Void Formation

The Truth of the Void Crossing Array

“Ahem.” Feeling Saint Emperor Li Ping’s gaze fixed on him, Master Yin cleared his throat.

“Alright, returning to the main topic. The creation of the Dark Repulsive Force is an instinctive behavior of the Grand Array. Even if the Grand Array is damaged, it will execute according to the original logic. This Void Crossing Star Array is truly remarkable. It should have begun to independently seek substitute energy sources after losing the Xuanhuang energy supply.”

“The You Clan was born because of this.”

“I imagine you’ve also noticed. The power generated by the You Clan’s prayers can, to some extent, replace the supply from the Xuanhuang heaven and earth…”

“I don’t know how much you understand about formations. If I put it this way, do you understand?”

As Master Yin spoke, he noticed Saint Emperor Li Ping’s somewhat strange expression, assuming he was explaining too esoterically and unclearly.

So he asked.

“I understand a little. The Void Crossing Star Array was built by King Xuan Tian. If what you say is true, then this Dark Sea is, like the Grand Array module for capturing worlds in the starry sea, an important functional part of the Void Crossing Star Array.” Li Ping said thoughtfully.

“Correct,” Master Yin nodded.

“Moreover, in my judgment, the Void Crossing Star Array, besides these two modules and the main control, should have other functions…”

“The principles of formations flow boundlessly. The golden chains and the Dark Sea alone do not constitute a complete formation cycle. There should indeed be two other auxiliary formation modules for this Grand Array to operate at maximum efficiency.”

Before Master Yin could reply, he heard Saint Emperor Li Ping state his own judgment.

“It seems your attainments in formations are far superior to mine,” Master Yin said with a subtle tone.

Li Ping did not respond, instead pondering the missing parts of the Void Crossing Star Array.

Concurrently, he continued the exchange with Master Yin.

“If we view the Xuanhuang Realm as a flying boat struggling near a whirlpool in the starry sea, then in a sense, this is the power source of the flying boat?”

Master Yin pondered for a moment and then agreed.

“Then, if… I’m just saying if, given enough energy supply to the Dark Sea, could it possibly struggle out of the whirlpool step by step?” Saint Emperor Li Ping asked with an unusual tone, slowly.

“… Theoretically, it’s possible. I don’t know the energy conversion efficiency of the Dark Sea. More likely, even burning the entire current Xuanhuang Realm might not be enough to move the Xuanhuang Realm even a fraction. Moreover, I have a feeling that due to the recent deficiency in the You Clan population, the Dark Sea’s energy supply has encountered problems again. Perhaps it has begun to trigger new forms of energy absorption.” Master Yin shook his head.

“I always have a faint sense of crisis. We cannot be careless,” Master Yin’s tone was somewhat solemn.

“However, you recently came up with a large number of You Clan members, didn’t you? If the energy supply to the Dark Sea can be restored, perhaps this evolution can be stopped,” Master Yin suddenly said.

Saint Emperor Li Ping of Great Qi remained silent.

…

Myriad Immortals Alliance Headquarters.

Li Fan, who had just failed to decipher the colorful rainbow, could not afford to rest and recover. Instead, he immediately began deducing the Xuanhuang Realm’s [Void Crossing Star Array].

Li Fan recalled the scene in the 119th life of Mo Ruobin, where he mysteriously disappeared in the Dark Sea, leaving only an empty shell.

“So, the Dark Sea is also part of the Void Crossing Star Array.”

“At that time, Mo Ruobin successfully learned information related to King Xuan Tian through the Heavenly Profound Mirror and eventually went to the Dark Sea. It’s uncertain whether he truly perished, but his entire cultivation might have been directly devoured by the Dark Sea and converted into Xuanhuang’s power source.”

“Whether he sacrificed himself for the Xuanhuang Realm out of great love, or faked his death to escape, it is almost certain that King Xuan Tian, or at least matters closely related to him, are hidden within the Dark Sea.”

“Before, I thought the Dark Sea was a manifestation of pure alien power, so I couldn’t do anything about it. But now that I know it’s a manifestation of the Grand Array’s power…”

“Perhaps I can still decipher it!”

Li Ping’s experiences in the Dark Sea, as well as the scenes from Mo Ruobin’s 119th life, all flashed through Li Fan’s mind.

The Ultimate Dissolution Disc, empowered by the Dao Transformation Stone, resonated with a hum.

It was operating at an unprecedented limit.

“No wonder when I asked the Heavenly Profound Mirror for the Void Crossing Star Array back then, it prevaricated and even offered Immortal-grade Grand Array diagrams to temporarily appease me. Now it seems this Void Crossing Array is fundamentally the ultimate modification array for the Xuanhuang. It transformed the Xuanhuang Realm from a pure immortal cultivation world into an eternal immortal ship capable of traversing the Immortal Ruins.”

“If the Grand Array were not damaged, if there weren’t still a high wall outside the Immortal Ruins…”

“Perhaps the Xuanhuang Realm would have already broken free from its constraints and roamed the starry sea.”

“Perhaps it was when I asked the Heavenly Profound Mirror for the Void Crossing Star Array diagram that I revealed a flaw. After all, given the importance of this Grand Array, why would the twelve Law Kings of the Heavenly Profound Sect be unaware of it? And my attitude at the time, treating it as an ordinary array, did not show the corresponding importance.”

Countless thoughts flashed through Li Fan’s mind simultaneously.

Time slowly passed, the Dissolution Disc and the Dao Transformation Stone pulsed with light.

Feeling the increasingly intense stinging sensation between his eyebrows, a sensation he hadn’t felt in a long time, Li Fan frowned slightly: “It seems the complexity of this Void Crossing Array is beyond my imagination. With too little information, even with three Immortal-grade Grand Arrays as a foundation, forcefully deducing it is too strenuous. It’s even difficult to merely deduce a flaw in the Dark Sea.”

“Furthermore, does this Grand Array seem to have a mechanism to prevent deciphering?”

Li Fan’s heart trembled slightly.

Every time the Ultimate Dissolution Disc reached a critical juncture in deduction, a large portion of the array data inexplicably dispersed and vanished.

It was as if some power, spanning across time and space, was interfering.

Li Fan even suspected that if his main body were not hiding in the Myriad Immortals Alliance’s Law Derivation Jade space, he might have been directly locked onto by this power, rather than just interfered with.

“Fortunately, after each deduction and restoration of the Grand Array, some data is retained. It’s just slower.”

“Of course, it’s best to maintain the current state of the Dark Sea without change.”

…

As Li Fan’s main body’s thoughts churned, Saint Emperor Li Ping’s decision also underwent a sudden change.

“I intend to contend with the Myriad Immortals Alliance for the Xuanhuang, and naturally, I will not stand idly by.”

Chapter 1217: Floating Bridge Within Another Ring

Another Link in Void Crossing

“The Xuanhuang Realm is our only sanctuary, and naturally, we must protect it completely,” Saint Emperor Li Ping said as a matter of course.

“When I return, I will allocate a portion of the You Clan to guide them in returning to the faith of the Dark Sea. Since the Myriad Immortals Alliance captured the You Clan and disrupted the balance of the Netherworld, the Saint Dynasty will bear the responsibility entirely.”

“However…”

Li Ping gazed at the deep, dark ocean before him.

“Although the Origin Force essence is vast, its quantity is limited after all. I wonder how many You Clan members must pray day and night to restore the Dark Sea?”

Master Yin was moved by Li Ping’s attitude, then pondered for a moment and replied: “According to the You Clan leader, during their peak period, their clan members’ footprints covered the entire underground cave world. It is estimated to be at least five hundred thousand people…”

Li Ping said slowly: “It seems we need to improve our methods of treating the You Clan.”

Master Yin also nodded in agreement.

“Let’s end this exploration for now. I have a feeling that we two have gradually attracted the attention of this darkness.”

“Good.”

A golden light enveloped Li Ping’s body, making him appear exceptionally sacred and majestic.

As the light and shadow fluctuated, space itself seemed to distort.

In the next moment, Saint Emperor Li Ping’s figure vanished into thin air and reappeared in the Great Qi small world.

He did not use the teleportation gate generated by the You Clan’s sacrifice and prayer but directly utilized the power of the Origin Force essence net.

“Currently, the Origin Force Net’s source is only in Great Qi. If, one day, You Clan members everywhere in the Xuanhuang Realm pray to me, then I can use this connection to appear anywhere at will,” Saint Emperor Li Ping mused.

Having understood the significance of the You Clan, Li Ping summoned Wang Xuanba.

He conveyed his new strategy for dealing with the You Clan.

Besides continuing to increase the production of You Clan members in the flesh factory, he also needed to simultaneously foster the growth of the normal You Clan population for sustainable development.

“For these other You Clan members, you should find ways to increase their lifespan,” Wang Xuanba, kneeling on one knee, listened to the Saint Emperor’s instructions. Although he didn’t know the reason for the sudden shift in attitude, he loyally accepted the task.

After Wang Xuanba left, Li Ping then summoned Sun Erlang.

He assigned Sun Erlang the task of leading the army to conquer several underground worlds.

Sun Erlang, who had been idle for a long time, gladly accepted.

Then, instead of dismissing him as he had Wang Xuanba, he continued to inquire.

“How has Yi Shu from the Taiyan Sect been performing recently?”

The Saint Dynasty’s destiny was tied to Li Ping. As the Saint Emperor of Destiny of Great Qi, he naturally knew everything happening within the Great Qi small world but still asked knowingly.

Sun Erlang did not dare to conceal anything and truthfully replied:

“I didn’t expect the Taiyan Sect to agree to your request,” Li Ping’s cold voice echoed in the Saint Emperor’s Throne without any emotion.

“But that’s good. If, one day, the Saint Dynasty falls, seeking refuge with the Taiyan Sect would be a good outcome.”

Sun Erlang was stunned, then his face changed: “Master, how could the Saint Dynasty…”

Li Ping surprisingly chuckled: “Where is there absolute certainty in this world? What’s wrong with having a backup plan? But this is only for you. Do not speak of this to your junior siblings.”

“You may go now.”

Sun Erlang left in fear and unease.

Li Ping sat above, alone in the empty Saint Emperor’s Throne.

Although the exploration of the Netherworld had only lasted a short while,

It had caused quite a shock to his state of mind.

“Void Crossing Star Array, Fishing Pond…”

“My strength is already considered half-step at the peak of Xuanhuang. Yet, there are too many hidden oddities in the Xuanhuang Realm. The Myriad Immortals Alliance has ruled half of Xuanhuang for so many years; their foundation must be deeper than what is revealed.”

“Moreover, the war with the Myriad Immortals Alliance must not only be won but also decided quickly. Otherwise, protracted cultivator wars will inevitably cause irreparable damage to this world again. It’s already a patched-up, broken boat; how can it withstand further turmoil?”

As the Saint Emperor of Destiny, he had many considerations.

After pondering for a long time, Li Ping’s figure flickered and disappeared from the Great Qi small world.

When he reappeared, he was already in Jiushan Prefecture, Xuanhuang Realm.

Protected by the Origin Force essence, he was now qualified to venture out occasionally without excessive concern for his personal safety.

“Tian Beast.”

Standing in mid-air, Li Ping sensed the chaotic and disordered space around him.

“If my guess is correct, the Tian Beast should also be part of the Void Crossing Star Array.”

“The starry sea is fraught with danger. To successfully cross it, it is essential to investigate the path ahead and avoid dangers.”

“Eye of the Tian Beast…”

Some vague images flashed in his mind.

Outside the Xuanhuang Realm, in an independent space called the Eye of the Tian Beast, one could observe deeper parts of the starry sea than within the Xuanhuang Realm.

“It’s a pity the Tian Beast is dead. To find that unique space, one can only rely on chance. The starry sea is vast, and the suction of the Immortal Ruins constantly affects it, making it even harder than finding a needle in a haystack.”

“Three out of the four components of the Void Crossing Array have appeared, but the last one remains elusive.”

“…”

He shook his head slightly, temporarily suppressing his thoughts, and silently arrived at the headquarters of the Spirit Yuan Sect.

The Spirit Yuan Sect was the largest local power in this chaotic region of Jiushan Prefecture.

All its disciples practiced the Common People’s Spirit Yuan Art. While it seemed to break the rule of not being able to cultivate multiple laws simultaneously, in reality, they were merely tools for the sect leader to refine and absorb Origin Force.

Easily bypassing various restrictions, Li Ping followed the aura of Origin Force to the underground base of Craftsman.”What exactly is missing?”

“Origin Force, Origin Force essence, the difference is like heaven and earth!”

The puppet, shaped by golden Origin Force, exploded with a bang, scattering light.

As if the experiment had failed, Craftsman seemed annoyed.

“Come here!”

He turned and coldly snorted at a female cultivator standing beside him, a whip appearing in his hand.

The female cultivator’s expression was blank, her eyes lacking the usual liveliness of a person.

“Not right, not at all! Nothing like the real Shangguan!”

Seeing the female cultivator’s appearance, Craftsman became even more annoyed.

As he was about to swing the whip down, he suddenly saw the figure of the Faceless Saint Emperor in the secret chamber.

As if caught in a guilty conscience, Craftsman’s hand trembled, and the whip almost fell to the ground.

“Who are you?!” Craftsman, both shocked and enraged, looked at Li Ping and roared.

In the secret chamber, the puppets, which had been like inanimate objects, suddenly came alive, all staring at Li Ping.

Chapter 1218: The Holy Emperor Receives His Mandate

The Saint Emperor Receives the Mandate

Surrounded, Li Ping showed no signs of panic.

These puppets were driven by Origin Force refined and extracted through the Common People’s Spirit Yuan Art.

And the Enlightenment Spirit Yuan Art, currently practiced by the people of the Saint Dynasty Great Qi, was an upgraded version of the Common People’s Spirit Yuan Art.

With just one look, Li Ping understood how Craftsman manipulated the puppets. The golden Origin Force net within his body emitted waves of invisible fluctuations.

The purity of the energy was infinitely close to Origin Force essence, forming a natural suppression on the puppets controlled by Craftsman.

In the blink of an eye, dozens of the menacing puppets in the secret chamber became disoriented and unable to stand.

Including the female puppet of Shangguan.

Craftsman’s face turned extremely grim. Having dealt with Origin Force for most of his life, how could he not recognize the method by which the mysterious person before him influenced the puppets?

He had already abandoned the idea of fighting head-on and began planning how to escape, or even simply abandon this body and be reborn using his memory backup.

Li Ping, seeing the fluctuating expression on Craftsman’s face, naturally saw through his schemes.

Unhurriedly, he revealed the locations of Craftsman’s several memory backup points one by one.

Craftsman’s mind trembled violently, and he could no longer hide his shock.

“Who exactly are you?!” His voice was even cracking with fear.

Unable to fight, unable to flee.

Since escaping to the Xuanhuang Realm, Craftsman had never felt such despair.

“Fellow Daoist Craftsman, don’t misunderstand. I am here to offer you an opportunity,” Li Ping said slowly.

However, his somewhat grim tone, coupled with his unidentifiable masked face, made his words utterly unconvincing.

Craftsman naturally did not believe him; in fact, his fear intensified.

Because Craftsman was a name he had never revealed to anyone in the Xuanhuang Realm.

The world only knew him as the mysterious Sect Master of Spirit Yuan.

Now, a mysterious person who could reveal his origins and knew everything about him had appeared!

Craftsman even began to suspect if there were other survivors from the Celestial Mystery Realm besides himself.

For a moment, Craftsman’s mind was in chaos. However, his jumbled thoughts vanished as Li Ping produced a shining golden orb of light in his hand.

“Origin Force… essence?!”

“How is this possible!”

Craftsman exclaimed again, his face filled with disbelief.

Before he could get a closer look, the golden orb was put away by Li Ping.

“Fellow Daoist, aren’t you seeking Origin Force essence but unable to find it? I can teach you.” This sentence from Li Ping completely stunned Craftsman once more.

“Fellow Daoist, don’t you want to recreate the Immortal-grade puppet ‘Ancestor’? I can also help you,” Li Ping continued slowly.

Craftsman was already somewhat numb from shock. He was not surprised at all that Li Ping knew of the existence of the Ancestor.

He only felt an immense sense of absurdity, yet a sliver of hope began to emerge.

What if this person was telling the truth?

“What are your conditions?” Craftsman asked directly.

Li Ping chuckled, “Seeing is believing. Fellow Daoist, please follow me first.”

Craftsman followed Li Ping, traveling eastward from Jiushan Prefecture to the depths of the Congyun Sea.

Near an underwater volcano.

“Hmm?”

Craftsman gazed at the terrain, vaguely sensing a sleeping life form within the earth veins below. Li Ping’s next words confirmed his guess.

“You’re saying, a puppet with complete self-awareness?” Craftsman sounded somewhat incredulous.

“Not a direct puppet creation, but one that has transformed into a puppet through a mystical method. It has absorbed the power of the earth veins for thousands of years and has yet to complete its transformation. If awakened prematurely, it might result in an incomplete puppet body. I brought you here to see if you have any solutions,” Li Ping said calmly.

“Transforming oneself into an object?” Craftsman repeatedly savored the meaning of these words.

Then, a golden light shot from his eyes, scanning the continuous earth veins below.

After a long while, the golden light faded, and Craftsman nodded: “This puppet below, through thousands of years of continuous tempering by the earth fire, has indeed swelled its power to an extent unattainable before. However, the intensity of the earth fire itself is limited. Even if it absorbs for another thousand years, its power will inevitably be capped at the peak of the Nascent Soul stage. Further progress is impossible.”

“And this earth fire formation was set up by him before he fell into dormancy. After such a long time, the two have begun to show signs of merging. If one were to casually modify it, it might awaken him.”

“Unless…”

Craftsman pondered for a moment, then said thoughtfully: “Unless the earth fire used to temper this puppet itself undergoes a change.”

“You know, the Heavenly Dao of Xuanhuang is extremely strange and prone to great natural upheavals. Earth fire is a manifestation of the Heavenly Dao’s power laws…”

“However, this opportunity is rare and unpredictable,” Craftsman said honestly.

Li Ping said slowly: “I understand.”

“As expected of a descendant of the Celestial Mystery Realm. My original plan was to use heavenly treasures to modify and elevate the Earth Fire Returning Yuan Formation. But now, thinking about it, your suggestion is better. Borrowing the power of heaven and earth to recreate the universe…”

Craftsman was slightly taken aback, then emphasized: “I said, this opportunity is rare and unpredictable.”

“Is that so?” Li Ping sneered.

“Fellow Daoist, watch my technique.”

After boasting, Li Ping closed his eyes and stood still.

Craftsman, thinking he was accumulating power for a divine ability, observed intently.

However, after waiting for a full half-day, there was no movement.

If not for the faint aura of Origin Force essence still locking onto him, Craftsman would have taken this opportunity to slip away.

But the situation was beyond his control. Since the other party remained silent, he could only continue to wait.

This wait lasted for more than half a month.

It was only because Craftsman, as a grandmaster of artifact refining, possessed an extraordinary temperament that he could barely endure.

And in a place unseen by Craftsman, within the Great Qi small world.

The large number of You Clan members, both those captured and those produced by the flesh factory, began to pray to the Dark Sea once more.

Perhaps because they were inherently created to provide power to the Dark Sea,

With little to no guidance, their praying efficiency was several times higher than praying to the Faceless Saint Emperor.

Subtly, a change began to occur in the Xuanhuang Realm.

And the Faceless Saint Emperor of Great Qi, standing in the depths of the Congyun Sea, silently felt this change in heaven and earth.

Some things did not happen overnight but accumulated slowly.

Half a month later, when Li Ping felt that the accumulation had finally reached a certain threshold…

“Reverse Heaven and Earth!”

The Faceless Saint Emperor softly chanted, his figure majestic as he pointed gently towards the continuous earth veins below.

What seemed like a casual gesture, however, caused Craftsman, who had been watching, to be greatly startled moments later!

Chapter 1219: Ink Flame Melts Heaven and Sun

Ink Flame Melts Heavenly Sun

The earth veins, which had already reached their theoretical limit, inexplicably began to burn more vigorously.

The flames surged and erupted.

Cracks appeared on the seabed, and countless bubbles churned incessantly.

What shocked Craftsman was not these anomalies.

But rather, a different kind of peculiar being was quietly born from this earth fire before him.

Having been in the Xuanhuang Realm for so many years, he was no longer unfamiliar with this kind of existence.

It had a name known to almost everyone: Earth and Heaven’s Soul!

As the embodiment of the Xuanhuang Realm’s heaven and earth laws, any cultivator who absorbed it could soar to the heavens and advance to the Harmonious Dao realm.

Earth and Heaven’s Souls were immensely precious cultivation resources, and their appearance was entirely unpredictable.

But now, an Earth and Heaven’s Soul had taken shape with a simple gesture from this mysterious Faceless person!

“This…”

As Craftsman’s perception struggled to comprehend, even more mystical things happened.

The Earth and Heaven’s Soul born from the earth fire did not make any aggressive moves.

Instead, it quietly catalyzed the earth fire. After the flames turned from orange-yellow to black, it actively threw itself into the Earth Fire Returning Yuan Formation!

It was a self-sacrifice, exchanging itself for the possibility of further progress for the dormant puppet within the formation!

The black flames leaped silently, and with the continuous operation of the Earth Fire Returning Yuan Formation, they merged into the massive puppet body beneath the earth.

Boom! Boom! Boom!

Continuous sounds of collapse and explosion reverberated from underground.

These were signs of the puppet’s body being purged of impurities.

“This Earth and Heaven’s Soul, not only did it not actively attack cultivators, but it actually helped this undersea puppet achieve further progress as that person intended?”

“How is that possible?”

As is well known, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao and Xuanhuang cultivators have an irreconcilable conflict.

When cultivators see an Earth and Heaven’s Soul, they are overcome with the desire to devour it.

And Earth and Heaven’s Souls relentlessly kill any cultivators who dare to appear before them.

But what was happening before him completely shattered Craftsman’s understanding.

“Even the Earth and Heaven’s Soul obeys him… Could it be that this person before me is the embodiment of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao?” Craftsman thought absurdly.

“Earth and Heaven’s Souls are born with a heavenly mandate. This black flame before me is called Ink Flame. Its duty is to assist in the birth of Harmonious Dao puppets…” Li Ping explained calmly.

His subsequent thoughts, however, remained unspoken: “Reversing Heaven and Earth can forge the will of the Heavenly Dao and generate Earth and Heaven’s Souls out of thin air. However, it ends there. Normally, to make an Earth and Heaven’s Soul, which opposes cultivators, sacrifice itself to aid a cultivator’s advancement…”

“This completely violates the commands of the Heavenly Dao. Under normal circumstances, it is impossible to achieve.”

“However…”

“I am the embodiment of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, and all my actions are for the Xuanhuang world!”

“Heaven and Earth will naturally aid me!”

Li Ping felt the subtle shift in the will of heaven and earth since the You Clan began to believe in the Dark Sea again under his command.

It was precisely due to the combined effect of these various factors that the Earth and Heaven’s Soul that appeared this time was the extremely powerful Ink Flame.

Even Li Ping felt a hint of danger from that unsettling black flame.

Under the refining of the Ink Flame, the undersea puppet also progressed at an unimaginable speed.

“It won’t be long before this puppet is born.”

“Although its realm is only Harmonious Dao, if it were to fight, I would likely be no match for it. And this is merely the result of the mysterious person’s casual gesture,” Craftsman discreetly glanced at Li Ping again.

While filled with fear, he could not help but look forward to the two favors the other party had mentioned.

“It seems he wasn’t boasting…”

Li Ping and Craftsman waited for the puppet’s birth.

As the Ink Flame and the puppet continued to merge, the disturbances in the surrounding sea intensified.

However, Li Ping concealed it with a formation.

Otherwise, such anomalies would have surely attracted numerous cultivators to watch.

Another half month later.

As if its fuel had run out, the deep-sea earth vein fire was completely extinguished.

The molten lava cooled into black crystals.

Only the seabed remained shrouded in thick mist due to the high temperature.

The aura of the Earth and Heaven’s Soul, Ink Flame, had completely disappeared. In its place, a new, powerful aura emerged from the seabed.

The sense of danger in his heart caused Craftsman to instinctively move slightly closer to Li Ping’s position.

Suddenly, that aura vanished from Craftsman’s perception.

Craftsman’s expression drastically changed, and a layer of silvery-white armor materialized, protecting him.

A dark figure quietly appeared beside them.

The target was not Craftsman, but Li Ping, the Faceless Saint Emperor of Great Qi!

Tian Yang, who had just awakened, was too vigilant. Sensing the two powerful auras nearby, he immediately attacked without a word.

As danger loomed, facing Tian Yang’s attack, Li Ping did not dodge.

He did not even summon the power of Origin Force essence for defense.

With a simple telepathic transmission, he awakened the somewhat confused Tian Yang and stopped his rash action.

“Tian Yang, do you want to avenge your Master and Senior Brother?”

Tian Yang’s body trembled violently, and he revealed his true form, staring intently at Li Ping.

His appearance was still that of a child no older than ten years old, just as he was before falling asleep.

However, his eyes occasionally revealed a depth of沧桑 (cāngsāng, vicissitude/world-weariness) completely incongruous with his age.

After calming down slightly, the scene of Li Ping helping him absorb the Earth and Heaven’s Soul while he slept also flashed through his mind.

Knowing that his current strength was entirely due to the other party’s help, the hostility in Tian Yan’s heart gradually dissipated.

However, he still stared fixedly at Li Ping, wanting an answer to his question just now.

“The culprit responsible for the countless sects and cultivators tragically killed in the great war against the Xuanhuang Realm years ago still exists…”

“I intend to…”

Li Ping slowly transmitted his explanation.

Tian Yang quietly listened to the plan, his aura fluctuating.

Then, he withdrew and flew to Li Ping’s side.

“This place is not suitable for lingering. Let’s go back first,” Li Ping said.

Then he looked at Craftsman: “Fellow Daoist, are you coming along?”

Since Tian Yang’s appearance, Craftsman’s gaze had not left him.

“Do I have a choice but to come along…” Craftsman muttered inwardly, nodding in agreement.

Only after the three of them traversed the void and arrived in the Great Qi small world did Craftsman’s gaze finally shift away from Tian Yang.
