Led by the Five Elements Great Cave Heaven,

A total of nine cave heavens surrounded the Great Qi small world,

Providing the pull for its movement in the void.

The spiritual energy concentration in this mysterious small world was even higher than in the Xuanhuang Realm itself.

It was as if an invisible force was concealing it; even Craftsman could not perceive the details within with his divine sense.

…

Just as Craftsman was once again filled with shock.

An aura arrived like a rainbow, causing Craftsman’s heart to jump suddenly.

Tian Yang, who had been silent, also became alert.

A Longevity Realm cultivator?

How is that possible?

Chapter 1220: The Fish is Finally Caught

The Fishing Pond Finally Yields Treasure

Daoist Hundred Blossoms came to report her work to Li Ping.

Of course, the main purpose was to request Origin Force essence.

After absorbing it several times and her strength soaring, Bai Hua had tasted the sweetness and found it difficult to let go.

In fact, the golden Origin Force created through the You Clan’s prayer ritual was still slightly different from genuine Origin Force essence.

However, for an ancient Longevity cultivator like Bai Hua, it was enough to allow her to advance further, making it indistinguishable from the real thing.

While greeting Li Ping, Bai Hua also noticed Craftsman and Tian Yang beside him.

Although Tian Yang appeared to be a teenager, the power contained within him made Bai Hua inwardly wary.

As for Craftsman, Bai Hua sensed a familiar aura.

An aura of a cultivator from outside the Xuanhuang Realm.

After carefully observing the two, Bai Hua said nothing more.

The Saint Dynasty Great Qi had gathered too many strange and peculiar individuals. She had long become accustomed to it.

This was actually a good thing for her.

After receiving Origin Force essence from Li Ping, Bai Hua happily returned.

“Fellow Daoist, who is that?” Craftsman asked somewhat reservedly.

“Daoist Hundred Blossoms, formerly the Sect Master of the Heavenly Lotus Sect in the Myriad Blooms Realm,” Li Ping introduced concisely.

This simple sentence shocked Craftsman, and he couldn’t help but let his imagination run wild.

Like him, she was a traveler from another immortal cultivation world. In that case, were there more such beings in this small world?

With this question, Craftsman and Tian Yang, led by Li Ping, took a general tour of the Saint Dynasty Great Qi.

Whether it was the Immortal Spirit Pagoda, which continuously released spiritual energy day and night, or the Sky Patrol Arrows, which flew through the heavens on guard, they both marveled.

During their travels, the occasionally encountered unfathomable individuals made them realize: the Saint Dynasty Great Qi was filled with hidden dragons and crouching tigers; beings like them…

There were many more.

Finally, they arrived at the Saint Emperor’s Throne.

Li Ping returned to his rightful place, looking down at the two, his voice echoing in the empty structure.

“Fellow Daoist Craftsman, I know your artifact refining skills are superb.”

“I have some ideas for refining new types of puppets here. You might want to take inspiration from them.”

Craftsman was quickly drawn in by the schemes Li Ping displayed.

“Origin Force essence, combined with self-transformation into Dao, and the artifact refining techniques of the Celestial Mystery Realm…”

“To create beings with their own consciousness, comparable to Immortal-grade puppets.”

The more Craftsman read, the more excited he became.

In his opinion, this plan was entirely feasible. Many of the concepts within even resonated with his long-held beliefs.

“I will specially designate a space within the Great Qi small world for you to conduct your research.”

“Tian Yang will also assist you,” Li Ping continued.

“First, refine some puppets as practice. Once there are no issues, help Tian Yang with his modification.”

Craftsman heard this, glanced at Tian Yang, and suddenly understood.

“Ink Flame as the foundation, Origin Force essence to aid sublimation…”

“Perhaps after completion, its power will not be inferior to Xuanhuang Longevity cultivators!”

Thinking that in the future, he could truly create beings of Longevity, or even immortal-level existences in a sense, Craftsman couldn't help but feel secretly excited.

Shortly after coordinating with the personnel related to Great Qi, Craftsman impatiently began his work.

“Everything is ready. Next, we just need to wait for the Medicine King Sect’s people to return,” Li Ping mused.

He had already laid a net, and once the Medicine King Cauldron returned to the Xuanhuang Realm, it would be directly drawn into the Great Qi small world.

Although elixirs were not very effective in enhancing the overall strength of Great Qi, Li Ping possessed many malicious pill formulas that could severely weaken the cultivators of the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

The Faceless Saint Emperor sat on the Saint Emperor’s Throne, his mind reviewing all the recent affairs of the Saint Dynasty. Without him needing to micromanage, everything was progressing in an orderly and stable manner.

With everyone knowing that the Saint Emperor was always watching, no one dared to slack off.

After reviewing all the minor matters, the Saint Emperor’s thoughts slowly calmed.

His figure flickered, and in the next moment, he arrived in the dark secret chamber beneath the Saint Emperor’s Throne.

This place resembled the endless starry sky, with dozens of treasures floating like stars, emitting resplendent light.

The Saint Dynasty’s fishing competition had never stopped.

The treasures fished from the fishing pond were countless.

Li Ping had not broken his promise.

All these treasures belonged to the individual citizens of the Saint Dynasty.

Of course, for those who didn’t need treasures due to personal inclinations or not understanding their specific uses, they could choose to hand them in and exchange them for other rewards.

Within this treasure vault existed the unclaimed treasures from the fishing pond.

Li Fan was indifferent to most of them.

Only one item…

Li Ping extended his right hand, and golden Origin Force essence appeared.

One of the light clusters in the treasure vault reacted the fastest. Before any other light cluster could move, it had already come to Li Ping’s side.

It spun around him as if trying to please him.

Within the light cluster, a small, adorable kitten could be vaguely seen staring intently at Li Ping.

Li Ping condensed his Origin Force essence at his fingertip, and the little kitten instantly understood his intentions.

It chirped excitedly and approached, licking Li Ping’s finger.

“Neither beast nor artifact, appearing and disappearing in the vast starry sea, truly full of wonders. Such a creation even exists.” Li Ping couldn’t help but sigh inwardly.

This little kitten, though seemingly harmless,

In fact, when it approached, the golden Origin Force net within Li Fan’s body sensed danger and automatically activated its defenses.

Although it looked like a living creature, it possessed no life aura.

In reality, when it was fished out, it was initially just a statue in the shape of a kitten.

No matter how the lucky fisherman tried to test it, they couldn’t find any use for this cat-shaped statue. In the end, they reluctantly handed it over to the Saint Dynasty in exchange for other rewards.

And at first, even Li Ping hadn’t noticed its peculiarity.

Until one day, he suddenly noticed that a treasure in the vault had inexplicably decreased. After using Origin Force essence for some “law enforcement fishing,” he finally caught the culprit.

The cat was merely one of its forms.

After eating its fill, it lazily prepared to sleep, but felt the telepathic message from Li Ping.

Although still somewhat reluctant, considering its future meals, the little kitten let out a weak meow.

With a flash of dark blue light, the kitten transformed into a small square box.

Strange images were engraved around the box.

Stars falling, myriad beasts emerging from the earth.

In the starry sea, countless massive ships sailed in succession.

Two colossal figures confronted each other, divided by a river of light in between.

…

Holding the small square box, Li Ping aimed it at one of the light clusters in the treasure vault.

One end of the box instantly emitted a faint blue light,

Enveloping the light cluster within.

Chapter 1221: Divine Object Outside the Great Wall

Divine Object Beyond the High Wall

After a moment, from the other end of the small box, a beam of light was also emitted.

The small box vibrated violently, seemingly having expended a great deal of energy.

Seeing this, Li Ping infused it with a bit more golden Origin Force essence.

Replenished, the small square box gradually stabilized.

Finally, the lights at both ends disappeared, and an item identical to the previously enveloped light cluster appeared in the Saint Dynasty’s treasure vault.

Li Ping grasped both light clusters and observed them closely.

Within both light clusters were two identical swords.

They appeared to be forged from ten-thousand-year-old frost, and the sword bodies emitted an ice-blue light.

“The Myriad Year Icebound Sword is crafted from the core of profound cold, an anomaly that caused an entire realm to freeze solid.”

“If the cold within were to be fully released, it would be enough to instantly freeze a prefecture of the Xuanhuang Realm.”

“I believe that even within the current Myriad Immortals Alliance, this sword would be a treasure of considerable value.”

“However…”

Li Ping looked at the other Myriad Year Icebound Sword in his hand.

He could discern no difference.

“This square box easily completed the replication.” Li Ping’s thoughts churned.

As Li Ping was contemplating, the small square box squirmed and transformed back into its kitten form.

It seemed to have expended a great deal of energy, appearing somewhat listless.

It yawned, and clearly didn’t intend to leave, napping directly on Li Ping’s shoulder.

This was clearly not an act; it had even lost interest in the golden Origin Force Li Ping had offered.

Li Ping did not drive it away either.

Such a treasure was best kept close.

“Currently, it appears that when this treasure transforms into a square box, its function is replication.”

“It can achieve complete replication of items. This treasure seems to be in its growth phase, and some things cannot be replicated yet. Furthermore, each replication consumes a great deal of energy and requires a period of rest and adjustment.”

“Moreover, this treasure is not limited to just the square box and cat forms. It likely has other transformations…”

Li Ping stroked the sleeping kitten, which responded with a weak meow.

“Interesting.”

“It was worth my painstaking efforts in setting the trap; the fishing pond has finally given me a surprise.”

“Since its manifestation was a cat-shaped statue, let’s call it [Cat Treasure].”

When Cat Treasure was fished out, it was merely a common white light cluster.

But clearly, Cat Treasure, with its [Replication] ability, could not possibly be of only white quality.

“Although it’s possible it wasn’t activated initially. But regardless, it even managed to deceive the Immortal Treasure fishing pond.”

“The origin of [Cat Treasure] is highly unusual.”

“It might even come from beyond the high wall…”

Li Ping’s figure flickered, returning to the Saint Emperor’s Throne.

“This [Cat Treasure] will be a great asset in my struggle against the Myriad Immortals Alliance.”

…

In the Sun family’s secret chamber.

Li Fan’s main body and other soul fragments had already learned of Cat Treasure’s existence.

However, in this life, Cat Treasure could exert its greatest value in the hands of the Saint Emperor, so there was no rush to exchange it using the anchor point.

“Furthermore, it is still in its infancy. Its ultimate potential remains to be observed.”

“Besides man-made magic treasures, could it replicate Xuanhuang Realm’s natural wonders, or even existences like the Ultimate Dissolution Disc?”

Li Fan pondered. If it could, it would merely accelerate his collection progress.

Wasn’t each of his returns to reality akin to replicating the entire world?

With this thought, Li Fan’s initially turbulent state of mind instantly calmed.

Returning his thoughts to the Sun family’s side.

The Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters had lifted its lockdown. Sun Luyao had been summoned by the Mirror Master Fu for a detailed consultation.

However, the matter of the colorful rainbow capable of escaping the Xuanhuang Realm remained under the strictest level of secrecy.

Despite the dual probing of the Heavenly Profound Mirror origin and the Boundless Mirror, nothing could be detected.

Li Fan was not in a hurry.

There was no wall that couldn’t be breached. Even the strongest protective measures would eventually fail over time.

His task was to wait patiently.

Moreover, he was not the only one in the Myriad Immortals Alliance interested in the colorful rainbow.

Using the Heavenly Profound Mirror, he could constantly monitor the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

As long as they discovered this secret through any means, it meant Li Fan would also know.

“Senior, that method you mentioned to resolve the wind disaster, can it really work?”

Sun Luyao, who had always been fearful of Li Fan, suddenly spoke up.

“Yes.” Before Li Fan could reply, Sun Luyao quickly explained.

“Recently, for some reason, strange scenes have been flashing in my mind. They are all things I haven’t experienced before. After much thought, they are most likely remnants of the annihilating wind disaster…”

At the signal from Li Fan’s divine sense, Sun Luyao projected the scenes he had seen.

The images were blurry and changed too rapidly.

Li Fan could only discern scenes of countless beings instantly turning to dust.

And the methods displayed by those beings on the brink of life and death…

Seemed beyond the capabilities of ordinary cultivators.

“Scenes of the Immortal Realm’s great tribulation.”

Li Fan mused inwardly, but outwardly showed no sign of gravity.

He snorted coldly, “Don’t scare yourself. Do you think what you’ve gone through is the true annihilating wind tribulation? It’s merely a remnant passed down through countless generations.”

“Don’t worry. As long as your brother can find clues about the You Clan, I have a ninety percent chance of helping you expel it.”

Such confident words instantly reassured Sun Luyao.

In his view, the mysterious senior’s displayed methods were likely comparable to legendary True Immortals.

Sun Luyuan did not keep them waiting long.

Three days later, he quietly returned to the secret chamber.

Unlike his previous somber demeanor, his face was now filled with unconcealed joy.

“Brother, have you found clues about the You Clan?” Sun Luyao asked.

Sun Luyuan shook his head: “We are still investigating that, but I believe we will have leads soon.”

“Then you…”

Sun Luyuan lowered his voice, unable to conceal his excitement: “Law Transmission Heavenly Venerate communicated with the Myriad Immortals Alliance this time and also conducted a sweep of the Immortal Alliance headquarters, issuing relevant directives and carrying out personnel adjustments.”

“That old fellow Fu, because his strength hasn’t improved much over the years, was apparently singled out for criticism by Law Transmission himself. He is extremely anxious and will be in closed-door cultivation for a long time, so he won’t be able to bother us for a while.”

Sun Luyao was also delighted to hear this.

“By the way, when the Heavenly Venerate inspected the Immortal Alliance, did he discover the human avatar of the Heavenly Profound Mirror?” Sun Luyao asked.

“That, I’m not sure. However, judging from the current situation, it seems he did not discover it.”

“I have also been monitoring the human avatar of the Heavenly Profound Mirror, and there are no abnormalities for the time being.”

Chapter 1222: Sun Family Welcoming the Holy Fetus

Sun Luyuan fell silent for a moment, then whispered, "That Saint Dynasty Great Qi, I'm planning to contact them myself."

"Hmm?" Sun Luyao was startled.

He knew his brother intended to contact Great Qi, but had previously planned to have his subordinates scout the situation first.

"Why the sudden change of heart?"

"Circumstances have changed," Sun Luyuan said with a serious expression. "Who knows how long this old man Fu will remain in seclusion? I want to use this rare period of freedom to make plans for the future of both my brother and the Sun family."

Sun Luyuan's eyes were grim. "Originally, I was still hesitant. But that colorful rainbow light that left the realm directly made me give up. In the Myriad Immortals Alliance, we will always only be tools to be exploited. Should a great calamity befall the Xuanhuang Realm one day, those Mirror Masters and Law Transmitters will certainly not take us with them when they flee."

"The situation on Great Qi's side is different. As they say, there is no greater merit than following the dragon. By pledging allegiance before they have truly risen, we will become Law Transmitters of Great Qi once our plans succeed."

"Of course, ultimately it depends on the strength of this Saint Dynasty Great Qi."

Sun Luyao nodded slightly.

"However, this Great Qi small world is exceptionally mysterious. There isn't much information about it even in the Heavenly Profound Mirror. Brother, how will you find them?"

Sun Luyuan smiled mysteriously. "I've asked a friend to help with the deduction. Although I couldn't pinpoint the exact location, I've found the entrance to the small world. We'll know once we see it with our own eyes."

"Brother, won't this be dangerous?" Sun Luyao suddenly felt a wave of unease.

Sun Luyuan was brimming with confidence. "Don't worry, with my strength, even if Great Qi is a dragon's den or a tiger's lair, I can retreat with my whole body intact."

After comforting his brother, Sun Luyuan continued, "Oh, and there's good news. Ninglu has broken through. She's in the late Nascent Soul stage, just a step away from Harmonious Dao."

"When she broke through, her vital energy was in turmoil, which made me notice another life force hidden within her."

"She was pregnant with Lu'er's child before, but some of her own ideas led her to seal it with a secret technique," Sun Luyuan said with a half-smile.

Seeing his brother's slightly strange look, Sun Luyuan said sternly, "I've already examined it. It's undoubtedly the bloodline of our Sun family. No matter what Ninglu's identity is, as long as she can produce offspring for our Sun family, it doesn't matter."

"I plan to have Ninglu temporarily seal the life force of the fetus in her womb. She can give birth after she reaches Harmonious Dao," Sun Luyuan suddenly added.

"Lu'er's talent is already extraordinary, and Ninglu's aptitude is also quite decent. Their offspring will definitely be the most promising among the younger generation of the Sun family."

"When cultivators absorb the Soul of Heaven and Earth, the laws of heaven and earth are imprinted upon them. If the fetus within the mother can sense this simultaneously..."

Sun Luyuan's tone was filled with excitement. "Perhaps this little one will have a talent no less than any prodigy in the Myriad Immortals Alliance after they are born. Only then will our Sun family truly have a successor."

"The most crucial thing is that, with our current strength, we have the means to scheme for a Soul of Heaven and Earth for him."

When discussing the future of the Sun family, Sun Luyuan seemed to have endless things to say.

His brother, Sun Luyao, was also rare in that he listened attentively and with a smile.

"What a touching scene of brotherly affection." It wasn't until Sun Luyuan left that the mysterious senior's ghostly laughter startled him awake.

Sun Luyao then realized he had already been forced to do many things that were unfavorable to his elder brother.

"Your Sun family's little one... is rather interesting."

The clone's words made Sun Luyao's heart leap into his throat.

"Don't worry, I wouldn't stoop to coveting a child's body," Li Fan sneered.

"I have a cultivation technique called the [Cauldron of Creation Technique], which can continuously excavate the potential of the physical body. Most importantly, it has no cultivation threshold; it can be practiced even in the womb. I also have a [Formless Balance Technique], which can continuously strengthen one's soul through the interaction of the five elements," Li Fan's clone casually uttered, shaking Sun Luyao to his core.

"Although the [Formless Balance Technique] requires assisting treasures of the five elements to cultivate, I believe with your Sun family's current foundation, it shouldn't be too difficult."

"To continuously temper one's soul and body from the prenatal stage, and to be able to sense the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao up close through the mother's body... Tsk tsk... I'm even looking forward to what kind of monster this little one will be when they are born." Li Fan's clone emitted a sinister smile.

"Senior... what are your conditions?" Sun Luyao was clearly tempted.

However, he deeply understood that there was no such thing as a free lunch in the world. He solemnly asked, "What are your conditions?"

Li Fan's clone let out a cold laugh. "Seeing is believing. Fellow Daoist, please follow me first."

Craftsman followed Li Fan, traveling eastward from Jiushan Prefecture to the depths of the Congyun Sea.

Near an underwater volcano.

"Hmm?"

Craftsman gazed at the terrain, vaguely sensing a sleeping life form within the earth veins below. Li Fan's next words confirmed his guess.

"You're saying, a puppet with complete self-awareness?" Craftsman sounded somewhat incredulous.

"Not a direct puppet creation, but one that has transformed into a puppet through a mystical method. It has absorbed the power of the earth veins for thousands of years and has yet to complete its transformation. If awakened prematurely, it might result in an incomplete puppet body. I brought you here to see if you have any solutions," Li Fan said calmly.

"Transforming oneself into an object?" Craftsman repeatedly savored the meaning of these words.

Then, a golden light shot from his eyes, scanning the continuous earth veins below. After a long while, the golden light faded, and Craftsman nodded: "This puppet below, through thousands of years of continuous tempering by the earth fire, has indeed swelled its power to an extent unattainable before. However, the intensity of the earth fire itself is limited. Even if it absorbs for another thousand years, its power will inevitably be capped at the peak of the Nascent Soul stage. Further progress is impossible."

"And this earth fire formation was set up by him before he fell into dormancy. After such a long time, the two have begun to show signs of merging. If one were to casually modify it, it might awaken him."

"Unless..."

Craftsman pondered for a moment, then said thoughtfully: "Unless the earth fire used to temper this puppet itself undergoes a change."

"You know, the Heavenly Dao of Xuanhuang is extremely strange and prone to great natural upheavals. Earth fire is a manifestation of the Heavenly Dao's power laws..."

"However, this opportunity is rare and unpredictable," Craftsman said honestly.

Li Fan said slowly: "I understand."

"As expected of a descendant of the Celestial Mystery Realm. My original plan was to use heavenly treasures to modify and elevate the Earth Fire Returning Yuan Formation. But now, thinking about it, your suggestion is better. Borrowing the power of heaven and earth to recreate the universe..."

Craftsman was slightly taken aback, then emphasized: "I said, this opportunity is rare and unpredictable."

"Is that so?" Li Fan sneered.

"Fellow Daoist, watch my technique."

After boasting, Li Fan closed his eyes and stood still. Craftsman, thinking he was accumulating power for a divine ability, observed intently. However, after waiting for a full half-day, there was no movement. If not for the faint aura of Origin Force essence still locking onto him, Craftsman would have taken this opportunity to slip away. But the situation was beyond his control. Since the other party remained silent, he could only continue to wait. This wait lasted for more than half a month. It was only because Craftsman, as a grandmaster of artifact refining, possessed an extraordinary temperament that he could barely endure. And in a place unseen by Craftsman, within the Great Qi small world. The large number of You Clan members, both those captured and those produced by the flesh factory, began to pray to the Dark Sea once more. Perhaps because they were inherently created to provide power to the Dark Sea, With little to no guidance, their praying efficiency was several times higher than praying to the Faceless Saint Emperor. Subtly, a change began to occur in the Xuanhuang Realm. And the Faceless Saint Emperor of Great Qi, standing in the depths of the Congyun Sea, silently felt this change in heaven and earth. Some things did not happen overnight but accumulated slowly. Half a month later, when Li Ping felt that the accumulation had finally reached a certain threshold... "Reverse Heaven and Earth!" The Faceless Saint Emperor softly chanted, his figure majestic as he pointed gently towards the continuous earth veins below. What seemed like a casual gesture, however, caused Craftsman, who had been watching, to be greatly startled moments later!

Chapter 1223: The Sacred Dynasty's Shock

The earth veins, which had already reached their theoretical limit, inexplicably began to burn more vigorously. The flames surged and erupted. Cracks appeared on the seabed, and countless bubbles churned incessantly.

What shocked Craftsman was not these anomalies. But rather, a different kind of peculiar being was quietly born from this earth fire before him. Having been in the Xuanhuang Realm for so many years, he was no longer unfamiliar with this kind of existence. It had a name known to almost everyone: Earth and Heaven’s Soul!

As the embodiment of the Xuanhuang Realm’s heaven and earth laws, any cultivator who absorbed it could soar to the heavens and advance to the Harmonious Dao realm. Earth and Heaven’s Souls were immensely precious cultivation resources, and their appearance was entirely unpredictable. But now, an Earth and Heaven’s Soul had taken shape with a simple gesture from this mysterious Faceless person!

"This..." As Craftsman’s perception struggled to comprehend, even more mystical things happened. The Earth and Heaven’s Soul born from the earth fire did not make any aggressive moves. Instead, it quietly catalyzed the earth fire. After the flames turned from orange-yellow to black, it actively threw itself into the Earth Fire Returning Yuan Formation! It was a self-sacrifice, exchanging itself for the possibility of further progress for the dormant puppet within the formation!

The black flames leaped silently, and with the continuous operation of the Earth Fire Returning Yuan Formation, they merged into the massive puppet body beneath the earth. Boom! Boom! Boom! Continuous sounds of collapse and explosion reverberated from underground. These were signs of the puppet’s body being purged of impurities.

"This Earth and Heaven’s Soul, not only did it not actively attack cultivators, but it actually helped this undersea puppet achieve further progress as that person intended?"

"How is that possible?"

As is well known, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao and Xuanhuang cultivators have an irreconcilable conflict. When cultivators see an Earth and Heaven’s Soul, they are overcome with the desire to devour it. And Earth and Heaven’s Souls relentlessly kill any cultivators who dare to appear before them. But what was happening before him completely shattered Craftsman’s understanding.

"Even the Earth and Heaven’s Soul obeys him... Could it be that this person before me is the embodiment of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao?" Craftsman thought absurdly.

"Earth and Heaven’s Souls are born with a heavenly mandate. This black flame before me is called Ink Flame. Its duty is to assist in the birth of Harmonious Dao puppets..." Li Ping explained calmly. His subsequent thoughts, however, remained unspoken: "Reversing Heaven and Earth can forge the will of the Heavenly Dao and generate Earth and Heaven’s Souls out of thin air. However, it ends there. Normally, to make an Earth and Heaven’s Soul, which opposes cultivators, sacrifice itself to aid a cultivator’s advancement..."

"This completely violates the commands of the Heavenly Dao. Under normal circumstances, it is impossible to achieve."

"However..."

"I am the embodiment of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, and all my actions are for the Xuanhuang world!"

"Heaven and Earth will naturally aid me!"

Li Ping felt the subtle shift in the will of heaven and earth since the You Clan began to believe in the Dark Sea again under his command. It was precisely due to the combined effect of these various factors that the Earth and Heaven’s Soul that appeared this time was the extremely powerful Ink Flame. Even Li Ping felt a hint of danger from that unsettling black flame.

Under the refining of the Ink Flame, the undersea puppet also progressed at an unimaginable speed. "It won’t be long before this puppet is born."

"Although its realm is only Harmonious Dao, if it were to fight, I would likely be no match for it. And this is merely the result of the mysterious person’s casual gesture," Craftsman discreetly glanced at Li Ping again. While filled with fear, he could not help but look forward to the two favors the other party had mentioned.

"It seems he wasn't boasting..." Li Ping and Craftsman waited for the puppet's birth. As the Ink Flame and the puppet continued to merge, the disturbances in the surrounding sea intensified. However, Li Ping concealed it with a formation. Otherwise, such anomalies would have surely attracted numerous cultivators to watch.

Another half month later.

As if its fuel had run out, the deep-sea earth vein fire was completely extinguished. The molten lava cooled into black crystals. Only the seabed remained shrouded in thick mist due to the high temperature. The aura of the Earth and Heaven’s Soul, Ink Flame, had completely disappeared.

In its place, a new, powerful aura emerged from the seabed. The sense of danger in his heart caused Craftsman to instinctively move slightly closer to Li Ping’s position.

Suddenly, that aura vanished from Craftsman’s perception. Craftsman’s expression drastically changed, and a layer of silvery-white armor materialized, protecting him. A dark figure quietly appeared beside them. The target was not Craftsman, but Li Ping, the Faceless Saint Emperor of Great Qi!

Tian Yang, who had just awakened, was too vigilant. Sensing the two powerful auras nearby, he immediately attacked without a word.

As danger loomed, facing Tian Yang’s attack, Li Ping did not dodge. He did not even summon the power of Origin Force essence for defense. With a simple telepathic transmission, he awakened the somewhat confused Tian Yang and stopped his rash action.

"Tian Yang, do you want to avenge your Master and Senior Brother?"

Tian Yang's body trembled violently, and he revealed his true form, staring intently at Li Ping. His appearance was still that of a child no older than ten years old, just as he was before falling asleep. However, his eyes occasionally revealed a depth of vicissitude completely incongruous with his age.

After calming down slightly, the scene of Li Ping helping him absorb the Earth and Heaven’s Soul while he slept also flashed through his mind. Knowing that his current strength was entirely due to the other party’s help, the hostility in Tian Yan's heart gradually dissipated. However, he still stared Fixedly at Li Ping, wanting an answer to his question just now.

"The culprit responsible for the countless sects and cultivators tragically killed in the great war against the Xuanhuang Realm years ago still exists..."

"I intend to..." Li Ping slowly transmitted his explanation. Tian Yang quietly listened to the plan, his aura fluctuating. Then, he withdrew and flew to Li Ping’s side.

"This place is not suitable for lingering. Let's go back first," Li Ping said. Then he looked at Craftsman: "Fellow Daoist, are you coming along?"

Since Tian Yang's appearance, Craftsman's gaze had not left him. "Do I have a choice but to come along..." Craftsman muttered inwardly, nodding in agreement.

Only after the three of them traversed the void and arrived in the Great Qi small world did Craftsman's gaze finally shift away from Tian Yang. Led by the Five Elements Great Cave Heaven, a total of nine cave heavens surrounded the Great Qi small world, providing the pull for its movement in the void. The spiritual energy concentration in this mysterious small world was even higher than in the Xuanhuang Realm itself. It was as if an invisible force was concealing it; even Craftsman could not perceive the details within with his divine sense.

...

Just as Craftsman was once again filled with shock. An aura arrived like a rainbow, causing Craftsman's heart to jump suddenly. Tian Yang, who had been silent, also became alert. A Longevity Realm cultivator? How is that possible?

Chapter 1224: The Heaven-Defying Invisible Net

Daoist Hundred Blossoms came to report her work to Li Ping. Of course, the main purpose was to request Origin Force essence. After absorbing it several times and her strength soaring, Bai Hua had tasted the sweetness and found it difficult to let go. In fact, the golden Origin Force created through the You Clan’s prayer ritual was still slightly different from genuine Origin Force essence. However, for an ancient Longevity cultivator like Bai Hua, it was enough to allow her to advance further, making it indistinguishable from the real thing.

While greeting Li Ping, Bai Hua also noticed Craftsman and Tian Yang beside him. Although Tian Yang appeared to be a teenager, the power contained within him made Bai Hua inwardly wary. As for Craftsman, Bai Hua sensed a familiar aura. An aura of a cultivator from outside the Xuanhuang Realm.

After carefully observing the two, Bai Hua said nothing more. The Saint Dynasty Great Qi had gathered too many strange and peculiar individuals. She had long become accustomed to it. This was actually a good thing for her. After receiving Origin Force essence from Li Ping, Bai Hua happily returned.

"Fellow Daoist, who is that?" Craftsman asked somewhat reservedly.

"Daoist Hundred Blossoms, formerly the Sect Master of the Heavenly Lotus Sect in the Myriad Blooms Realm," Li Ping introduced concisely.

This simple sentence shocked Craftsman, and he couldn’t help but let his imagination run wild. Like him, she was a traveler from another immortal cultivation world. In that case, were there more such beings in this small world?

With this question, Craftsman and Tian Yang, led by Li Ping, took a general tour of the Saint Dynasty Great Qi. Whether it was the Immortal Spirit Pagoda, which continuously released spiritual energy day and night, or the Sky Patrol Arrows, which flew through the heavens on guard, they both marveled. During their travels, the occasionally encountered unfathomable individuals made them realize: the Saint Dynasty Great Qi was filled with hidden dragons and crouching tigers; beings like them... There were many more.

Finally, they arrived at the Saint Emperor’s Throne. Li Ping returned to his rightful place, looking down at the two, his voice echoing in the empty structure.

"Fellow Daoist Craftsman, I know your artifact refining skills are superb."

"I have some ideas for refining new types of puppets here. You might want to take inspiration from them."

Craftsman was quickly drawn in by the schemes Li Ping displayed.

"Origin Force essence, combined with self-transformation into Dao, and the artifact refining techniques of the Celestial Mystery Realm..."

"To create beings with their own consciousness, comparable to Immortal-grade puppets."

The more Craftsman read, the more excited he became. In his opinion, this plan was entirely feasible. Many of the concepts within even resonated with his long-held beliefs.

"I will specially designate a space within the Great Qi small world for you to conduct your research."

"Tian Yang will also assist you," Li Ping continued. "First, refine some puppets as practice. Once there are no issues, help Tian Yang with his modification."

Craftsman heard this, glanced at Tian Yang, and suddenly understood.

"Ink Flame as the foundation, Origin Force essence to aid sublimation..."

"Perhaps after completion, its power will not be inferior to Xuanhuang Longevity cultivators!"

Thinking that in the future, he could truly create beings of Longevity, or even immortal-level existences in a sense, Craftsman couldn't help but feel secretly excited. Shortly after coordinating with the personnel related to Great Qi, Craftsman impatiently began his work.

"Everything is ready. Next, we just need to wait for the Medicine King Sect’s people to return," Li Ping mused. He had already laid a net, and once the Medicine King Cauldron returned to the Xuanhuang Realm, it would be directly drawn into the Great Qi small world. Although elixirs were not very effective in enhancing the overall strength of Great Qi, Li Ping possessed many malicious pill formulas that could severely weaken the cultivators of the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

The Faceless Saint Emperor sat on the Saint Emperor’s Throne, his mind reviewing all the recent affairs of the Saint Dynasty. Without him needing to micromanage, everything was progressing in an orderly and stable manner. With everyone knowing that the Saint Emperor was always watching, no one dared to slack off.

After reviewing all the minor matters, the Saint Emperor’s thoughts slowly calmed. His figure flickered, and in the next moment, he arrived in the dark secret chamber beneath the Saint Emperor’s Throne. This place resembled the endless starry sky, with dozens of treasures floating like stars, emitting resplendent light. The Saint Dynasty’s fishing competition had never stopped. The treasures fished from the fishing pond were countless. Li Ping had not broken his promise. All these treasures belonged to the individual citizens of the Saint Dynasty. Of course, for those who didn’t need treasures due to personal inclinations or not understanding their specific uses, they could choose to hand them in and exchange them for other rewards.

Within this treasure vault existed the unclaimed treasures from the fishing pond. Li Fan was indifferent to most of them. Only one item...

Li Ping extended his right hand, and golden Origin Force essence appeared. One of the light clusters in the treasure vault reacted the fastest. Before any other light cluster could move, it had already come to Li Ping’s side. It spun around him as if trying to please him. Within the light cluster, a small, adorable kitten could be vaguely seen staring intently at Li Ping.

Li Ping condensed his Origin Force essence at his fingertip, and the little kitten instantly understood his intentions. It chirped excitedly and approached, licking Li Ping’s finger.

"Neither beast nor artifact, appearing and disappearing in the vast starry sea, truly full of wonders. Such a creation even exists." Li Ping couldn’t help but sigh inwardly.

This little kitten, though seemingly harmless, In fact, when it approached, the golden Origin Force net within Li Fan’s body sensed danger and automatically activated its defenses. Although it looked like a living creature, it possessed no life aura. In reality, when it was fished out, it was initially just a statue in the shape of a kitten. No matter how the lucky fisherman tried to test it, they couldn’t find any use for this cat-shaped statue. In the end, they reluctantly handed it over to the Saint Dynasty in exchange for other rewards. And at first, even Li Ping hadn’t noticed its peculiarity. Until one day, he suddenly noticed that a treasure in the vault had inexplicably decreased. After using Origin Force essence for some “law enforcement fishing,” he finally caught the culprit.

The cat was merely one of its forms. After eating its fill, it lazily prepared to sleep, but felt the telepathic message from Li Ping. Although still somewhat reluctant, considering its future meals, the little kitten let out a weak meow.

With a flash of dark blue light, the kitten transformed into a small square box. Strange images were engraved around the box. Stars falling, myriad beasts emerging from the earth. In the starry sea, countless massive ships sailed in succession. Two colossal figures confronted each other, divided by a river of light in between. ...

Holding the small square box, Li Ping aimed it at one of the light clusters in the treasure vault. One end of the box instantly emitted a faint blue light, enveloping the light cluster within.

Chapter 1225: Immortal Boat Trapped and Seeking Survival

After a moment, from the other end of the small box, a beam of light was also emitted. The small box vibrated violently, seemingly having expended a great deal of energy.

Seeing this, Li Ping infused it with a bit more golden Origin Force essence. Replenished, the small square box gradually stabilized.

Finally, the lights at both ends disappeared, and an item identical to the previously enveloped light cluster appeared in the Saint Dynasty’s treasure vault.

Li Ping grasped both light clusters and observed them closely. Within both light clusters were two identical swords. They appeared to be forged from ten-thousand-year-old frost, and the sword bodies emitted an ice-blue light.

"The Myriad Year Icebound Sword is crafted from the core of profound cold, an anomaly that caused an entire realm to freeze solid."

"If the cold within were to be fully released, it would be enough to instantly freeze a prefecture of the Xuanhuang Realm."

"I believe that even within the current Myriad Immortals Alliance, this sword would be a treasure of considerable value."

"However..." Li Ping looked at the other Myriad Year Icebound Sword in his hand. He could discern no difference.

"This square box easily completed the replication." Li Ping’s thoughts churned.

As Li Ping was contemplating, the small square box squirmed and transformed back into its kitten form. It seemed to have expended a great deal of energy, appearing somewhat listless. It yawned, and clearly didn’t intend to leave, napping directly on Li Ping’s shoulder. This was clearly not an act; it had even lost interest in the golden Origin Force Li Ping had offered.

Li Ping did not drive it away either. Such a treasure was best kept close.

"Currently, it appears that when this treasure transforms into a square box, its function is replication."

"It can achieve complete replication of items. This treasure seems to be in its growth phase, and some things cannot be replicated yet. Furthermore, each replication consumes a great deal of energy and requires a period of rest and adjustment."

"Moreover, this treasure is not limited to just the square box and cat forms. It likely has other transformations..." Li Ping stroked the sleeping kitten, which responded with a weak meow.

"Interesting."

"It was worth my painstaking efforts in setting the trap; the fishing pond has finally given me a surprise."

"Since its manifestation was a cat-shaped statue, let's call it [Cat Treasure]." When Cat Treasure was fished out, it was merely a common white light cluster. But clearly, Cat Treasure, with its [Replication] ability, could not possibly be of only white quality.

"Although it’s possible it wasn’t activated initially. But regardless, it even managed to deceive the Immortal Treasure fishing pond."

"The origin of [Cat Treasure] is highly unusual."

"It might even come from beyond the high wall..." Li Ping’s figure flickered, returning to the Saint Emperor’s Throne.

"This [Cat Treasure] will be a great asset in my struggle against the Myriad Immortals Alliance."

...

In the Sun family’s secret chamber.

Li Fan’s main body and other soul fragments had already learned of Cat Treasure’s existence. However, in this life, Cat Treasure could exert its greatest value in the hands of the Saint Emperor, so there was no rush to exchange it using the anchor point.

"Furthermore, it is still in its infancy. Its ultimate potential remains to be observed."

"Besides man-made magic treasures, could it replicate Xuanhuang Realm’s natural wonders, or even existences like the Ultimate Dissolution Disc?" Li Fan pondered. If it could, it would merely accelerate his collection progress. Wasn’t each of his returns to reality akin to replicating the entire world?

With this thought, Li Fan’s initially turbulent state of mind instantly calmed.

Returning his thoughts to the Sun family’s side.

The Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters had lifted its lockdown. Sun Luyao had been summoned by the Mirror Master Fu for a detailed consultation. However, the matter of the colorful rainbow capable of escaping the Xuanhuang Realm remained under the strictest level of secrecy. Despite the dual probing of the Heavenly Profound Mirror origin and the Boundless Mirror, nothing could be detected.

Li Fan was not in a hurry. There was no wall that couldn’t be breached. Even the strongest protective measures would eventually fail over time. His task was to wait patiently. Moreover, he was not the only one in the Myriad Immortals Alliance interested in the colorful rainbow. Using the Heavenly Profound Mirror, he could constantly monitor the Myriad Immortals Alliance. As long as they discovered this secret through any means, it meant Li Fan would also know.

"Senior, that method you mentioned to resolve the wind disaster, can it really work?" Sun Luyao, who had always been fearful of Li Fan, suddenly spoke up.

"Yes." Before Li Fan could reply, Sun Luyao quickly explained.

"Recently, for some reason, strange scenes have been flashing in my mind. They are all things I haven't experienced before. After much thought, they are most likely remnants of the annihilating wind disaster..."

At the signal from Li Fan’s divine sense, Sun Luyao projected the scenes he had seen. The images were blurry and changed too rapidly. Li Fan could only discern scenes of countless beings instantly turning to dust. And the methods displayed by those beings on the brink of life and death... Seemed beyond the capabilities of ordinary cultivators.

"Scenes of the Immortal Realm’s great tribulation." Li Fan mused inwardly, but outwardly showed no sign of gravity.

He snorted coldly, "Don't scare yourself. Do you think what you’ve gone through is the true annihilating wind tribulation? It's merely a remnant passed down through countless generations."

"Don’t worry. As long as your brother can find clues about the You Clan, I have a ninety percent chance of helping you expel it." Such confident words instantly reassured Sun Luyao. In his view, the mysterious senior’s displayed methods were likely comparable to legendary True Immortals.

Sun Luyuan did not keep them waiting long. Three days later, he quietly returned to the secret chamber. Unlike his previous somber demeanor, his face was now filled with unconcealed joy.

"Brother, have you found clues about the You Clan?" Sun Luyao asked.

Sun Luyuan shook his head: "We are still investigating that, but I believe we will have leads soon."

"Then you..." Sun Luyuan lowered his voice, unable to conceal his excitement: "Law Transmission Heavenly Venerate communicated with the Myriad Immortals Alliance this time and also conducted a sweep of the Immortal Alliance headquarters, issuing relevant directives and carrying out personnel adjustments."

"That old fellow Fu, because his strength hasn't improved much over the years, was apparently singled out for criticism by Law Transmission himself. He is extremely anxious and will be in closed-door cultivation for a long time, so he won’t be able to bother us for a while." Sun Luyao was also delighted to hear this.

"By the way, when the Heavenly Venerate inspected the Immortal Alliance, did he discover the human avatar of the Heavenly Profound Mirror?" Sun Luyao asked.

"That, I'm not sure. However, judging from the current situation, it seems he did not discover it."

"I have also been monitoring the human avatar of the Heavenly Profound Mirror, and there are no abnormalities for the time being."

Chapter 1226: New Laws of the Darkest Sea

Although Zhao Wuji did not explicitly state the method of stripping talent, judging from the fact that those so-called geniuses from the Academy who had appeared in the past had disappeared from public view, their fate was likely not good.

What was most critical was that Zhao Xian had not encountered anything related to this in his dreams, which made him, who thought he could foresee the future, feel a slight, uncontrollable panic for the first time.

However, he was no longer the naive youth he once was. He quickly calmed down, a cold energy surging from his heart. He thought rapidly: "Indeed, exposing one's talent will attract the scrutiny of the Academy's higher-ups, and might even cost him his life. But crises often come with opportunities. It's no longer the era when the Academy could utterly dominate. The Xuanxian Boat is facing great changes. The Immortal Severing Tower and the Immortal Pivot Court are fiercely competing for control of the Xuanxian Boat's future. I believe even the Dao Proving Academy will have to consider the impact of this conflict on the future of the Xuanxian Boat."

"Talent is merely talent. As long as I can continue to survive, there will never be a shortage of geniuses." Zhao Xian felt his thoughts becoming unprecedentedly clear, as if something was guiding him, sifting through the messy clues to deduce the correct future.

"If I cower and hesitate, the Xuanxian Boat will still head towards destruction. Only by confronting the three major powers of the Xuanxian Boat and seeking survival in the midst of death can I lead the Xuanxian Boat to find a way to live."

At this thought, the fear in Zhao Xian's eyes completely disappeared, and his aura calmed down from its previous chaos. Zhao Wuji looked at his disciple's transformation with astonishment, not understanding why.

Zhao Xian took a deep breath and responded somberly, "I, as a subordinate, dedicate myself to benefiting others; a sage dedicates himself to benefiting the world. I have received the Academy's favor, and it has led me to where I am today. If my talent is useful to the Academy, then take it! What do I have to regret?"

"Conversely, if I were to cultivate using the Academy's resources and deliberately hide it, wouldn't that be ungrateful?"

These words, spoken with righteous indignation and standing on a moral high ground, left Zhao Wuji completely unable to refute. He looked at the young disciple, as if truly seeing him for the first time. Zhao Xian's sincere and firm gaze made Zhao Wuji feel ashamed.

The two stood in silence, confronting each other. Finally, Zhao Wuji conceded. "Fine. Since you have such conviction, it makes me seem petty." Zhao Wuji sighed, looking dejected, and left.

Zhao Xian watched his master's retreating figure, a complex expression flashing across his face, before disappearing. "Xuanxian Boat, I must save it." The thought in his mind became increasingly firm.

Neither the master nor the disciple noticed that the reason for Zhao Xian's stubbornness was not his noble character or unwavering faith. It was purely because... a clone hidden in his sea of consciousness was acting up.

"Interesting. I didn't expect the Dao Proving Academy to have methods to usurp others' talents. As expected of a civilization that survived in the Darkest Star Sea at the end, it indeed has its merits."

"Whether it's the secrets of the Dao Proving Academy or the control of the True Immortal Script by the Immortal Pivot Court and the Immortal Severing Tower, they are all valuable to me. How could I possibly let this brat Zhao Xian back down? Besides, with me around, it's not so easy to harm him."

The news of Zhao Xian's rapid breakthrough to the Golden Core realm in a short period spread throughout the Academy within three days. The Academy had not produced such a genius in a long time, and with the impending storm, under the instigation of some interested parties, Zhao Xian's reputation quickly spread beyond the Academy, becoming more and more exaggerated.

From barely breaking through to Golden Core, it became directly Golden Core, perfected in seven days. Finally, it escalated to the exaggerated degree of Half-step Nascent Soul. At this point, even those who knew the truth and tried to clarify became useless. Outsiders would only consider it as the Academy trying to cover up the story of such an unparalleled genius.

The Immortal Severing Tower and the Immortal Pivot Court both sent people to inquire about Zhao Xian's background. Within the Academy, there were also disagreements on how to handle this cultivation genius, who appeared once in several hundred years.

Amidst the surging tide, Zhao Xian became even more resolute, casting aside all distractions. He wisely hid in a secret chamber specially cleared for him by the Academy, focusing on accelerating his cultivation as much as possible.

"I don't need to worry about the spiritual energy being insufficient. This is truly enjoyable. Is this the treatment of a true disciple of the Academy?"

"Moreover, until a final decision is made regarding my fate, I can enjoy most of the Academy's resources for free."

His divine sense strength soared, converting into his cultivation base. As his realm improved, it in turn nourished his divine sense, causing it to grow stronger. This formed a perfect cycle, allowing Zhao Xian's cultivation speed to reach an unimaginable level. Especially since there were no bottlenecks or obstacles whatsoever.

Zhao Xian felt his heart as solid as rock. No distracting thoughts or inner demons could affect him in the slightest. "I didn't cultivate this quickly even in my dreams. Am I really a genius?"

"My previous slow progress was simply due to a lack of resources and not finding the right cultivation technique?" Zhao Xian couldn't help but think this.

At this moment, Li Fan's clone, which had been blocking all his inner demons, was slightly overstretched. Even with the Immortal Heart Curse's blessing, these breaking-prohibition inner demons were not easy to deal with. The vividly realistic illusions he experienced, although Li Fan could maintain his self-awareness, still took considerable effort to escape from each time. Especially since the process of fighting the inner demons seemed to be recorded, making the next encounter even stronger. Ultimately, it was only a clone, and some wear and tear was normal.

"One can imagine the difficulty of advancing in cultivation before the laws of the Darkest Star Sea were shattered."

"No wonder the new method is feasible in the Xuanhuang Realm. It seems that in normal circumstances, the new method should also be able to be cultivated normally in this star sea."

"The corresponding requirements will need to be magnified to the scale of the star sea..."

"Foundation wonders, Golden Core methods, Nascent Soul heavens, etc., are all manifestations of world laws. The Darkest Star Sea's laws are shattered, filled with the power of True Immortal Glyphs."

"Conversely, these True Immortal Glyphs are the current manifestations of the Darkest Star Sea's laws." A flash of inspiration struck Li Fan's mind, as if he had grasped some crucial clue.

"Does Law Transmission Heavenly Venerate have any connection with this rapidly rising Immortal Severing Tower?"

"What is his purpose in summoning sixteen Harmonious Dao cultivators to the Darkest Star Sea?"

"Also, when I first came to this place full of remnants, the cultivator I encountered... was not from the Xuanxian Boat. There should be other cultivation civilizations here. Is it the Merchant Immortal Boat, or is it related to Law Transmission?"

Li Fan's thoughts were disturbed by the intense energy fluctuations within Zhao Xian. A vortex of spiritual energy formed above Zhao Xian's head, being frantically drawn into his body. And in his dantian, the slightly purplish Golden Core showed cracks, as if something was gestating within.

After two months of frantic secluded cultivation, Zhao Xian entered the Nascent Soul stage! However, this Nascent Soul... was not the vibrant infant image seen in Li Fan's ancient texts from the Xuanhuang Realm, but directly a miniature version of the real Zhao Xian. It even looked older than Zhao Xian himself.

Observing closely, Li Fan found that the age at which this Nascent Soul manifested seemed to have a mystical significance. "Is it predetermined fate? Zhao Xian's innate limitation to break through to the next realm. That is to say, before reaching the age for the Nascent Soul manifestation, Zhao Xian cannot break through to the Divine Transformation realm?"

After a long while, Li Fan had a vague guess. "This is considered... a different kind of bottleneck? I've never heard of such a thing in the records of the Xuanhuang Realm. I just don't know if this predetermined lifespan can be altered."

Zhao Xian, who had finally emerged from his seclusion, also discovered the abnormality of his Nascent Soul. His rapid progress had caused his mental state to be slightly unstable, and it took him a while to accept this fact. He secretly sought out Zhao Wuji to inquire.

"What? You've already formed your Nascent Soul?" This time, Zhao Wuji wasn't shocked, but rather terrified. The Academy hadn't even finished discussing how to handle Zhao Xian's Golden Core breakthrough, and he had already reached the Nascent Soul stage! Wouldn't all the previous discussions be rendered useless? "How could this be?"

Only when he saw the slightly aged miniature version of Zhao Xian emerging from his body did Zhao Wuji completely believe it. "Judging by your condition, you have a good chance of reaching Divine Transformation within ten years. This..." Zhao Wuji stared blankly for a while, not knowing what to say.

"No, I can't make this decision. I must directly inform the Palace Master." Zhao Wuji fled as if escaping, his figure appearing very disheveled.

Li Fan's clone took this opportunity to temporarily transfer to Zhao Wuji. Zhao Xian would definitely be strictly investigated soon. He was not clear about the strength of the Dao Proving Academy's Palace Master, so it was better to avoid the limelight for now.

Zhao Wuji rushed to the top floor of the Academy and pushed open the door. Three white-haired old men were present, all looking at the agitated Zhao Wuji with surprise. "Zhao Xian has formed his Nascent Soul."

A single sentence caused all three old men's expressions to slightly change. As Li Fan had predicted, they could no longer bother with the communicative Zhao Wuji. They flickered and appeared directly beside Zhao Xian.

When Zhao Wuji saw Zhao Xian again, it was seven days later. He had just formed his Nascent Soul, but his aura had already completely stabilized.

"The Palace Master reviewed the recording of our meeting that day. Because of my impassioned words, the Palace Master ultimately abandoned the original plan and decided to truly nurture me."

"Geniuses are not uncommon. But those who are talented and absolutely loyal are rare." Zhao Xian said to Zhao Wuji. Zhao Wuji recalled the events of the past few days and felt a sense of unreality.

"However, Master, what you said was not entirely wrong. If I were still at the Golden Core stage, I would probably have been refined into a Dao Pill and swallowed by the Palace Master by now. Fortunately, I was a step faster and sought survival in the face of death. After all, the Palace Master is also nearing his limit. The Academy needs a successor." Zhao Xian whispered.

"This is also the last time I will call you Master." Zhao Wuji watched Zhao Xian's retreating figure, feeling a sense of loss.

Li Fan's clone then transferred to Zhao Xian. As the Academy's successor, Zhao Xian's treatment had changed dramatically compared to before. Not only did he reside in the secondary highest level of the Academy, but he also gained access to many secrets that were previously unattainable. For example, the true power system of the Xuanxian Boat.

One of the three elders of the Academy, a cultivator named [Yu Shuo], personally taught Zhao Xian. "Nascent Soul, Divine Transformation, Harmonious Dao. These realms are merely superficial."

"In the face of the pervasive True Immortal energy filling the star sea, they fundamentally have no difference. The so-called higher strength is merely living a little longer."

"Those who are destined to die will still die." Seeing Zhao Xian's confused expression, which showed a severe impact on his worldview, Yu Shuo continued with a smile, "Our Dao Proving Academy is worthy of the name [Dao Proving] because we were the first to discover a method to avoid the harm of True Immortal power and even utilize it."

"We call it the [Path Entering Method]."

"Path Entering Method?" Zhao Xian was still confused.

"Legend has it that every True Immortal has their own unique [Dao]. The Darkest Star Sea we are in is filled with the unique powers of True Immortals. Mortals, to avoid being affected by True Immortals, must enter the Dao with their bodies." As Yu Shuo spoke, his body underwent a strange transformation. His appearance flickered for no reason. From a white-haired, kindly old man, he turned into a naive child, then suddenly into an ambitious youth. Not only his appearance, but his body and aura were constantly changing.

"Once you enter the path of a True Immortal, not only can you avoid harm, but you can also largely block out the True Immortal powers from other parts of the star sea." Yu Shuo returned to his original appearance, saying proudly, "This is also the method used by the Immortal Pivot Court and most of the upper-level cultivators of the Immortal Boat."

After some thought, Zhao Xian astutely pointed out the key issue. "Does the Path Entering Method have any flaws? Did the Immortal Severing Tower find a new way to utilize True Immortal power?"

Yu Shuo nodded, showing a look of approval. "The power of True Immortals is not something anyone can dabble in. Mortals who wish to control it not only have strict requirements on their physique and aptitude but also need special materials and methods to proceed gradually. If ordinary people come into contact with too much at once, they will only suffer death and destruction."

"Old Yu, are you referring to the relics of world destruction?" Zhao Xian suddenly remembered something and quickly asked.

"Correct. And only the relics where the remaining power of True Immortals is about to dissipate, and which are at their weakest, will yield the best results."

"As for why the Immortal Severing Tower can contend with the Immortal Pivot Court in such a short time, it is said they have found a method to absorb the relics of world destruction harmlessly and perfectly." Yu Shuo's tone held a hint of disbelief.

Chapter 1227: I Enter the True Immortal Path

"I have also seen the cultivator from the Immortal Severing Tower who reputedly entered the Dao using the new method. It is said he achieved Dao in only three years, and his ability to control True Immortal power is no less than mine." Yu Shuo's tone was inscrutable.

"If that is the case, why do you still seem to have doubts?"

"Because all the cultivators in the Immortal Severing Tower who have reportedly [Entered Dao] and appeared in public so far, all control the same type of True Immortal power." Yu Shuo's tone was melancholy.

"What does that prove?" Zhao Xian was somewhat confused.

Yu Shuo glanced at Zhao Xian, his expression inscrutable.

After a long silence, he finally spoke calmly, "Zhao Xian, you must remember this. When dealing with True Immortal power, never let your guard down."

"The deeper you enter the Dao, the more dangerous you yourself become." Yu Shuo did not explain directly but said this unexpectedly.

"Today's lesson ends here. Next time, it will be Nangong Lai."

Yu Shuo's figure disappeared along with his voice.

Zhao Xian remained in place, pondering Yu Shuo's last sentence.

A flash of inspiration struck his mind, making him instantly understand the underlying meaning.

"True Immortal power is like a net. By borrowing the True Immortal net, although one can wield True Immortal power, the result is only getting deeper and deeper..."

The sudden realization of this principle was like a basin of cold water drenching Zhao Xian, leaving him chilled to the bone.

"If that's the case, then our Dao Proving Academy, and even the entire Xuanxian Boat, are not..."

But soon, Zhao Xian gave a bitter smile.

"For survival, it's a necessary evil. After all, survival is the top priority for the Immortal Boat. Moreover, we have been adrift in the star sea for so many years, only seeing the remnants of True Immortal power, not the True Immortals themselves. The risk is indeed there, but it can be temporarily disregarded."

At the same time, Zhao Xian understood why Yu Shuo found the Immortal Severing Tower peculiar. In the Darkest Star Sea, the remnants of True Immortal power were mixed. If they had truly mastered the method to absorb the relics of world destruction harmlessly and perfectly, then the Path Entering manifestations of the Immortal Severing Tower cultivators should also show various states. After all, not everyone could adapt to the same True Immortal remnant power.

In the Darkest Star Sea, there were no less than five types of True Immortal powers known to the Immortal Boat. Each of the three leaders of the Dao Proving Academy had a different path of entering Dao. However, the six Path Entering cultivators of the Immortal Severing Tower who had appeared so far, all displayed the same type of Path Entering power. While this possibility existed, it was extremely small.

"Either this technique they mastered is only effective against a single type of True Immortal power."

"Or else..."

Zhao Xian's heart turned cold, daring not to think further.

Currently, his task from the Academy was to stabilize his Nascent Soul cultivation first, and then attempt to reach Divine Transformation.

"Path Entering should not be attempted too early, nor too late."

"If one comes into contact with True Immortal power too early, a frail soul and will would almost certainly be unable to withstand the immense power of True Immortals, most likely leading to madness or becoming a deformed monster."

"But if it's too late..."

"The traditional Harmonious Dao realm, when merged with the residual Heavenly Dao laws of this star sea, would create a strong repulsion with the True Immortal Dao. The difficulty of attempting to [Enter Dao] would increase by several times."

The teachings of the Dao Proving Academy Palace Master, Nangong Lie, echoed in Zhao Xian's mind.

"The Academy will not press too hard for now. The immediate priority is to quickly improve my strength."

"Although the Tribulation of Trapped Nascent Soul indicated that I can only break through after fifty, the Palace Master said that the limitations of the shattered star sea's residual Heavenly Dao are not absolute. With the Academy's foundation and the accumulation from my dreams, it's not impossible to defy fate."

Zhao Xian was very confident in this.

In fact, many details in the future dream Zhao Xian had initially experienced already differed greatly from reality. Normally, if Zhao Xian were more meticulous, he should have noticed these discrepancies long ago. However, under the continuous subtle influence of a certain entity, Zhao Xian had intentionally or unintentionally ignored all the inconsistencies. Let alone ordinary Nascent Soul cultivators, even the three top figures of the Dao Proving Academy of the Xuanxian Boat, their methods of manipulating people were likely far inferior to Li Fan's.

And at this moment, Li Fan's clone was using Zhao Xian's authority to browse through all sorts of secret knowledge within the Dao Proving Academy. Records related to True Immortal power were all hidden and inaccessible. However, there was not much concealment regarding the history of the Xuanxian Boat. Consistent with his previous understanding, the Xuanxian Boat originated from the split of the ancient Immortal Boat [Xuan Shang].

More details revealed that the primary cause of the internal strife within the Immortal Boat was an outsider. Appearing as an outsider, he quickly gained the trust of over half of the Immortal Boat's population. He even misguided them into attempting to cross the invisible high wall that sealed off the Darkest Star Sea. At the critical moment, an Immortal Boat cultivator named Cai Zhengjun, who later became the first head of the Immortal Pivot Court of the Xuanxian Boat, timely led the masses to prevent this suicidal act. However, it ultimately led to a war between the two factions, and the Immortal Boat was broken. The outsider was only briefly mentioned, his true identity remaining a mystery.

Regarding the situation in the Darkest Star Sea, the Dao Proving Academy had many detailed descriptions. Besides the spatio-temporal charts recorded during the Xuanxian Boat's drifting and fleeing over the years, the Immortal Boat also had unique theories about the Sea of Relics and the High Wall.

"Further into the Sea of Relics, near the invisible High Wall, lies the graveyard of myriad realms, the burial ground of the star sea. The terrifying suction from the center of the star sea spans across the star sea, but is blocked by the High Wall. Over time, coupled with the mysterious influence of the High Wall, the suction, like tides, becomes fixed, forming a reverse force field."

"The closer one gets to the High Wall, the stronger the suction becomes. After dozens of explorations by the Immortal Boat, all ending in failure, they have currently given up on further investigation."

...

Li Fan was overjoyed to unexpectedly find this report. Perhaps due to its special location, the Xuanxian Boat's understanding of the overall situation in the star sea was far superior to that of the Xuanhuang Realm.

"Under the High Wall, the tides are locked, world fragments?" Li Fan's mind seemed to conjure an image of boundless, continuous broken worlds in a desolate, silent scene.

"So, what I previously thought to be an existence comparable to the suction of the Immortal Ruins in the depths of the star sea is merely a reflection of the High Wall's suction on the Darkest Star Sea?"

Although slightly disappointed, Li Fan was rather relieved. After all, as long as it wasn't another True Immortal, everything was manageable.

"The invisible High Wall can block all the power of the [Hunger] mantra, and even cause it to converge in reverse."

"What kind of incredible power is this?"

Chapter 1228: Outsider on the Immortal Boat

Li Fan had personally witnessed the true power of the Hunger mantra in the Immortal Ruins. Therefore, regarding the High Wall that could firmly contain the suction of the star sea, Li Fan felt an inexplicable sense of awe. Then, his curiosity became uncontrollable.

"It's a pity that the Xuanxian Boat's exploration of the other side of the star sea also stopped over two thousand years ago. With the changes in time and space, the charts recorded back then can only be used as a reference; they are not of much practical value."

Li Fan recalled the great upheaval in the Xuanhuang Realm not long ago. "It seems that Law Transmission and Heavenly Physician, their main areas of activity in the star sea are in that graveyard of world fragments."

"Under the High Wall, something seems to have gone wrong, causing the suction, which has always been stable, to erupt towards the interior of the Darkest Star Sea." Li Fan's thoughts raced.

"Law Transmission could notify the Myriad Immortals Alliance in advance, which indicates that this matter is definitely related to Him. And his summoning of those sixteen Harmonious Dao cultivators here is likely also related to this."

Thinking of this, Li Fan's heart stirred: "If I wait here, I might actually be able to wait for that colorful rainbow."

"Based on the time it took me to cross the star sea and the speed of the colorful rainbow's flight..."

"If I can indeed encounter it, it should be within these few days."

...

After reading the most important parts, Li Fan began to sort out other valuable gains. Not only could this life help Great Qi's uprising proceed more smoothly, but it would also be of great help to Li Fan in his future reincarnations.

Among them, the most important to Li Fan was the refinement of the [Dao Pill].

In the difficult years immediately following the fracturing of the Immortal Boat, the Xuanxian Boat cultivators, facing extreme scarcity of resources, accumulated considerable cannibalistic experience. The prototype of the Dao Pill originated from that period. With limited resources, how to maximize absorption efficiency became the most crucial concern for Xuanxian Boat cultivators at that time.

The Dao Pill, a secret technique that refines cultivators into pills, was the pinnacle of experience summarized from the historical period of darkness in the Immortal Boat. It not only refined the opponent cultivator's memories and souls for one's own use but also integrated their talents, temperaments, and innate divine abilities!

Of course, side effects were unavoidable. The stronger the raw material for refining the Dao Pill, the more significant the side effects. If one's own strength was insufficient and they forcibly consumed it, they would be unable to withstand the influx and could easily suffer a backlash, becoming neither human nor ghost. In their madness, they would disregard all ties and engage in indiscriminate slaughter.

Therefore, after the Xuanxian Boat gradually stabilized, this Dao Pill secret technique became one of the Immortal Boat's forbidden arts, known only to the core of the Immortal Boat.

"It's quite complex." Li Fan studied the entire refining process in detail, frowning slightly. The root of this secret technique was still alchemy. Alchemy was not Li Fan's strong suit, but his formation skills were already superb. The Dissolution Disc simultaneously parsed, disassembled, and converted each step into corresponding formations.

"As long as this formation is set up, the entire Dao Pill refining process can be automated, saving trouble and effort."

"Although I am not too concerned about innate talents anymore, I have still mastered another special means."

"It is also very useful for deterring those so-called prodigies."

"The only concern is whether this method is effective in the Xuanhuang Realm." The two ends of the star sea not only had different time flows. The Xuanxian Boat, exposed to the chaotic and disordered Darkest Star Sea, lacked the protection of primordial world power. Li Fan dared not guarantee that the rules here would also be effective in the Xuanhuang Realm.

"I'll know if I have a chance to try."

Besides the Dao Pill, what else mattered to Li Fan was a communication method that could minimize interference from the remaining True Immortal forces in the star sea. It was created by the second head of the Immortal Pivot Court, named [Boundless].

Its principle was to generate a power that "resisted" the remaining True Immortal forces, based on the residual Heavenly Dao attributes in the star sea. However, its shortcomings were also obvious. It required knowledge of the opponent's specific spatio-temporal coordinates. Moreover, due to the ubiquitous suction in the Darkest Star Sea, this communication was often only one-way, following the direction of the suction. The Xuanxian Boat had almost no records of other survivors in the Darkest Star Sea. Therefore, this Boundless communication method was not valued at all.

But for Li Fan, it could serve a different purpose.

Outside the Xuanxian Boat, in the Sea of Relics. Li Fan, the Saint Embryo, who was comprehending the Heavenly Dao of the Darkest Star Sea, suddenly opened his eyes. A playful look flashed in his eyes, and he immediately shot a silver beam towards the direction of the Xuanhuang Realm he sensed.

"If cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm receive this message, their reaction should be quite interesting." However, this was just Li Fan's momentary whim. The Xuanxian Boat was too far from the Xuanhuang Realm, and it was also very close to the Immortal Ruins. Li Fan was actually not sure if this Boundless communication could successfully reach the Xuanhuang Realm. He was just doing it for fun.

The Saint Embryo had gained considerable rewards on the Xuanxian Boat; after all, it was the accumulation of a civilization. Even if it wasn't the absolute best part, it was still extremely precious to Li Fan.

Returning the perspective to the Xuanhuang Realm.

Since returning from Saint Dynasty Great Qi, Sun Luyuan had been exceptionally busy. He hadn't visited all the prodigies on the list, but he had investigated their general situations through his connections. Although Ou Shangtian hadn't urged him about the matter of subversion, Sun Luyuan deeply understood that this was his first task since joining Great Qi. Not only must it be successful, but it must also be done brilliantly, leaving no room for criticism, and even earning praise.

After careful selection, Sun Luyuan quickly decided on his sacrifice target to earn merit: the renowned Fairy Kongyou in the Myriad Immortals Alliance!

Fairy Kongyou was also at the Harmonious Dao realm. But in the eyes of ordinary cultivators in the Myriad Immortals Alliance, Kongyou was far more important than Sun Luyuan. Besides Kongyou's unparalleled beauty in the Myriad Immortals Alliance, she also possessed the complementary wondrous item [Yin Yang Jade]. Fairy Kongyou could fuse the Yang half of the [Yin Yang Jade] with her dao companion through the method of Yin Yang dual cultivation, thus elevating her dao companion's Foundation Wonder, Golden Core, Nascent Soul Heavenly Caves, and even subsequent transformations. It was enough to elevate a mediocre person to the rank of a prodigy, and a peerless prodigy to an existence that would shake the Xuanhuang Realm!

As early as during the Great Qi trip, Sun Luyuan heard that the few disciples under the Great Qi Saint Emperor were currently all without dao companions. If he could trick Kongyou over and facilitate a match, not only would it make subsequent subversion easier by leveraging Kongyou's fame, but it would also bestow a great favor upon the Saint Emperor's disciples. Wasn't it killing two birds with one stone?

Sun Luyuan's eyes narrowed, and a plan had already formed in his mind.

Chapter 1229: All Heavenly Talents Become Pills

All the Heavenly Prodigies Become Elixir

Li Fan had personally witnessed the true might of the Hunger Mantra in the Immortal Ruins. Therefore, he couldn't help but feel a sense of awe, mixed with uncontrollable curiosity, towards the high wall that could so firmly contain the suction of the star sea.
