"It's a pity that the Xuanxian Boat's exploration of the other side of the star sea also ceased over two thousand years ago. With the transformations of time and space, the charts recorded back then can only serve as a reference and are not of much practical value."

Li Fan then recalled the great upheaval in the Xuanhuang Realm not long ago. "It seems that Law Transmission and Heavenly Physician mainly operate in that graveyard of world fragments in the star sea."

"Something must have gone wrong beneath the high wall, causing the normally stable tidal suction to erupt towards the interior of the Darkest Star Sea." Li Fan's mind raced with thoughts.

"Law Transmission's ability to notify the Myriad Immortals Alliance in advance clearly indicates that this matter is inextricably linked to Him. And it's highly probable that his summoning of those sixteen Harmonious Dao cultivators here is also related to this."

Thinking this, Li Fan's heart stirred: "If I wait here, I might actually manage to catch sight of that colorful rainbow."

"Based on the time it took me to traverse the star sea and the speed of the colorful rainbow's flight..."

"If I do encounter it, it should be within these few days."

...

After finishing the most significant parts, Li Fan began to organize other valuable gains. Not only could this life assist Great Qi's uprising more smoothly, but it would also be of immense help to Li Fan in his future reincarnations.

Among these, the most crucial for Li Fan was the refinement of the [Dao Pill].

The Dao Pill, a secret technique for refining cultivators into pills, represented the pinnacle of experience summarized from the Xuanxian Boat's dark historical period. It not only allowed the user to refine and assimilate the memories and souls of other cultivators but also integrated their talents, temperaments, and innate divine abilities!

Of course, side effects were unavoidable. The stronger the raw material for refining the Dao Pill, the more pronounced the side effects. If one's own strength was insufficient and they forcibly consumed it, they would be unable to withstand the influx and could easily suffer a backlash, becoming neither human nor ghost. In their madness, they would disregard all ties and engage in indiscriminate slaughter.

Therefore, after the Xuanxian Boat gradually stabilized, this Dao Pill secret technique became one of the Immortal Boat's forbidden arts, known only to its core members.

"It's quite complex." Li Fan meticulously studied the entire refining process, frowning slightly. The root of this secret technique was still alchemy. Alchemy was not Li Fan's forte, but his mastery of formations was already superb. The Dissolution Disc simultaneously parsed, disassembled, and converted each step into corresponding formations.

"As long as this formation is set up, the entire Dao Pill refining process can be automated, saving trouble and effort."

"Although I am no longer particularly concerned about innate talents, I have still acquired another special method."

"It is also very useful for deterring those so-called prodigies."

"The only concern is whether this method will be effective in the Xuanhuang Realm." The two ends of the star sea not only had different time flows. The Xuanxian Boat, exposed to the chaotic and disordered Darkest Star Sea, lacked the protection of primordial world power. Li Fan dared not guarantee that the rules here would also be effective in the Xuanhuang Realm.

"I'll know if I have a chance to try."

Besides the Dao Pill, another aspect that caught Li Fan's attention was a communication method capable of minimizing interference from the remaining True Immortal forces in the star sea. It was created by the second head of the Immortal Pivot Court, named [Boundless].

Its principle was to generate a power that "resisted" the remaining True Immortal forces, based on the residual Heavenly Dao attributes in the star sea. However, its shortcomings were also obvious. It required knowledge of the opponent's specific spatial-temporal coordinates. Moreover, due to the ubiquitous suction in the Darkest Star Sea, this communication was often only one-way, following the direction of the suction. The Xuanxian Boat had almost no records of other survivors in the Darkest Star Sea. Therefore, this Boundless communication method was not valued at all.

But for Li Fan, it could serve a different purpose.

Outside the Xuanxian Boat, in the Sea of Relics. Li Fan, the Saint Embryo, who was comprehending the Heavenly Dao of the Darkest Star Sea, suddenly opened his eyes. A playful look flashed in his eyes, and he immediately shot a silver beam towards the direction of the Xuanhuang Realm he sensed.

"If cultivators in the Xuanhuang Realm receive this message, their reaction should be quite interesting." However, this was merely a momentary whim of Li Fan's. The Xuanxian Boat was too far from the Xuanhuang Realm, and also very close to the Immortal Ruins. Li Fan was actually unsure if this Boundless communication could successfully reach the Xuanhuang Realm. He was just doing it for fun.

The Saint Embryo had gained considerable rewards on the Xuanxian Boat; after all, it was the accumulation of a civilization. Even if it wasn't the absolute pinnacle, it was still extremely precious to Li Fan.

Returning the perspective to the Xuanhuang Realm.

Since his return from Saint Dynasty Great Qi, Sun Luyuan had been exceptionally busy. He hadn't visited all the prodigies on the list, but he had investigated their general situations through his connections. Although Ou Shangtian hadn't explicitly urged him about the matter of subversion, Sun Luyuan deeply understood that this was his primary task since joining Great Qi. Not only must it be successful, but it must also be executed brilliantly, leaving no room for criticism, and even earning praise.

After careful selection, Sun Luyuan quickly decided on his target for a meritorious deed: the renowned Fairy Kongyou of the Myriad Immortals Alliance!

Fairy Kongyou was also at the Harmonious Dao realm, but in the eyes of ordinary cultivators in the Myriad Immortals Alliance, Kongyou was far more significant than Sun Luyuan. Besides Kongyou's unparalleled beauty within the Myriad Immortals Alliance, she also possessed the complementary wondrous item, the [Yin Yang Jade]. Fairy Kongyou could fuse the Yang half of the [Yin Yang Jade] with her dao companion through the method of Yin Yang dual cultivation, thus elevating her dao companion's Foundation Wonder, Golden Core, Nascent Soul Heavenly Caves, and even subsequent transformations. It was enough to elevate a mediocre person to the rank of a prodigy, and a peerless prodigy to an existence that would shake the Xuanhuang Realm!

As early as during the Great Qi expedition, Sun Luyuan had heard that the few disciples under the Great Qi Saint Emperor were currently all without dao companions. If he could trick Kongyou over and facilitate a match, not only would it make subsequent subversion easier by leveraging Kongyou's fame, but it would also bestow a great favor upon the Saint Emperor's disciples. Wasn't that killing two birds with one stone?

Sun Luyuan narrowed his eyes, a plan already forming in his mind.

Chapter 1230: Body Absorbing the World's Evil Thoughts

The Fairy Kongyou, possessing unparalleled beauty, had numerous suitors within the Myriad Immortals Alliance. The heaven-defying efficacy of the Yin Yang Jade was enough to drive all cultivators under heaven into a frenzy.

Apart from her unique qualities, Kongyou also seemed to possess a hidden background.

Whispers among the higher echelons of the Immortal Alliance suggested that Kongyou was a forbidden plaything of a certain Law Transmission Lord. Not only did she originate from a private world reserved for Law Transmitters, but even her half of the Heavenly Wonder, the Yin Yang Jade, was implanted within her. The intention was to harvest her later after she had matured.

As the saying goes, where there's smoke, there's fire. These rumors were not without basis.

The Heavenly Soul of Earth and Heaven, "Dark Hues," which Kongyou used for her integration with the Dao, was one of the many reserves held and nurtured by the Myriad Immortals Alliance. Kongyou had quietly used it for her breakthrough without any official comment from the Alliance.

Furthermore, over thirty years ago, a cultivator named Qin, who had just ascended to the Harmonious Dao realm, was instantly smitten with Kongyou. After his ardent pursuit failed, he resorted to schemes and intrigue to forcibly possess her. The result was that not only he, but also his once-prominent Qin family, vanished from the world, ceasing to exist.

Sun Luyuan was not deterred by Kongyou's potentially special status; instead, it strengthened his resolve to choose her as the sacrifice. He went to his brother, Sun Luyao, intending to use the power of the Heavenly Profound Mirror to pinpoint her current location.

"Brother, are you not afraid of doing this...?" Sun Luyao asked, somewhat bewildered.

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance is completely unaware of Saint Dynasty Great Qi at present. What trouble could arise from me merely inviting the famously renowned Fairy Kongyou to admire the scenery in a particularly picturesque small world within the Immortal Alliance?" Sun Luyuan chuckled.

"A figure like Fairy Kongyou would face absolutely no life-threatening danger within Saint Dynasty Great Qi. You can rest assured about this."

There were, however, some ulterior motives that Sun Luyuan did not disclose to his brother.

Aside from currying favor with the Saint Dynasty, he also wished to use Fairy Kongyou's backing to test Great Qi's strength. While his previous visit to Great Qi had indeed demonstrated the Saint Dynasty's power, a real contest was still needed.

"If I cannot even deal with a single Law Transmitter, how can I speak of contending with the Myriad Immortals Alliance?" Sun Luyuan mused inwardly.

Unbeknownst to Sun Luyuan, every one of his actions was being observed by the Saint Emperor of Great Qi.

How could he, in his self-perceived stealth, possibly deceive Li Fan, who had experienced countless reincarnations?

"Fairy Kongyou." A peerlessly beautiful visage flashed through the mind of Saint Emperor Li Ping.

"Very well. My disciples are indeed getting on in years. If they can produce some more prodigies for my Great Qi, it would be a joyous occasion."

As for the power behind Kongyou, Li Ping truly did not pay much heed.

However, Sun Luyuan's self-proclaimed clever stratagem earned him a special mark from Li Ping.

"All deeds done today will be repaid."

Such a minor event was merely one of countless scenes flickering through the mind of the Faceless Saint Emperor as he sat on the Saint Emperor's Throne.

It did not stir the slightest ripple in his heart.

Li Ping's primary focus remained on guiding the [Netherworld] and deducing the new cultivation method.

Ever since a portion of the Nether Race members were dispatched to replenish the energy deficiency in the Dark Sea, Li Ping felt an increasing degree of favor from the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.

Not long after assisting Tian Yang in his Harmonious Dao breakthrough, the amount of world power he could manipulate and draw upon had increased by dozens of times compared to before.

While he grasped more control, a certain inexplicable urgency originating from the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao appeared more frequently in Li Ping's mind.

As the hope for the future of the tens of billions of citizens of Great Qi rested on this incarnation, Li Ping naturally did not act rashly.

Before his eyes flashed images from the Heavenly Dao's perception.

A scene of a desolate Gobi desert. Everything in sight was a hazy gray.

A towering stone mountain, seemingly connecting heaven and earth, stood in the center of the scene.

An old man sat atop the stone mountain.

Behind the old man was a coffin. Although it was merely a perceived image, Li Ping could still detect an aura of decay and malevolence emanating from the coffin.

It even caused Li Ping a slight discomfort.

"The sealed malice of the Xuanhuang Realm."

Li Ping naturally knew the reason for the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao's constant urging.

A part of itself was sealed, drastically weakening its strength. As a result, after the "Law Cannot Be Cultivated Simultaneously" tribulation thousands of years ago, it had been unable to unleash any methods targeting cultivators.

If this lost power could be recovered, perhaps the situation could turn around.

But...

Even across hundreds of millions of miles, Li Ping seemed to feel the unsettling presence beneath the coffin lid.

"If this malice is allowed to return, after being sealed by cultivators for so many years and suppressed for so long, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao would undoubtedly undergo extreme changes. This might not necessarily be a good thing for human cultivators, or even for the Xuanhuang Realm itself."

"However, the value of replenishing the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao power is indeed substantial."

In an instant, Saint Emperor Li Ping made his decision.

He would absorb this portion of malice first.

When he had reshaped the universe in the future and reintegrated into the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, this power would naturally return to the Xuanhuang Realm.

Until then, the control of this power by him, as opposed to the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao...

In Li Ping's view, there was no significant difference.

With Li Ping's current strength, subduing the Xuanhuang malice still carried certain risks. Especially the cultivator named Xu Ke, who guarded the Xuanhuang malice, could not be assessed by ordinary standards.

Therefore, without thorough preparation, Li Ping would not act rashly.

He merely feigned ignorance of the Xuanhuang Realm's urging.

When dealing with world power, there was actually someone in Saint Dynasty Great Qi who served as a worthy example.

Venerable Yin.

As a residual soul manifestation from another cultivation world, Venerable Yin possessed extensive experience in battling world consciousness.

However, there seemed to be some taboo involved.

Li Ping sent inquiries several times, but Venerable Yin, uncharacteristically, remained tight-lipped and unresponsive.

Fortunately, he was also busy researching potential breakthroughs for the new cultivation method, so Li Ping did not press the matter.

"The will of the world..."

Without Venerable Yin's assistance, Li Ping could only rely on himself to find a solution.

In his memories, the Xuanhuang Realm still harbored numerous fragments from other cultivation worlds, which still retained their own consciousness.

Perhaps interacting with them could yield some gains.

With this thought, Li Ping's figure flickered, and he arrived outside the entrance to Great Qi's small world, the Congyun Sea.

At first glance, he saw the nascent Heavenly Soul of Earth and Heaven, Crimson Flame, about to gestate.

As if sensing Li Ping's presence, the Crimson Flame, still in the process of formation, transmitted a perplexed emotion.

Li Ping did not interfere with the progression of the Crimson Flame Burning Sea.

He knew this was a necessary process for the fragments of other worlds to truly integrate into the Xuanhuang Realm.

Chapter 1231: Array Thought Swallows Congyun Sea

Li Ping stood silently, feeling the unreconciled will of the vast ocean beneath his feet.

Faced with a life-or-death crisis, any existence would struggle with all its might.

Li Ping could also sense the ocean's fervent desire to survive.

But its survival, for the Xuanhuang Realm, was nothing less than naked "malice."

Li Ping, considering himself an avatar of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, naturally could not stand on the side of the Congyun Sea.

"Since you have come, you shall submit properly."

"There is no need for further futile struggles."

With a thought, his divine sense enveloped the entire Congyun Great Ocean.

Instantly, the scenes on the tens of thousands of islands scattered throughout, as well as the myriad lives dwelling within the sea, appeared in Li Ping's mind.

Li Ping remained silent for a moment.

"This is a necessary sacrifice."

A flicker of determination flashed in his eyes, and strands of golden light surged from his body, scattering to all parts of the Congyun Sea.

This power, akin to Origin Force essence, was undetectable by anyone in the Congyun Sea, where only cultivators of the Soul Transformation stage held sway.

The golden light spread throughout the Congyun Sea's various regions within mere breaths, piercing deep into the ocean's depths, all the way to the seabed.

Beneath the seabed of the Congyun Sea, violent tremors, unknown to any, began to occur.

If viewed from the sky, the surface of the entire ocean appeared to have formed a colossal net.

Enveloping this verdant sea of life.

Suddenly, dark clouds gathered in the sky.

The previously calm sea surface was violently churned by surging waves.

The waves were even more ferocious than those during past wind disasters.

Some islands were capsized without warning, while the spiritual islands with cultivators were left precariously endangered amidst the tempest.

The cultivators of the Congyun Sea looked at the abnormal changes in heaven and earth with bewildered unease.

Some cultivators with keen spiritual senses felt a premonition of impending doom. Their expressions changed, and disregarding everything else, they immediately used the teleportation arrays of the Myriad Immortals Island to flee the area.

Their act of fleeing attracted the attention of a considerable number of people. A small portion of cultivators chose to follow them.

However, the vast majority scoffed at these "alarmist, timid fugitives."

They comfortably remained on the Myriad Immortals Island, watching the dramatic changes in the Congyun Sea's skies and waters.

Li Ping paid no heed to the fleeing cultivators, nor did he care about the onlookers.

His objective, from beginning to end, was solely the residual will of the Congyun Sea.

The golden giant net, invisible to ordinary cultivators, had already sealed the Congyun Sea.

The energy of the Origin Force essence accumulated and evolved within, and a grand formation was about to reveal its might.

The consciousness of the Congyun Sea clearly felt the increasingly tight restraint of the golden giant net, kicking up even more violent waves.

However, in Li Ping's view, it was merely a futile rage.

"How can the will of a world be extinguished?"

Li Ping mused on this question as he constructed the formation.

"I shall refine gods with all sentient beings."

He quickly came up with this immensely formidable formation.

"A formation that can even resist True Immortals, I presume it won't be a significant problem to deal with a residual world consciousness."

"Let countless meaningless extraneous thoughts impact it..."

As Li Ping set up the formation, strange images began to appear inexplicably in the sky above the Congyun Sea.

They were contorted, despairing faces.

They wailed and flailed their arms.

As if pleading for help, or perhaps merely uttering instinctive cries of agony.

The sky was filled with an increasing number of bizarre faces.

They were densely packed, almost filling every visible space.

To the ears of the living beings within the Congyun Sea, only the wails of these demonic faces could be heard, drowning out all other sounds.

"Ah!"

Those with weak wills were influenced by these demonic faces and quickly became equally desperate and insane.

And those who could barely hold on soon fell into boundless, terrifying nightmares.

Vaguely, they seemed to see a black sun rising in the sky, the horrifying spectacle of the entire world on the brink of destruction.

Just like the despairing demonic faces in the sky, they collectively experienced this unimaginable tribulation.

The teleportation arrays on Myriad Immortals Island remained open.

However, all cultivators who witnessed the myriad faces in the sky lost the ability to control their own thoughts.

Regardless of their cultivation level, from nascent Qi Refiners to island masters of the Soul Transformation stage.

All were affected.

Although their minds were filled with boundless despair, they couldn't muster the slightest thought of escape.

It must be known that the formation Li Ping laid out did not target these cultivators.

They were merely caught in the crossfire, and had already reached such a state. One could only imagine the cruel scene currently faced by the consciousness of the Congyun Sea.

The residual world will of an entire prefecture was utterly incapable of resisting it.

Amidst the continuous wails of billions of demonic faces, Li Ping felt the will of the Congyun Sea dissipating.

The monstrous waves were slowly subsiding.

It seemed as though everything would pass, and the sun would shine again after the rain.

But Li Ping knew that the Congyun Sea, from this moment on, would not be the same as before.

The process of annihilating the Congyun Sea's consciousness lasted for a full day.

During this period, any cultivator who entered the Congyun Sea's range was affected and fell into terrifying illusions.

However, since no large-scale casualties occurred, the Myriad Immortals Alliance had not yet had time to react.

The dark clouds in the sky dispersed, and the Congyun Sea became as clear as azure silk.

An eerily silent atmosphere settled.

Li Ping felt the scattered remnants of the Congyun Sea's will throughout the heavens and earth.

The golden giant net slowly retracted, drawing back the world remnants, now fragmented into myriad pieces, into his body.

"Urgh..."

As Li Ping absorbed the consciousness of the Congyun Sea, countless images flashed through his mind.

Even though he was accustomed to constantly monitoring every event within the Great Qi Saint Dynasty.

The sheer volume of information was on entirely different scales.

In the vast ocean, humanity was not the only existence.

Beneath the calm sea surface, billions upon billions of lives thrived.

From Li Ping's subjective perspective, he would naturally not pay much attention to these creatures lacking intelligence.

However, at this moment, he was passively absorbing this information.

In the perception of the world's will, these fish were not fundamentally different from human cultivators.

Li Ping endured the searing pain in his sea of consciousness, accepting all the information.

As if he had consumed a potent tonic, the strength of his divine soul began to swell like an inflating balloon.

Li Ping's divine soul was already sufficiently resilient among cultivators.

But in this process of rapid expansion, it was unavoidable that cracks began to appear.

An ordinary cultivator encountering such a situation would only face despair and soul dispersion.

But Li Ping was different.

Possessing the Heavenly Emperor's Stellar Canon, he not only used the countless citizens of the Great Qi Saint Dynasty as anchors.

His body also contained the transcendent Origin Force essence.

Golden energy surged, mending the wounds in his divine soul.

Simultaneously, it acted as a supplement to the expanding divine soul.

After passing the initial dangerous phase, Li Ping gradually adapted.

Chapter 1232: Clear Wind Nowhere

When the pain subsided, it was followed by a rapid expansion of the soul.

The will of the world, even just the remnants of a single prefecture, was an absolute tonic for cultivators.

In the past, when Emperor Li Ping inspected and monitored various affairs within Great Qi, he still operated from a "human" perspective, receiving and handling countless trivial matters. But from now on, having absorbed the consciousness of the Congyun Sea, Li Ping could perhaps oversee every detail of the Sacred Dynasty from the overarching perspective of "the world itself."

Seven days passed without wind after the Congyun Sea's consciousness perished.

Li Ping stood between the sea and the sky, waiting for the fusion to complete.

Even without deliberate effort, Li Ping, having devoured the Congyun Sea's consciousness, could easily perceive every event occurring within it.

He saw the cultivators affected by the demonic faces, most of whom had not recovered from their madness after he retracted his divine ability. Less than one in a hundred of the cultivators remained normal after this ordeal.

He saw the Crimson Flame, an Earth and Heaven's Soul, brewing in the sky. Due to the demise of the Congyun Sea's consciousness, there was no longer any need for it to descend upon the sea. The condensed laws of power quietly dispersed.

He saw, in the center of the Congyun Sea, the Cloud Water Heavenly Palace, which had been on the verge of reappearing from its seal due to loosened restrictions. After a flash of mysterious blue light, it once again fell into silence.

He also saw that the anomalies in the Congyun Sea had attracted the attention of certain beings in the Xuanhuang Realm. Several massive divine senses instantly descended and swept across the ocean. But at this moment, Li Ping had taken the place of the Congyun Sea's consciousness, perfectly integrated into heaven and earth. The combined concealment of his formation and the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao ensured that Li Ping was not discovered.

Although he had temporarily evaded detection, the sense of impending crisis in Li Ping's heart did not disappear.

"It seems this place is not suitable for lingering," Li Ping thought to himself after thoroughly absorbing and digesting the Congyun Sea's consciousness.

However, before returning to the Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi, he had one more thing to do.

His figure flickered, and Li Ping instantly arrived at the seabed near the Congyun Sea and the Flowing Cloud Island.

Here, amidst the abyssal trenches of the seabed, lay a strange vortex.

At the center of the vortex, a pale blue pearl emitted a faint glow.

"The Vast Sea Pearl."

As part of the Congyun Sea's contingency plan, the Vast Sea Pearl was its last means of survival.

Li Ping extended his hand, and the pale blue pearl flew out of the seabed vortex and into his palm.

"Since I have already become a part of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, let's sever all ties completely."

Golden energy enveloped the Vast Sea Pearl, then was forcefully infused into it.

When the light dispersed, the pearl in Li Ping's hand had changed from pale blue to a deep azure.

But it had lost its former vitality.

Li Ping had completely erased the last trace of the Congyun Sea's faint consciousness within the Vast Sea Pearl.

"From now on, the Vast Sea Pearl is simply the Vast Sea Pearl, with no connection to the Congyun Sea."

Li Ping did not pocket the pearl, but instead flicked his finger, sending it randomly towards a corner of the Congyun Sea, awaiting a destined individual.

Having done all this, Li Ping finally left the ocean.

The cultivators of a prefecture were all turned into imbeciles.

When the Myriad Immortals Alliance finally noticed the changes in the Congyun Sea, they were furious.

While sending people to investigate, the handling of these dangerous, deranged cultivators also became a difficult problem.

In the end, it took the combined efforts of five Harmonious Dao cultivators to barely manage the chaos in the Congyun Sea.

Among these five was the patriarch of the Sun family, Sun Luyuan.

Previously, he had tried every method and finally managed to contact Fairy Kongyou.

Sun Luyuan had already thoroughly investigated Kongyou's background, knowing that she had a simple nature, wore her emotions on her sleeve, and was exceptionally curious about novel things. Thus, Sun Luyuan concocted a partially true, partially false lie.

"I heard before that you, Fairy, once turned an ungrateful male cultivator into a dog and tortured him day and night?"

"That scene was truly unbearable to watch. Coincidentally, when I was touring a small world some time ago, I encountered a similar scene. They also transformed criminals into strange beasts as a means of punishment..."

Sun Luyuan recounted some of his experiences in the Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi.

"The emperor of this small world has ideas that coincide with mine? Interesting."

"And from your description, this small world is quite developed..."

After several casual mentions, Kongyou was indeed drawn in.

She agreed that if she had the opportunity, she would visit with a few other acquaintances within the Alliance for a tour.

Seeing that his plan had succeeded, Sun Luyuan was overjoyed.

He even thought it might be a good idea to use Fairy Kongyou's fame to trick more talents from the Myriad Immortals Alliance to come.

Who would have thought that before the plan could be implemented, a tragedy would suddenly strike the Myriad Immortals Alliance? The deception plan had to be temporarily suspended.

Originally, the mess in the Congyun Sea had nothing to do with him.

However, Xu Yuanxian, the Chief of the Law Enforcement Hall, gave him a task privately.

It was only then that Sun Luyuan had to make the difficult journey.

"Clear Breeze Hall. This is it."

After subduing and rounding up all the deranged cultivators who attacked anyone on sight, Sun Luyuan arrived at this building on Myriad Immortals Island.

He felt no sign of living beings inside.

And when Sun Luyuan truly entered and saw the situation within, his pupils suddenly contracted.

An old man, lying on a wooden chair, had tree roots growing from all over his body, binding him firmly to the ground.

Although the old man was not completely dead, a trace of his breath remained. But in Sun Luyuan's eyes, he was no different from a dead person.

It was as if his soul had been completely devoured by these strange roots, leaving only an empty shell.

"This is the guardian of Clear Breeze Hall that Elder Xu mentioned. He was at least at the Nascent Soul stage, and yet he died so mysteriously."

Sun Luyuan shook his head slightly.

His gaze shifted from the old man and scanned the interior of Clear Breeze Hall.

After a moment, he discovered a hidden entrance.

Heightening his vigilance, Sun Luyuan strode through the faint green fissure.

A somewhat spacious area.

"Boom! Boom! Boom!..."

Continuous sounds of tremors from the ground.

Sun Luyuan looked towards the source of the noise and saw a large tree that had grown two human-like legs.

It was running on the ground.

In the center of the tree trunk was an incredibly ancient, wizened face.

At this moment, the tree-face was filled with endless terror.

This tree-being was running frantically, and because its two legs were not enough to support its body, it kept falling and getting up. But it never stopped running.

It muttered to itself, "Again, the calamity has arrived. This terrifying scene, I have never seen even in my father's most malicious curses!"

"But it never happened!"

"It's fake, it's fake!"

...

The tree-person spoke incoherently, its words contradictory and completely unintelligible.

However, it was deeply trapped in its own delusion. Even when Sun Luyuan tried to communicate with it, it was futile.

"Ah Liu has gone mad."

Just then, a clear female voice suddenly sounded in Sun Luyuan's ear.

"Hmm?" Sun Luyuan was startled.

Because he had already searched thoroughly, and there seemed to be no one else here besides the tree-person.

But immediately, Sun Luyuan thought of the task Elder Xu had entrusted him with this time.

He immediately asked, "Could you be Fellow Daoist Clear Breeze?"

The female voice did not respond.

"I am here on Elder Xu's orders to escort you back. He said that this spirit wood has gone mad, and the passage within it cannot be used, so Fellow Daoist Clear Breeze is trapped here."

Sun Luyuan spoke while carefully observing his surroundings.

He wanted to confirm the location of this "Clear Breeze."

But even with his Harmonious Dao realm perception, he found no trace.

"Ah Liu has gone mad." The female voice still did not answer directly, merely repeating the phrase several times.

Sun Luyuan couldn't help but frown slightly. Could it be that this female cultivator had also been affected by the demonic faces and gone mad?

"Ah Liu and I had the best relationship. Now that it's crazy, who will play with me in the future?"

The mournful voice echoed in the small space, overlapping with Ah Liu's occasional mournful cries, sending shivers down one's spine.

For some reason, Sun Luyuan felt the same sense of dread he had experienced while wandering in the Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi.

"Fellow Daoist Clear Breeze..." Sun Luyuan coughed lightly, steeling himself.

Although he didn't know the relationship between this female cultivator named Clear Breeze and Elder Xu.

But the fact that the usually rigid and unfeeling Xu Yuanxian had broken his usual norm to find him privately was enough to indicate their extraordinary relationship.

Fortunately, things did not develop as Sun Luyuan had expected.

Clear Breeze seemed to sob softly for a moment, then finally emerged from her grief.

"So you were sent by Little Xu. So he hasn't forgotten me."

Clear Breeze's simple words made Sun Luyuan's hair stand on end.

"Little Xu? Xu Yuanxian?"

Sun Luyuan almost doubted if he had heard correctly.

Elder Xu had been the Chief of the Law Enforcement Hall for over three thousand years, a true ancient monster.

This young-sounding girl called him "Little Xu"...

If she wasn't mad, how old could she be?

Who exactly was this "Clear Breeze"?

Countless thoughts flashed through Sun Luyuan's mind, but he dared not dwell on them. His expression became timid.

He no longer dared to address her as "Fellow Daoist Clear Breeze" and cautiously changed his address to, "Senior, why do you not reveal yourself? Have I done something wrong?"

After a moment of silence in the space.

Clear Breeze's somewhat strange voice sounded from behind Sun Luyuan.

"Haven't I always been here?"

"Oh, right. I forgot. Most people can't see me."

Clear Breeze's words made Sun Luyuan break out in a cold sweat.

"Elder Xu said that he would send someone to deal with this mad spirit wood later. Please, Senior, return with me for now," Sun Luyuan said quickly.

"Ah! That's great. I knew Ah Liu could be saved." Clear Breeze, like a simple little girl, suddenly became cheerful.

"It's all that doomsday howling scene that scared it silly temporarily. If you hadn't come, no one would have talked to me for a long time."

Clear Breeze's voice grew closer and closer to Sun Luyuan.

Finally, it seemed to stop on his back.

"Alright. Then I'll listen to Little Xu and leave for now."

"The aura here has changed. It's not very comfortable anymore."

Feeling the seemingly real weight on his back, Sun Luyuan's heart pounded, and he wiped the cold sweat from his forehead.

"Shall I just leave directly?" he asked tentatively.

"Yes. I'm already on your back."

Clear Breeze's words confirmed Sun Luyuan's guess.

Sun Luyuan dared not delay and left the bizarre space directly.

The sounds of the maddened spirit wood continued to echo there.

"Shall we... return to the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters?" Sun Luyuan asked again as he rapidly flew away from the Congyun Sea in a beam of light.

"Not there. That place makes me uncomfortable. Let's go to Luoyan Prefecture."

Clear Breeze's mood seemed to have improved, and she said with a hint of cheerfulness in her tone.

"Luoyan Prefecture?" Sun Luyuan nodded.

Elder Xu's task was merely to escort Clear Breeze out and settle her in a Clear Breeze Hall in another prefecture.

Sun Luyuan did not dwell on it and set off towards Luoyan Prefecture.

Along the way, he pondered the true identity of the being on his back.

With the Boundless Mirror, an Immortal artifact, at home, Sun Luyuan considered himself quite knowledgeable.

However, he had never heard of such a bizarre existence like Clear Breeze.

He couldn't even gauge Clear Breeze's strength.

Why would Elder Xu send him on such a long journey just because she was trapped?

From this perspective, Clear Breeze's strength couldn't be that high.

But Clear Breeze's strange words and various peculiar behaviors made Sun Luyuan's heart palpitate.

It was clear that this formless, shapeless being called Clear Breeze was by no means simple.

Sun Luyuan secretly lamented and accelerated his pace.

He just wanted to complete the task quickly and get rid of her.

Clear Breeze remained silent throughout the journey.

And they were getting closer and closer to Luoyan Prefecture.

Just as relief was in sight, a sudden remark from Clear Breeze, however, plunged Sun Luyuan into the abyss.

"You're getting a bit impatient."

"As expected, not many people in this world are good to me."

Sun Luyuan felt a chill rise from the bottom of his heart.

Although Clear Breeze said nothing further, his sense of unease grew stronger and stronger.

"What feels not quite right?"

Sun Luyuan knew that a change was happening to him.

But he could not perceive the specific details of the change.

It wasn't until Sun Luyuan arrived in Luoyan Prefecture and inadvertently glanced downwards that he suddenly realized.

He was very close to the ground.

The scorching sun shone brightly overhead.

Yet, inexplicably, he had no shadow on the ground.

Sun Luyuan knew very well that he had not used any techniques to conceal his form.

But his shadow had vanished.

He extended his arms in bemusement.

He seemed to be becoming insubstantial.

His existence was fading.

He was about to become formless and shapeless, just like Clear Breeze.

The change came too quickly, leaving Sun Luyuan with no time to even feel fear.

His mind was simply a blank.

Just as Sun Luyuan felt his connection to this world growing weaker and weaker...

A brilliant golden light erupted from within his body.

Chapter 1233: Heavenly Dao Grants Great Strength

Let's rewind the perspective to a moment ago.

The Faceless Saint Emperor, having devoured the residual world will of the Congyun Sea and returned to the Great Qi small world, finally gained a more concrete understanding of the changes within himself.

Previously, he needed to focus intently on the numerous complex and trivial matters within the Sacred Dynasty, leaving him with little spare time for contemplation.

But now, even without using a third of his strength, Li Ping could effortlessly handle all matters, large and small, within the Sacred Dynasty.

In addition to a pure increase in quantity, Li Ping's soul also seemed to have become more sensitive.

He looked down upon this world and discovered the nascent, nascent consciousness of the small world, which was undergoing transformation. Before this, the Great Qi small world had merely operated on instinct, unlike the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, which exhibited clear "personified" characteristics. But due to Li Ping's continuous modifications to the Great Qi small world, it had already met the basic conditions for the birth of self-awareness.

The birth of world will was a lengthy process. According to Li Ping's estimation, at the current normal pace, it would take at least a thousand years.

However, if Li Ping continued to promote the advancement of Great Qi, this time would be proportionally shortened.

The current state of the Great Qi small world, with its splendid scenery, was entirely due to Li Ping's modifications. And the powerful, upward-surging, unstoppable fortune of the Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi, which was integrated with Li Ping, also exerted various subtle influences on the small world.

All cultivators are born of nature. But in Li Ping's case, the current Great Qi small world was more like his creation. The grace of re-creation was akin to that of heaven and earth as parents.

Seated on the Saint Emperor's throne, all sorts of profound insights constantly arose in his mind.

These were not only from his own thoughts but also aided by the world itself.

Li Ping felt as though he had grasped some critical information.

However, at this very moment, his thoughts were inexplicably interrupted by a sense of premonition.

"Hmm?"

Li Ping checked and discovered that one of the prey within the Origin Force essence net he had cast had shown signs of breaking free.

Faint, peculiar fluctuations emanated from it, as if trying to escape the restraint of the golden net.

"Sun Luyuan?"

Li Ping still had some impression of this Harmonious Dao cultivator from the Myriad Immortals Alliance who had recently pledged allegiance to the Sacred Dynasty.

"Could it be that people from the Myriad Immortals Alliance have discovered this and intervened?" Li Ping couldn't help but think.

But he soon sensed what was happening to Sun Luyuan.

"Oh?"

Li Ping's heart instantly became solemn.

Using the Origin Force essence within Sun Luyuan, Li Ping instantly arrived beside him.

He placed his hand on Sun Luyuan's shoulder, and the surging golden power was continuously infused into his body.

After a while, Sun Luyuan's body, which had been slowly becoming transparent, finally solidified again.

"Many thanks to the Saint Emperor for saving my life," Sun Luyuan said, still shaken by what had just happened, his face filled with lingering fear and gratitude.

Li Ping slowly withdrew his hand, but his senses did not leave Sun Luyuan's back.

He could not directly observe the entity named "Clear Breeze."

Even influencing her perceptions of the outside world was impossible.

"You are an interesting person," Li Ping mused.

If not for Clear Breeze's voice, which happened to sound out, Li Ping would almost have believed she was a figment of Sun Luyuan's imagination.

It was hard to believe that there was still something in the Xuanhuang Realm that he, Li Ping, could not observe.

"What are you?"

There was no malice in his tone, and Li Ping asked with genuine seriousness.

Sun Luyuan lowered his head, hiding all expression from his face.

Unexpectedly, Clear Breeze did not get angry. "I want to know that too."

"It's a pity that I've forgotten," she said with some regret.

"My memory is a bit poor. Besides Little Xu and Ah Liu, I don't have a deep impression of others..."

"What's your name?" Clear Breeze asked.

"Li Ping," Li Ping replied concisely.

He sensed an aura similar to Yin Shangren on Clear Breeze, yet subtly different.

"Perhaps I can help you recall it." His intuition told him that the secret behind Clear Breeze might be helpful in the future war against the Myriad Immortals Alliance, so he offered.

"Hehe, I feel like you're not up to anything good."

As expected, Clear Breeze revealed the truth in a single sentence.

"Alas, there are indeed few people in this world who are truly good to me," Clear Breeze's tone became melancholic and low again.

The moment Li Ping heard this, the golden Origin Force within his body surged spontaneously.

This was a sign of its automatic protective activation.

Since Clear Breeze chose to make a move, Li Ping naturally wouldn't be polite.

Behind him, the magnificent silhouette of the Sacred Dynasty suddenly appeared.

Golden light continuously erupted from the image of the Sacred Dynasty.

It formed a giant hand that directly grasped the space where Clear Breeze was located.

Li Ping thought that since he couldn't observe her, he might as well seal off and confiscate the space she occupied and study her later.

But this strangely elusive Clear Breeze could not be subdued by such simple means.

The golden giant hand returned to the silhouette of the Sacred Dynasty, leaving behind only a black void – proof that a small piece of space had completely vanished.

However, Clear Breeze's voice still echoed from within the void.

"You want to take me back?"

"Do you want to be with me forever? If so, why resist?"

"Insolent." The Faceless Saint Emperor responded with a cold snort.

On Li Ping's originally featureless face, indistinct facial features vaguely manifested.

But they were not like those of ordinary humans. They were more like an evolution of different energies.

Especially his eyes, which were silver-white whirlpools, as brilliant as the stars in the sky.

"Heaven and Earth power, bestow yourselves upon me!"

Li Ping's majestic voice echoed like thunder.

The sky of Luoyan Prefecture instantly changed its colors due to this declaration.

"If you want to drag me down with you, you'll need to have the weight for it!"

Sensing the extremely close connection between himself and the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, Li Ping then released the protection of his golden Origin Force, allowing Clear Breeze's strange power to engulf him.

Boom! Boom! Boom!

Streaks of lightning flashed through the dense dark clouds, and the earth trembled slightly.

Li Ping's body's color momentarily faded.

But it quickly returned to normal.

On the other hand, Clear Breeze was actually pulled out of some blurry images!

"Found you!"

In Li Ping's vortex-like eyes, two beams of light suddenly shot out.

Like chains, they locked onto Clear Breeze.

"Come out for me!"

Li Ping roared, and the golden giant hand reappeared.

Grabbing the silver chains, he yanked fiercely.

The previously small, healing black spatial rift suddenly showed signs of violently collapsing outwards.

Chapter 1234: Ink Kill Breaks the Shadow Trail

As the space in Luoyan Prefecture of the Xuanhuang Realm continued to collapse, Clear Breeze was also slowly pulled out, revealing her true form.

She was a willow tree with fluttering branches and leaves!

However, Clear Breeze was clearly not an ordinary tree. At first glance, she appeared to be a willow, but upon closer inspection, she seemed to have merged with the characteristics of many other trees.

After pulling out more than half of Clear Breeze's true form, the silver chains stopped advancing, remaining suspended in mid-air.

It was as if they had encountered immense resistance.

Despite appearing so disheveled on the outside, Clear Breeze strangely showed no sign of pain.

She just kept muttering to herself, as if Li Ping's actions had truly made her remember something.

"This place is..."

"What has happened over the years?"

"I am Clear Breeze? No, no, that's the name Xu Yuanxian gave me. My original name was..."

"It was..."

"Tian..."

"Tian Yin?!"

A silver light, identical to the previous one, shot out from within the willow tree.

It aimed directly at Li Ping, towards his brain, his sea of consciousness.

The automatic defense of the golden Origin Force essence was also incredibly fast.

A shield materialized in front of Li Fan, colliding violently with the silver light.

There was no earth-shattering explosion, only the intense dissipation of their respective lights.

"Run?"

Simultaneously, Li Ping vaguely sensed a thought transmitted from the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.

It was actually a warning, urging him to flee quickly.

Li Ping's heart sank, and he looked ahead.

Under the attrition of the golden Origin Force essence, the radiant silver light slowly revealed its true form.

It was a seemingly ordinary silver needle.

Although the light enveloping it was slowly fading, the sense of threat it posed to Li Ping had not diminished in the slightest.

"I am now empowered by the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, making me a half-step Longevity Realm cultivator."

"Yet, I am locked in a fierce battle with a mere silver needle..."

Li Ping felt no frustration, but rather a surge of anger.

Along with the silver needle, an old, kind face appeared in Li Ping's mind.

"It is indeed related to the people of the Heavenly Law Realm."

"Those who sow chaos in Xuanhuang deserve death!"

Li Ping's killing intent surged continuously.

However, he also knew that he was not a match for the Heavenly Physician at this moment and had to retreat for the time being.

He loosened the silver chains in his hand, and Clear Breeze, or rather Tian Yin, her voice once again became slowly transparent.

"Go."

Li Ping could no longer afford to care about her at this moment.

While resisting the silver needle's attack, Li Ping prepared to leave Luoyan Prefecture.

At the brink of danger, he still remembered to bring the completely stunned Sun Luyuan with him.

Wrapped in golden Origin Force, Li Ping's figure also slowly faded.

The Heavenly Physician's silver needle did not pursue, but returned to Tian Yin's body, suppressing her within the formless and shapeless.

ωwш..C○ Before escaping, Li Ping vaguely heard a sigh from the sky.

"Where will the ethereal Tian Yin finally land..."

"Where will the ethereal Tian Yin finally land."

After Li Ping completely disappeared from Luoyan Prefecture, the anomalies in the heavens and earth did not cease.

Instead, they escalated.

Lightning bolts struck madly, and violent thunderstorms raged, like the end of the world.

Or rather, the end of the world had truly arrived.

Because a figure as black as ink had already descended upon Luoyan Prefecture.

If Li Fan were present, he would have recognized this familiar existence at a glance.

It was the Earth and Heaven's Soul, Ink Kill!

As the ultimate world-destroying means of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, it decisively descended now that Li Ping had left.

Ink Kill first glanced in the direction Li Ping had departed.

Then, it transformed into ten thousand, ten thousand into a hundred million.

Without any hesitation, it skillfully manifested infinite ink.

To completely eradicate Luoyan Prefecture.

The descent of Ink Kill, and its spread this time, was much faster than the sea-slaughter Li Fan had experienced before.

The cultivators of Luoyan Prefecture had no time to resist or flee.

In just the time it takes to steep a cup of tea, the originally desolate but vibrant Luoyan Prefecture had completely turned into nothingness.

The sudden appearance of Ink Kill naturally alerted many hidden powerful figures within the Xuanhuang Realm.

But Luoyan Prefecture no longer existed.

Even if they wanted to find any clues, they were powerless to do so.

The impact of Ink Kill's abrupt annihilation of an entire prefecture had only just begun.

In the Saint Emperor's Throne of the Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi.

Li Ping sat, the residual power of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao on his body telling him what had happened in Luoyan Prefecture.

He knew that this was the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao's action to prevent him from being detected and tracked by the Heavenly Physician.

Coupled with the fact that Luoyan Prefecture was originally a fragment of the Heavenly Law Realm, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao's cleanup was decisive.

"That woman was called Tian Yin?"

"Like the Heavenly Physician, she has the ability to perceive people's hearts."

"She is formless and shapeless, hidden within the Xuanhuang Realm. Besides her own abilities, it might also be due to the embellishment of the Heavenly Physician's silver needle."

"Although I don't know her true purpose, it is certainly not a good thing for the Xuanhuang Realm itself."

Although this encounter with the Heavenly Physician ended in failure, it allowed Li Ping to understand the gap between himself and the Heavenly Physician.

"Law Transmission Heavenly Venerate, and even stronger."

"It seems the path I have to walk is still very long."

"However, the power of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao I borrowed this time was limited. After all, I only intended to subdue that woman. If it were a life-or-death struggle, the blessing of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao could have been dozens of times greater."

"Our Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi still has infinite prospects."

"And the fishing pond is a supreme treasure. Perhaps it can give me some surprises from beyond the high wall."

Self-pity was not Li Ping's style.

After a brief failure, he immediately began to summarize and seek solutions.

"But this alone is still not enough."

Li Ping naturally thought of the sealed malevolent thought of the Xuanhuang Realm.

Having devoured the remnant will of the Congyun Sea this time, he had a clearer understanding of the power of world will.

"If I can devour the Xuanhuang malevolent thought..."

"With the Xuanhuang power fully restored, I will undergo another qualitative change."

"It seems this matter must be put on the agenda."

While Li Ping was contemplating, Sun Luyuan trembled and hid under the Saint Emperor's Throne, not daring to move.

The performance of the Saint Emperor, Tian Yin, and the silver needle before him had all profoundly shocked Sun Luyuan.

He was also a Harmonious Dao cultivator, yet before them, he was like a child, completely powerless to resist.

"What do you think of that woman named Tian Yin?"

After a long while, the voice of the Destined Saint Emperor reached Sun Luyuan's ears.

Sun Luyuan shuddered and wore a bitter expression.

Chapter 1235: The Crimson and Green See Xu Ke

"This... this..." Sun Luyuan stammered for a long time, unable to utter a single word.

Fortunately, Li Ping did not make things difficult for him.

With a wave of his hand, a golden light shot into Sun Luyuan's body. Li Ping said lightly, "From now on, you probably can't go back to the Myriad Immortals Alliance. You'll stay in our Sacred Dynasty for now."

"After some time, I will arrange for you to return to the Myriad Immortals Alliance under a different identity."

Sun Luyuan looked up at Li Ping with a bewildered expression.

During this time, Li Ping then displayed the scene of the world-ending destruction of Luoyan Prefecture to him.

As endless fear surged through Sun Luyuan's heart, he suddenly understood the use of the golden light he had just received.

It had erased the mark left by the Myriad Immortals Alliance within him.

"That Tian Yin is involved in too many secrets. If an entire prefecture is not completely wiped out, it's hard to avoid people tracing the clues back," Li Ping explained.

"Then what about our Sun family..." Sun Luyuan suddenly realized something, his expression changing drastically.

"That will depend on your luck. If Tian Yin tells the Myriad Immortals Alliance what happened to her, then the Sun family will surely be implicated and completely vanish, with no one spared."

Li Ping's words turned Sun Luyuan deathly pale.

But then he changed his tone: "However, you don't need to worry too much. Tian Yin is formless and shapeless. If she doesn't reveal herself, the Myriad Immortals Alliance likely won't be able to find her. Tian Yin and the Myriad Immortals Alliance are not allies."

"Moreover, my attack before leaving, while it didn't destroy her, did heavily injure her. Tian Yin's condition was unstable to begin with. When she reappears and regains consciousness, she may not necessarily remember us."

Even though Li Ping said this, it couldn't completely reassure Sun Luyuan.

The hidden meaning in Li Ping's words was clear: there was a terrifying existence behind Tian Yin, one that even the unfathomable Great Qi Saint Emperor had to be wary of.

"Damn Xu Yuanxian, claiming it was just a simple errand. I actually believed your lies..."

Thinking of how he was inexplicably dragged into such a matter, not only were his original plans disrupted, but his entire family might be implicated, Sun Luyuan's heart filled with baseless anger.

"This old geezer, like the other higher-ups of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, is truly worthless!" he cursed inwardly.

Then he thought of the various crises his family would face after his disappearance, and Sun Luyuan's mind became a mess.

Chapter 1237: Borrowing Luck to Devour the Heavens

He simply couldn't find anyone capable and trustworthy.

In his memory and cognition, this formation could indeed hinder the descent of True Immortals for a while.

And although Xu Ke had lived for a long time, he had never truly witnessed the power of a True Immortal, so he had no reason to doubt Li Ping's words.

"With this formation, even if it's released directly, it won't be able to escape."

Xu Ke also had some understanding of formations.

This Myriad Spirits Great Formation was indeed as Li Ping said, profound and boundless.

After touring the Myriad Spirits Great Formation, Li Ping took Xu Ke to Yin Shangren.

The scene before him overlapped somewhat with the scene he saw there, and Xu Ke couldn't help but become somewhat dazed.

Yin Shangren's reaction, however, was one of terror.

He, who was teaching the children, suddenly froze completely.

After a moment's pause, he abruptly stood up and stared intently at the coffin behind Xu Ke.

His body trembled, and then he actually split open from his body, revealing another self that had been hidden all along.

What concerned him even more was the performance of the Xuanhuang malevolent thought behind him.
