Instead, it seemed to have been frightened into silence.

A moment later, the Xuanhuang malevolent thought began to pound on the coffin lid again, announcing its presence.

But in Xu Ke's eyes, it looked more like a hollow threat.

Li Ping's figure shielded Yin Shangren and the Xuanhuang malevolent thought, allowing the two to return to normal.

Yin Shangren's body, which had split open, closed again. He grinned and said, "I didn't expect that the esteemed Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao would fall to such a state?"

"If my brothers knew about this, they might be overjoyed."

Yin Shangren licked his lips and said, "I've eaten quite a lot of world spirits like trash. But I've never tasted a complete world intention. I wonder what it tastes like."

Xu Ke was horrified upon hearing this.

Then, he heard Li Ping's telepathic introduction of Yin Shangren's origin.

"A world spirit left behind by the Xuanhuang Realm's devouring, who greatly admired Mr. Bai?"

Initially, Xu Ke had some doubts, but after seeing the white rib bone that Yin Shangren treasured, he had no other thoughts.

Even though it looked like an ordinary rib bone,

But Xu Ke knew with a single glance that it belonged to Mr. Bai.

Mr. Bai's smiling face reappeared in Xu Ke's mind, then shattered in an instant.

Only this white rib bone remained.

Xu Ke was suddenly overcome with sorrow.

Yin Shangren, upon learning of Xu Ke's special relationship with Mr. Bai, put away his fierce demeanor and became peaceful.

However, his eyes still occasionally swept towards the decaying coffin.

"With Daoist Yin here, if it escapes the heavy restrictions, at most it will end up as a meal on the plate," Li Ping said calmly.

Xu Ke, whose emotions had stabilized, finally believed the identity and plan of this Faceless Saint Emperor.

The moment his obsession was released, Xu Ke felt unprecedentedly relaxed.

"I've held on for so long. From now on, let the Xuanhuang Realm deal with it itself," Xu Ke thought to himself.

"What, are you also interested in it?" Yin Shangren curiously looked at Li Ping.

Li Ping briefly recounted what had happened in Luoyan Prefecture, then said, "It has been of great help to me."

Yin Shangren shrugged, "Then I won't fight you for it. Even if I eat it, at most it will satisfy my appetite, and it will still have to be expelled."

Li Ping remained silent, not replying.

"That silver needle..." Yin Shangren suddenly showed Li Ping an image.

"Does it look like this?"

Li Ping nodded. "Why? Have you seen it before?"

"I seem to have some impression, but it was a long time ago." Yin Shangren narrowed his eyes, trying to recall something.

"Oh, right. A long time ago, I saw it in this place. But it wasn't me then, it was a remnant memory of a part of me that I devoured. So the specific details are quite blurry. If you're interested, you can go look there; perhaps you'll find something."

Yin Shangren transmitted a location to Li Ping.

Perhaps as a world spirit, it still retained a faint connection to its original body. The location transmitted by Yin Shangren was precisely the current location of the Xuanhuang Realm.

"I understand. Let's deal with this matter first. With my current strength, even if I truly found something, it would be difficult to investigate further," Li Ping said frankly, without any reservations.

"The Xuanhuang Realm truly has too many strange and powerful beings," Yin Shangren snorted softly.

Li Ping then looked at Xu Ke. "Daoist Yin and I planned to gather Mr. Bai's scattered remains and bury them properly. After this matter is concluded, if you are willing, you can assist us."

Xu Ke naturally agreed without hesitation, his voice even trembling slightly. "Yes, yes."

Having successfully persuaded Xu Ke, the guardian, the next step was to release and absorb the Xuanhuang malevolent thought.

Although Li Ping was absolutely confident, he did not act carelessly.

He made thorough preparations.

The next day, a piece of news spread throughout the entire Sacred Dynasty.

Seven days later, the Supreme Saint Emperor would bestow his blessings.

All citizens who sincerely prayed during these seven days would receive the Saint Emperor's reward.

Praying to the Saint Emperor was already a mandatory task for the citizens of Great Qi. Now that the Saint Emperor had explicitly promised rewards, how could they dare to be negligent?

Thus, within just half a day of the imperial decree being issued, Li Ping felt the Xuanhuang Great Qi's fortune condense unprecedentedly.

Even the Origin Force of fortune generated within his [Celestial Emperor's Jade], seemed to be on the verge of transforming from purple to golden.

"This method is only effective temporarily and cannot last long."

"If I break my promise, I will suffer backlash, and might even fall in cultivation realms."

Li Ping felt his strength constantly climbing towards its peak, but his mind remained calm.

Golden Origin Force was drawn out, converging all sentient beings into one mind.

The Myriad Spirits Great Formation slowly operated accordingly.

It masked all contact with the outside world.

At this moment, not only was the Great Qi small world undetectable from the Xuanhuang Realm, but even Daoist Hundred Blossoms, who was in the Five Elements Great Cave Heaven nearby, suddenly lost her sense of the Great Qi small world.

If Li Ping had not notified her in advance, Bai Hua would likely have mistakenly believed that Great Qi was facing some terrifying disaster.

The process of devouring the Xuanhuang malevolent thought still required blocking the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao from the outside.

Otherwise, unimaginable things might happen.

Seven days passed in the blink of an eye.

Li Ping's state had reached its peak during these seven days of preparation.

At this moment, within the eye of the formation, Yin Shangren, Xu Ke, and Yi Shu stood in a triangular formation.

Li Ping sat suspended in the air, in the center of the three.

Yi Shu, as part of the Taiyan Dao-Transformation Stone, naturally sensed the unusual changes occurring within the Great Qi small world.

He proactively sought Li Ping out to inquire.

And Li Ping, who had nothing to hide, directly revealed his plan to devour the Xuanhuang malevolent thought.

After a brief moment of stunned silence, Yi Shu immediately offered to help.

He even proactively suggested that perhaps the cooperation between the Taiyan Sect and the Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi could be further deepened in the future.

After pondering for a moment, Li Ping agreed to Yi Shu's request.

He invited these three merely as a formality.

Within the Myriad Spirits Great Formation, everything was under his control.

If Yi Shu behaved honestly, it would be fine. But if he had any ulterior motives, Li Ping could refine him with a single thought.

Along with the Xuanhuang malevolent thought, to be devoured.

"Formation, activate!"

Li Ping coldly commanded.

The three within the formation felt the sky suddenly become chaotic.

Purple stars flickered intermittently within it.

It was as if they had entered the endless void, leaving the real world behind.

All three were startled.

Li Ping then gently pointed at the decaying wooden coffin placed beside him.

There was no sound of violent destruction.

The wooden layers dispersed like black smoke, vanishing completely.

A figure, transitioning from blurry to clear, appeared within the formation, in front of Li Ping.

Unlike the previous malevolent and resentful appearance,

The figure before him now was indistinguishable from the Mr. Bai in his memory.

It smiled faintly and asked, "Are you going to devour me?"

There was no hatred in his eyes, but rather relief and acceptance.

"Mr. Bai?!" Xu Ke was the first to exclaim in shock.

It wasn't that Xu Ke lacked self-control, but that this figure bore too much resemblance to Mr. Bai.

Li Ping remained unmoved, nodding faintly. "Correct."

"To merge with me, you have died a worthy death."

With just these simple words, the previously calm Xuanhuang malevolent thought's expression froze abruptly.

"Who do you think you are?!"

The Xuanhuang malevolent thought's disguise shattered, and it shrieked in exasperation.

It suddenly transformed into a black mist and lunged at Li Ping.

But before Li Ping, there seemed to be infinite distance.

No matter how hard it tried, it could not get close.

"Noisy."

"When you merge with me, you will know who I am."

Li Ping glanced at the Xuanhuang malevolent thought.

A majestic force descended from the heavens.

It instantly bound the black mist that the malevolent thought had transformed into.

"Myriad Spirits, Myriad Beings, Great Millstone of Heaven and Earth!"

Li Ping chanted softly, and a purple-golden vortex slowly formed above everyone's heads.

Chapter 1238: Great Heavenly Venerate Immortal Body

Within the purple-golden vortex, wind and thunder surged.

At the bottom of the funnel-like energy vortex was the somewhat panicked figure of the Xuanhuang malevolent thought.

Images of faces of different life forms flashed rapidly within the wind and thunder vortex, like a hurricane, tearing at the Xuanhuang malevolent thought.

As a result, its body gradually became distorted and blurred.

"I am the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao! The father and mother of you cultivators! How dare you treat me like this!"

"Again! Again! All you humans deserve to die!"

The Xuanhuang malevolent thought roared.

Choosing not to die passively, its appearance, which had originally resembled Mr. Bai, finally revealed its true form.

Its body expanded like an inflating balloon, instantly forming a monstrous, grotesque creature covered in blue and purple mixed-colored lumps. What was even more terrifying was that the Xuanhuang malevolent thought's face had disappeared. Or rather, the countless black shadows rapidly moving on its surface were its faces now!

Their expressions varied, but none revealed positive emotions. Madness, hatred, despair, brutality...

All the darkest and most twisted parts of sentient beings were displayed on the Xuanhuang malevolent thought.

Tangible black malevolent energy surged from its body, shooting straight up into the sky, directly meeting the rotating force of the purple-golden vortex.

In a silent collision, even Li Ping's Great Millstone of Heaven and Earth paused slightly.

Li Ping noticed that about one-third of the faces on the Xuanhuang malevolent thought were all staring directly at him.

"Die! Die! Die! Die! Die! Die! Die!"

A sharp curse erupted, sweeping towards them.

Xu Ke and the other two guarding the formation frowned slightly at this moment.

On Li Ping's originally featureless face, vague facial features faintly appeared due to the impact of this malevolent thought.

Countless tentacles covered in blue-purple sarcomas extended from the Xuanhuang malevolent thought's monstrous body, flailing wildly, attempting to break free from the Myriad Spirits Great Formation's restraint.

However, this ultimate formation, which could be considered the culmination of the Dissolution Disc's derivation, was not so easily broken?

After a brief pause, the purple-golden vortex began to rotate slowly again.

The sound of wind and thunder became even more intense than before.

From within, the sounds of human prayers emerged, resonating to form a unique rhythm, forcefully suppressing the Xuanhuang malevolent thought's earth-shattering roars.

"Evil, in the end, cannot triumph over justice."

"Look at what you've become. Do you still deserve the title of [Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao]?!"

Li Ping's calm voice, with a hint of mockery, penetrated the noise of the formation's conflict and accurately reached the ears of the Xuanhuang malevolent thought.

"Bastard! Who did this?!"

After a moment of stunned silence, it became completely enraged.

Clearly, even the Xuanhuang malevolent thought itself found it difficult to accept its current predicament.

Its body, suppressed by the Great Millstone of Heaven and Earth, actually showed signs of rallying and resisting again.

Li Ping, however, nodded slightly, constantly provoking and inciting the Xuanhuang malevolent thought with words, while focusing his attention on presiding over the Myriad Spirits Great Formation.

He absorbed the fragments stripped from the Xuanhuang malevolent thought into his own body through the vortex.

The negative emotions, like trickling streams, continuously flowed into Li Ping's consciousness.

The three guards within the formation couldn't help but feel nervous.

Being inside the formation, they could more clearly feel the terrifying nature of the Myriad Spirits Great Formation.

Even after being sealed for thousands of years, it was still a part of this world's Heavenly Dao. Yet, before this formation, it had no power to resist at all.

It even rendered their previous preparations useless. They could only quietly watch Li Ping perform.

The more terrifying the formation, the more they couldn't help but worry.

If the Saint Emperor were to be influenced by the malevolent thought and lose control...

It would likely be a disaster far more terrifying than the Xuanhuang malevolent thought escaping.

Even though they had great confidence in the Saint Emperor's strength, they couldn't help but feel nervous at this moment.

After all, they were still within the formation at this time.

"No need to worry, I'm fine," Li Ping seemed to have sensed their emotional fluctuations and calmly explained through telepathic transmission.

Not to mention Li Ping's own resilient will, but with the blessing of the Xuanhuang Immortal Heart Curse, he would never have his personality distorted by this Xuanhuang malevolent thought. Moreover, he was not resorting to a brute-force swallowing method, but using the Great Millstone of Heaven and Earth to slowly crush and absorb the Xuanhuang malevolent thought bit by bit, minimizing the side effects.

"Furthermore, with the intentions of the billions of citizens of Great Qi anchoring me."

"Billions of beings can refine gods. This is merely a part of the original Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, how could it possibly affect me?"

Li Ping's mind was clear.

Rather than dealing with the "malevolent thought," Li Ping's greater pressure at this moment was in digesting the chaotic and complex memories within the other party.

Although most of them were blurred by thousands of years of distorted despair.

But these fragmented memory shards were deeply embedded in its consciousness. Now, as its body was being dismembered, they flowed into Li Ping's mind.

Scenes of fragmented memory rapidly flashed through Li Ping's mind.

Most of them were difficult to discern in detail.

Only one scene repeatedly emerged.

It was clear that this was a memory that the Xuanhuang malevolent thought found unforgettable. During its time sealed, it had replayed countless times in its mind.

In the endless dark void.

A rapidly fleeing figure suddenly stopped.

"Why aren't you moving?"

The voice in the memory asked.

The initial emotion was one of relief and excitement.

But at this moment, it carried a hint of confusion.

The figure in white, Mr. Bai, turned around and looked back.

His expression constantly changed, appearing very complex.

"What's wrong?"

The perception from the memory gradually became agitated in the deathly silence.

"I can't go."

Finally, Mr. Bai took a deep breath and said slowly.

"Why can't you go?"

"The calamity has already occurred, and the general trend is irreversible. Rather than staying here, it's better to head towards the high wall and fight with all our might. Perhaps there's still a glimmer of hope for survival." The voice from the memory paused for a moment, unable to understand. Then it became somewhat urgent, and frantically tried to persuade him.

"With the remnants of the First Great Heavenly Venerate as protection, and by detonating those few immortal artifacts as fuel, the two of us working together have a very high chance of crossing the high wall!"

"We've prepared for so long, why change your mind now?!"

Even after such a long time, Li Ping could feel the incomprehension and anger within the separated Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao consciousness.

Mr. Bai, perhaps knowing he was in the wrong, remained silent.

"Say something!"

Only when the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao finally stopped did Mr. Bai slowly respond.

"That is my homeland."

"From birth until now, everyone I've known, everyone I've heard of, and those I love and hate, have all spent their lives there."

"Now it is facing tribulation. I can indeed leave it behind. But what about them?" Mr. Bai asked quietly.

The Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao could not understand Mr. Bai's emotions at all. In its view, ensuring its own survival was the most important thing.

"As long as I am here, and we find another suitable world, we can quickly create another Xuanhuang Realm."

"Even those people you know, I can recreate them." It tried to explain.

Mr. Bai merely smiled lightly and shook his head.

Without further hesitation, he turned and headed back towards the Xuanhuang Realm.

Seeing that things were developing uncontrollably, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao became increasingly anxious.

It kept trying to persuade him.

Mr. Bai simply turned a deaf ear, his decision made.

"I know you haven't treated me badly."

"You always say I'm the reincarnation of that person."

"But I know, I am myself."

"Su Bai. An ordinary mortal." The Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao's memory became somewhat unstable amidst its growing rage.

But Mr. Bai's words, though intermittent, remained extremely clear.

"I don't want to cultivate at all, nor do I want to be an immortal."

"I just want to..."

"Save the people I care about."

"I'm sorry."

"As for what you've given me, the Immortal Body of a Great Heavenly Venerate, and those immortal artifacts..."

"Even this cultivation, I will return it all to you."

Mr. Bai said calmly.

...

Boom!

The memory shattered like a bubble.

Having inherited the power of the Xuanhuang malevolent thought, Li Ping could now empathize with the extreme anger of being deceived and betrayed.

"Die! Die!"

The Xuanhuang malevolent thought's voice began to echo in his mind.

Even Li Ping's aura fluctuated slightly.

And within the formation, the deformed malevolent entity, being suppressed and crushed by the Great Millstone of Heaven and Earth, seemed to sense the change occurring in Li Ping.

It couldn't help but scream, "Do you feel it?! Can you understand me?!"

"The pain of being deceived, and then sealed for thousands of years!"

...

Unexpectedly, its plea was cut short by Li Ping's words.

"I am currently in human form."

"Therefore, the one I can empathize with more is the one you hate so much."

"I think Mr. Bai did the right thing."

"Some things are ultimately beyond your comprehension. Therefore..."

"Rest in peace."

Li Ping's voice gradually turned icy.

The facial features that had vaguely manifested on the Faceless Saint Emperor's face due to the impact of the Xuanhuang malevolent thought's memory disappeared again.

A cold and ruthless aura emanated from the Faceless Saint Emperor.

Without hesitation, he accelerated the operation of the Great Millstone of Heaven and Earth.

Like an indestructible, towering dam, it blocked all the onslaught of the malevolent thought.

Seeing this scene, the three guards within the formation breathed a sigh of relief.

They had genuinely feared that the Saint Emperor would be influenced by the malevolent thought.

Especially Yin Shangren.

He jokingly said to Xu Ke, "Actually, my essence is not much different from the Xuanhuang malevolent thought."

"If he can devour it so easily, then devouring me would be a simple matter."

"It seems I need to stay further away from him in the future."

Xu Ke remained silent.

Watching the figure in the formation that seemed to grow taller and taller, he felt a sense of loss, unsure if handing over the Xuanhuang malevolent thought was the right decision.

The purple-golden vortex spun continuously, and the sound of wind and thunder grew louder.

The Xuanhuang malevolent thought's struggles grew weaker and weaker.

It was only a matter of time before it was completely devoured.

As the power of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao was absorbed and refined, the majestic figure of the Faceless Saint Emperor grew increasingly tall.

It seemed as if it would burst through the sky of the Great Qi small world and reach another realm.

Li Ping's figure appeared on the sky curtain.

All the billions of citizens of Great Qi could now clearly see the Saint Emperor's face.

The fervent hearts of the people reached their peak at this moment.

The condensed fortune instantly broke through the purple barrier and turned into incomparably dazzling, brilliant golden light.

Even if it was only for this moment and would soon revert,

Li Ping felt a resonance and keenly seized this sliver of opportunity.

With a gentle wave of his hand, he scattered a portion of the Xuanhuang malevolent thought's power, converted by the Great Millstone of Heaven and Earth, into the Great Qi small world.

Countless purple-golden dots, like heavenly flowers descending, scattered among the populace.

And from the perspective of the ordinary citizens of Great Qi below, they saw the rumored "Saint Emperor's blessings" from a few days ago.

These purple-golden flowers seemed to possess an innate power to captivate the hearts of people,

Causing the citizens of Great Qi to disregard the Saint Emperor's majesty and reach out to touch them.

And the changes brought about by the purple-golden flowers entering their bodies caused those people to immediately kneel and shout praises for the Saint Emperor's might.

The fortune of Great Qi, which had already reached its peak, was as if catalyzed, undergoing another transformation.

This time, under the unified acclamations of billions of Great Qi citizens, the originally unstable golden fortune finally stabilized completely.

Billions of beings, like a roaring tide.

This caused the three guardians of the formation above Great Qi to be momentarily stunned.

"This is what is meant by 'when one man attains the Dao, even his dependents ascend to heaven,' right?" Yin Shangren couldn't help but sigh.

Xu Ke unconsciously sized up Li Ping's motionless body, and for some reason, saw the figure of Mr. Bai.

"Perhaps I didn't make the wrong decision," Xu Ke thought to himself.

Meanwhile, Yi Shu of the Taiyan Sect narrowed his eyes, seemingly deducing something, his eyes filled with astonishment.

The Celestial Emperor's Jade Scripture, having transformed into its final stage and completely stabilized.

With power shifting from one side to the other, the Xuanhuang malevolent thought finally had no chance of resistance.

"I will wait for you."

"You will end up in the same situation as me."

Before his consciousness completely dissipated, the Xuanhuang malevolent thought cursed venomously for some unknown reason.

Saint Emperor Li Ping remained unmoved, unaffected.

The Great Millstone of Heaven and Earth pressed down heavily.

The power from the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao flowed continuously into his body.

Li Ping felt a sense of resonance, as if an invisible shackle had been broken.

"Longevity Realm?"

"Or perhaps, an alternative Longevity Realm."

He mused thoughtfully.

...

Meanwhile.

In the Dharma Projection Jade space within the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters.

The feedback from the clone's breakthrough abruptly stopped the moment the Saint Emperor reached the Longevity Realm's power.

Therefore, it did not attract the attention of others in the space.

The Saint Emperor's breakthrough was within Li Fan's expectations.

What Li Fan was truly concerned about was the memory from the Xuanhuang malevolent thought.

"Immortal Artifact?"

"And, the Immortal Body of the First Great Heavenly Venerate?"

Li Fan closed his eyes, concealing the astonishment within his eyes.

"Mr. Bai's words, 'I will return it to you,' mean that these things are still within the Xuanhuang Realm?"

Chapter 1239: Source Power Sealing Immortal Disaster

In the 119th life, Li Fan had concocted the rumor of the so-called [True Immortal Remnants]. And using it as bait, he had lured cultivators from the Myriad Immortals Alliance into the small world of the Life and Death Reversal Great Array, exposing [Rebirth Heavenly Venerate] to the world prematurely.

Unexpectedly, the Xuanhuang Realm actually hid a True Immortal Remnant.

And it was no ordinary immortal.

"The Immortal Body of the First Great Heavenly Venerate?"

"Interesting."

This single sentence contained many secrets.

The Great Heavenly Venerate of Xuanhuang did not refer to a specific cultivator, but rather represented a certain status or title.

Li Fan had already learned this in the deepest part of the Immortal Extermination Realm.

"My conjecture back then was correct. As long as one passes the trials of the Immortal Extermination Realm, they should be able to succeed as the new Great Heavenly Venerate of Xuanhuang, and possibly obtain the few immortal artifacts left behind by Mr. Bai."

"Then, where would Mr. Bai have hidden the Immortal Body of the First Great Heavenly Venerate? Would it still be in the Immortal Extermination Realm?"

Li Fan's thoughts raced.

And this First Great Heavenly Venerate was even more intriguing to Li Fan.

The remnant could be called an Immortal Body, so undoubtedly, this Great Heavenly Venerate was at least at the True Immortal cultivation level.

Why did this True Immortal die? And why did he choose to leave his remnants within the Xuanhuang Realm before his death?

Was the birth of the Immortal Extermination Realm related to this True Immortal Great Heavenly Venerate?

Now, the Saint Emperor clone had reached the pinnacle of the Xuanhuang Realm.

Including the natural expansion of the Xuanhuang Realm over the years, the Saint Emperor's strength, compared to Mr. Bai back then, was probably only a hair's breadth short.

With a concrete reference point, Li Fan was now certain that Mr. Bai alone could not have created the illusory and enormous Immortal Extermination Realm.

However, during the era of the Ten Immortal Sects, people were unaware of the existence of the Immortal Extermination Realm.

Therefore, it was certain that even if Mr. Bai did not personally create it, the Immortal Extermination Realm must have had a significant connection to him.

The multiple illusory trials undoubtedly confirmed this point.

"Although Mr. Bai 'betrayed' the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, he did not break his promise. The immortal artifacts and the immortal body were both returned to the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao. Even his cultivation was returned to heaven along with his death during the process of reversing the principles of immortality."

Li Fan mused in his heart but had no intention of actively searching for the Great Heavenly Venerate's Immortal Body.

Although the Great Heavenly Venerate's Immortal Body was considered a supreme treasure, it was of little use to Li Fan at the moment. Even if he could cross the high wall with the protection of the Immortal Body, Li Fan would never leave rashly without knowing anything about the world outside the high wall.

Not to mention, Li Fan's current realm was still far from being able to utilize Immortal Spiritual Energy.

Just how to detonate the immortal artifacts and use their explosive power to cross the high wall without harming himself was beyond Li Fan's knowledge.

"One must proceed step by step. Anyway, as long as it is within the Xuanhuang Realm, or within the range of the Darkest Star Sea, it will eventually be mine."

Li Fan had a clear understanding of his advantages.

"The Saint Emperor clone in this life already has enough capital to contend with the Myriad Immortals Alliance. And with all the current augmentations, his strength has surpassed mine. Let's see how he stirs up trouble."

"This Xuanhuang Realm is like a small pond. Only by thoroughly stirring up the water will those old fellows who have been hiding in every corner of the pond reveal themselves one by one. And I just need to wait patiently here and watch the changes in the world."

"However, the clone I left in the Sun family can be trained to become a future Great Heavenly Venerate."

Li Fan's focus shifted instantaneously.

The clone had now completely taken control of Wu Ninglu's body.

But she remained unaware.

Silently, it influenced her every decision and action.

Most importantly, it encouraged her to sacrifice her own cultivation to nourish the fetus in her womb.

If it were the Wu Ninglu of the past, she would definitely not have done this.

She merely regarded the unborn child as a bargaining chip to control Sun Ang.

But now that Li Fan had intervened, things naturally became different.

Since the clone had sensed the unusual nature of the fetus previously, it had begun its meticulous prenatal education.

Having experienced the stage of cultivation before birth with the celestial bird Little Black in the Immortal Extermination Realm, Li Fan had considerable experience.

With his personal guidance, the fetus gradually compensated for its congenital deficiencies by absorbing the cultivation essence and vital energy from its mother.

Its physique grew stronger day by day, and its consciousness slowly stabilized from its initial faintness.

In a state of chaos, completely ignorant of everything, it was led by Li Fan's clone into one meticulously crafted illusion after another.

"They say saints are born naturally. But in reality, saints can also be forged afterward."

"Speaking of actions rather than intentions, as long as one consistently upholds strict moral standards and codes of conduct, even to the point of death without breaking them..."

"Then, in the eyes of outsiders, this is a true saint."

Cultivating from a state of innate chaos was certainly easier than later education.

What Li Fan was doing now was more like shaping the personality of a living being.

He did not have much experience in this regard and could only explore through practice. If this method proved feasible, then not to mention saints, at the very least, mass-producing gentlemen would be entirely possible.

Li Fan had discovered that although the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao had been deceived once by Mr. Bai, it still trusted people like Mr. Bai more easily.

This was particularly true for the Faceless Saint Emperor in this life.

"The reason for this is likely traceable to Xuanhuang King Xuanyuan Hong, and even the first Great Heavenly Venerate of Xuanhuang," Li Fan mused.

The birth of the fetus within Wu Ninglu, Li Fan had planned to coincide with her devouring of an Earth and Heaven's Soul and advancing to the Harmonious Dao realm.

"If the method is proper, perhaps the power of the Heavenly Dao condensed within the mother's body can be directly transferred to the child through childbirth."

"Perhaps, it might even give birth to the first cultivator in the Xuanhuang Realm to be born Harmonious Dao..."

"Such an anomaly, who would dare say he is not a saint?"

Li Fan thought this way, and couldn't help but feel a sense of anticipation for the fetus's future.

He had even pre-written the script of its destiny.

"Such a prodigy would undoubtedly be regarded as the hope for the Myriad Immortals Alliance's future. And it is precisely such a figure who, when the Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi and the Myriad Immortals Alliance are locked in fierce battle, resolutely chooses to turn against them."

"And firmly claims that he stands on the side of justice."

...

"The scene of the entire Xuanhuang Realm forcing the Law Transmitters to show themselves must be quite interesting."

Vivid scenes flashed through Li Fan's mind.

Without needing to use the Dao-Transformation Stone for deduction, he could roughly predict the subsequent trajectory of this life.

However, this was the most ideal scenario.

Whether it was cultivating an innate saint or the Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi truly developing to a point where it forced the Law Transmitters to appear, it would still take a long time to develop slowly.

Also in the Sun family.

The divine sense hidden within the Boundless Mirror had a much more leisurely time than the clone.

Besides continuously peeking into the secrets of the Heavenly Profound Mirror, most of his energy was spent trying to lure out the Annihilating Wind Disaster from within the mirror.

Since Sun Luyuan had defected to the Saint Emperor, he had the good fortune to borrow over a hundred recently born, robust You Clan members.

They were currently hidden in a secret underground chamber of the Sun family, beside the family's Essence Blood Pool. These You Clan members received even better treatment than their counterparts in the Sacred Dynasty.

They even had two hours of rest time each day.

Of course, this wasn't Li Fan's benevolence, but rather the Boundless Mirror could not withstand overly frequent experiments and needed time to rest.

"As I suspected, this Annihilating Wind Disaster does indeed actively attack [Immortal] level power."

At this moment, the Boundless Mirror, emitting waves of dim light, floated in mid-air.

The mirror surface did not reflect the outside scene, but rather quick flashes of scenes depicting civilizations suffering destruction and calamity.

A sense of vastness and antiquity emanated from the mirror.

The Boundless Mirror, which had just recovered its essence blood, became damaged again.

The invisible black destructive wind was drawn out from the Boundless Mirror.

It flew towards a golden square not far away.

The square was naturally composed of pure Origin Force.

Although not comparable to the Saint Emperor clone's Origin Force essence, it was sufficient to lure out this Annihilating Wind Disaster.

As the destructive wind entered the range covered by the Origin Force, its form instantly changed.

The power that transcended the mortal realm instantly disappeared. The reduction in the purity of the Origin Force led to a drop in energy level.

Having lost its target, the Annihilating Wind Disaster paused for a moment.

It was about to continue spreading outwards.

However, the Origin Force transformed and formed a great formation.

It enclosed and sealed the power of the Annihilating Wind Disaster within.

This great formation was based on the incomplete [Profound Origin Primordial Spirit Great Formation]. Li Fan used the formation to simulate a relatively static space.

There was nothing within the great formation, an absolute void.

It resembled the scene of the end times after all had been destroyed.

The Annihilating Wind Disaster was indeed enticed, its energy no longer surging but slowly subsiding.

The remaining power of the wind disaster within the Boundless Mirror also calmed down.

"Senior's methods are truly divine. With just a few more attempts like this, the hidden dangers within me will be completely eliminated," said Sun Luyuan, the spirit of the Boundless Mirror, overjoyed.

Li Fan ignored him and carefully collected the golden small cubes containing the Annihilating Wind Disaster.

He had already manufactured more than twenty similar small cubes.

Due to differences in technical proficiency, the power of the wind disaster contained within them varied.

But undoubtedly, if the equilibrium of each golden cube were to be broken, a terrifying calamity would erupt.

Sun Luyuan did not pay attention to Li Fan's silence and continued to speak of his own changes.

"Senior, I have a feeling that after completely removing this wind disaster, my control over the Boundless Mirror will reach a new level. At that time, I might be able to sense the location of other fragments of the Boundless Mirror and completely restore this Immortal Artifact."

"Mm," Li Fan replied faintly, his attention still focused on the golden cubes.

Having witnessed Li Fan's methods, and eager to claim credit, Sun Luyuan hesitated for a moment before speaking again. "Senior. When I have completely restored the Immortal Artifact, I might even be able to simultaneously sense the whereabouts of other potential Immortal Artifacts within the Xuanhuang Realm."

Upon hearing Sun Luyuan's words, Li Fan finally turned his head slightly.

"Oh? Are you so sure?"

Sun Luyuan's spirits lifted, and he quickly explained, "Beings like us can generally sense each other. Especially since my Boundless Mirror also possesses the ability to measure the heavens and investigate the earth. If there really are other Immortal Artifacts in the Xuanhuang Realm, then after I recover, the probability of finding them is quite high."

Li Fan smiled. "I think you've been confined for too long and are simply itching to get out and explore, aren't you?"

Sun Luyuan smiled sheepishly. "There's that reason, of course. But my desire to help Senior find immortal artifacts is definitely not false."

Li Fan glanced at him. "Let's focus on completely removing this wind disaster first."

Li Fan's expression was somewhat solemn. "Don't underestimate it just because it seems extremely weakened now. Its root cause has not completely diminished."

"After all, it is a power that surpasses the mortal realm. We cannot be careless."

Sun Luyuan nodded in agreement, feeling the same.

...

Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi.

More than ten days had passed since Li Ping completely devoured the Xuanhuang malevolent thought.

Having gained such immense power, Li Ping needed some time to digest and adapt.

He was enjoying a rare period of rest.

But within the Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi, prosperity had reached unprecedented levels.

Currently, the fortune of the Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi was highly bound to Saint Emperor Li Ping.

Under normal circumstances, after cultivating the Celestial Emperor's Jade Scripture, the growth of the dynasty's fortune would drive the emperor's strength to advance.

But in Great Qi now, it was a rare situation where the Saint Emperor's breakthrough in strength was feeding back into the dynasty's fortune.

And as the people's hearts and the dynasty's fortune further strengthened, it in turn fed back to the Saint Emperor.

Thus, in addition to the strength gained from devouring the Xuanhuang malevolent thought,

Li Ping's Celestial Emperor's Jade Scripture was also approaching transformation shortly after his breakthrough.

However, there were no records in the original scripture for the path ahead.

The path was blocked.

"Anything below the True Immortal realm, similar to the Longevity realm, is the limit for the fortune-based cultivation path."

"After all, relying solely on imperial fortune to break through the shackles and achieve True Immortal..."

"Is too difficult."

"Unless it is a great dynasty that spans across star seas."

Li Ping shook his head slightly, suppressing this thought.

Given the premise of the Darkest Star Sea, even if the Sacred Dynasty of Great Qi unified the Xuanhuang Realm, it would not be enough to support him in breaking through to the True Immortal realm.

"Since this path is blocked, I must find another way."

"The Xuanhuang malevolent thought has been devoured by me. Next, if I want to become stronger..."

"First, the Supreme Treasure Fishing Pond."

"Second..."

The Saint Emperor sat on his throne, and the figures of Ruo Mu, Shi Ban, and other native creations of the Xuanhuang Realm appeared in his mind.

"As part of the Xuanhuang Realm's laws, the Heavenly Dao suffered a great calamity, yet they still survived."

"Heaven granted them these things. Since they are useless to Heaven, they must be taken back by Heaven."

A murderous aura emanated from the Faceless Saint Emperor.

(End of this chapter)
